üîé

Can the drunk or poisoned Acrobat die with one or more drunk or poisoned neighbours?

No. The Acrobat dies only at its turn in the night order. If they are drunk/poisoned at that time, they would not be able to die to their own ability.

Is the Marionette Townsfolk considered poisoned for the sake of the Acrobat?

No, they are sober and healthy. Also, they are an evil Minion, and the Acrobat only cares about neighbouring living good players.

If the Acrobat is sat next to a Minion what happens?

The Acrobat's ability skips over evil and dead players, looking only at its nearest alive good players.

If the Acrobat has a drunk or poisoned neighbour N1 and then is between two sober people N2, do they still die? (for instance, they neighbour a drunk Sailor the first night who becomes sober the second)

The Acrobat dies at their turn in the night order only, so if by then they are between two sober and healthy players, they do not die.

Why does the Acrobat, unlike characters with other triggered abilities (Choirboy / Farmer / Grandmother / Poppy Grower / Ravenkeeper / Sage / Acrobat / Barber / Hatter / Plague Doctor / Sweetheart / Tinker / Scarlet Woman / ...), only act at their spot in the night order?

Because:

  • it is not intended for the source of drunking / poisoning to be figured out by night order
  • the evil team needs a chance to poison them.

Some STs do run some of the other triggered abilities at their spot in the night order and they should clarify how they do it. But triggered abilities, except the Acrobat, can happen right after whatever triggered them, or only slightly delayed until the night time in cases such as:

  • the executed Barber or Hatter
  • the Scarlet Woman, who although would have immediately become the Demon, being formally confirmed as such

What happens when the Alchemist is drunk or poisoned on their first night? / How does the Philosopher picking Alchemist N1 affect the Alchemist?

Their ability is something the Alchemist starts knowing and just as with any start knowing character who is drunk or poisoned they can get wrong info on their first night that is not corrected if they become sober and healthy.

On N1 the ST assigns the Alchemist an out of play Minion ability. But if they are N1 drunk or poisoned then instead of learning their correct ability they are told that they have another ability, typically one that is in play, and the ST will treat them as having that ability. When the Alchemist becomes sober and healthy, they do not change abilities, their actual ability that they had from setup now functions correctly, and the ST treats them as having that ability. Note that the Alchemist is only ever informed of a change of ability when they actually change ability, which is not the case here, so the ST tells them nothing.

Does the Alchemist only change their Minion ability when the current ability enters play?

Yes.

If the Alchemist gains a new ability due to a Hatter, are they informed of the new ability they have, or do they have to figure it out like the Cannibal?

The ST wakes them at night to tell them about their new ability.

Can the good Apprentice have the Alchemist so gain a Minion ability?

Yes.

The Bounty Hunter turning the Alchemist evil ... that is just another Minion ability being used by evil, right?

Yes.

The Alchemist Cerenovus picks a player. What token is that player shown?

Madness due to the Cerenovus or the Alchemist Cerenovus runs the same: the target is still shown the Cerenovus token, as well as the token of the role that they are mad as.

Does the Alchemist ping the Chambermaid when they learn what Minion ability they have?

Yes, and after N1 they might still register to the Chambermaid, depending on the Minion ability gained.

How does the Alchemist Evil Twin work?

The Alchemist ET learns an evil player and their role as their twin. The evil player learns the Alchemist. If the good Alchemist ET is executed, evil wins.

What is announced when the Alchemist Fearmonger has picked a player?

The announcement is the same as for the Fearmonger: "a player has been chosen with the Fearmonger ability‚Äù.

Can the Alchemist get the Legion ability?

No, Legion does not register as a Minion until it is in play.

Is it valid for the Alchemist Goblin's win condition for them to publicly claim to be the Alchemist Goblin rather than the Goblin?

Yes.

Technically the ability requires claiming to be the Goblin in order to win when executed, but it would be harsh to not treat both as valid claims.

Can the Alchemist have the Legion ability?

No, Legion is a Demon not a Minion. Only after the ability is in play can the Legion player register as Minion. Likewise the Alchemist cannot have the Recluse ability.

How does the Alchemist who gains the Marionette ability work? / How does the Marionette who thinks that they are the Alchemist work?

These pairings should be avoided as it is unfun and uninteresting.

In both cases they are effectively the poisoned/drunk Alchemist and are told the wrong ability that has no effect, and the Demon would learn who the Marionette is and would be their neighbour. If it is the Alchemist with the Marionette ability, the Demon would immediately know this as they would not have been shown them as a Minion during Demon info.

How does the Alchemist Mezepheles work? Could it turn an evil player good?

The ability still works as it normally does - the first good player to say the word turns evil.

The Alchemist can say it immediately and turn themselves evil, or they could not say it and not lead anyone else to say it and just play for the good team with the knowledge that there is no extra evil player in the game.

The Alchemist has the Baron ability, but on the second night, they are drunk / poisoned. Can they be told that the Baron has come into play, they now have the Poisoner ability, and for them to choose a player? Can they continue to be asked to choose players when they become sober and healthy?

While drunk or poisoned, they can be told anything. Once they sober up, they must act as their actual ability does.

Does the Drunk who thinks that they are the Alchemist Baron add Outsiders?

No.

Does the Alchemist Godfather change the Outsider count?

Yes, and learns which Outsiders are in play.

Does the Alchemist Baron change the Outsider count?

Yes. Two Townsfolk characters are replaced by Outsiders.

Does the Alchemist with a Minion ability like the Godfather or the Baron change the Outsider count?

Yes, if they started the game with that ability then its setup effect happens.

If they start the game with a Minion ability that has no setup effect and are later switched to having one that does, then the setup effects do not happen mid game.

How is the Alchemist run if all the Minion abilities on the script are in play?

They duplicate an in play ability.

This could happen for instance in a 14 player Lil' Monsta game, which results in four in play Minions - this is why it is better to have 5+ Minions on an Alchemist/Lil‚Äô Monsta scripts to avoid such a scenario.

What happens if the Pit-Hag changes a player into the Alchemist but there is no out of play Minion abilities?

If all Minion abilities are already in play, then the ST gives the Alchemist the ability of an in play Minion. This is true whether an Alchemist is created after all Minion abilities are put into play or an Alchemist has always been around.

Can the Minion the Alchemist has the ability of come into play (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Engineer / ...) ?

Yes, and the Alchemist would then change ability if there is still an out of play Minion ability available.

If there is no out of play Minion ability remaining, the Alchemist could either keep the same ability or change to a different in play ability. It should probably change to signal to the Alchemist that the corresponding Minion has entered play as is usually the case.

If an Alchemist ever changes ability, they should be told by showing the "you are‚Äù token, followed by the Alchemist token and new Minion token.

Can the Alchemist Pit-Hag make a Pit-Hag?

Yes, but then as the Alchemist no longer has an out of play minion ability, they must be given a new out of play Minion play. Unless all Minion abilities are in play, in which case it is ST choice whether to let the Alchemist keep the Pit-Hag ability or switch it.

Does an Alchemist wake up with Minions to decide who babysits Lil' Monsta?

No, the Alchemist is not a Minion.

How does the Alchemist Scarlet Woman work in a Legion game?

When any Legion player dies, the SW becomes Legion.

If the Alchemist has the Vizier ability, do players know that they are the Alchemist?

They are announced as the Vizier. The "everyone knows who you are" refers to the ability they have.

The same applies to Cannibal Nightwatchman, Philosopher King etc.

How does the Alchemist interact with the Marionette ability?

From the experimental how to run: "Marionette: Do not make the Alchemist the Marionette if you can avoid it, it is not fun or interesting. In both cases (the Alchemist who gains the Marionette ability or the Marionette who thinks that they are the Alchemist) the only resolution is to just treat them as a poisoned/drunk Alchemist and tell them the wrong ability and not have it affect anyone. In both cases the Demon would learn who the Marionette is and would be their neighbour. If it is an Alchemist with the Marionette ability, the Demon would immediately know this as they would not have been shown them as a Minion during Demon info."

The Alchemist jinx with the Spy is that the Alchemist cannot get the Spy ability, so if the only out of play Minion is the Spy, does the Alchemist get an in play Minion ability instead?

That is a reasonable solution.

Can the Alchemist Scarlet Woman become the Demon?

Yes.

If the Imp self-kills, does the Alchemist Scarlet Woman become the Imp?

Yes. But, as the Alchemist is not a Minion, a living Minion also becomes the Imp.

If the Alchemist is dead when the Minion she has the ability for is put into play, is she still told she changed ability?

No, because she no longer has the ability that would be giving her that an out of play Minion ability. But if she were to later come back to life, then she would be told she has a new ability, but she will not know if that is because that Minion has entered play while she was dead, or if the ST just gave her a different out of play Minion ability (since that resurrected Alchemist would be a new instance and can get a new ability so long as it is also out of play).

Can the Alchemist Goblin be nominated, claim Goblin, then nominate the Virgin, and win?

Yes.

The Goblin's ability reads "if you publicly claim to be the Goblin when nominated and are executed that day, your team wins." So she does not have to be executed because of her nomination, but if she is executed the same day, her team, the good team, wins.

Could the good Goblin be nominated, claim Goblin, then nominate the Virgin, and win?

No, as the Goblin is a Minion and only Townsfolk can trigger the Virgin.

Could the Alchemist Goblin publicly claiming to be the Goblin trigger their win condition if they are executed for breaking Cerenovus madness?

Yes, if the ST is feeling really generous.

How can the Al-Hadikhia resurrect players?

A dead player who chooses live will come back to life, as long as one of the other picks says die.

For the Al-Hadikhia, do all deaths happen simultaneously (when all choose live) or do they happen in the order chosen?

In the order chosen, like any multi-kill Demon. If a player chooses die they die immediately upon choosing so. If all players live, they each die in the order chosen.

In an Al-Hadikhia game, do other players know who else was chosen?

Yes, they are announced publicly. The ST will announce, "The Al-Hadikhia has chosen X" then wake X for their choice of live or die. Then they do the same for the next two players chosen. All of this is done in player silence. So the first player chosen will not know who has been chosen second or third, and the second player chosen will not know who has been chosen third. But all players do learn. The ST also asks for silence during this time frame, so the only thing players will be hearing during this time (in terms of the game anyway) is the ST making said announcements.

If the Al-Hadikhia is drunk or poisoned, are her picks still woken?

No, she is drunk / poisoned so she cannot affect other players: there is no announcement and no waking of her targets. The Al-Hadikhia will then realise that she was drunk / poisoned or think that she might be the Lunatic.

The Al-Hadikhia includes a dead character with a trigger on death ability (Ravenkeeper / Sage / ...) in their three. All three picks choose live so all die. The dead character was resurrected then died again so should get to use their ability tonight, correct?

Yes.

Players are alive the moment that they choose to live. In this case because all players chose to live, the Al-Hadikhia attacked all the players again so the resurrected player died and got to use their ability again.

If an Al-Hadikhia pick does not die due to protection (Soldier / Innkeeper / Tea Lady / Sailor / Monk / Fool / ...) does this register to the Mathematician?

Yes, as the Al-Had's ability has malfunctioned due to another character's ability.

It does not, however, register for the Fool if they end up dying twice to the Al-Hadikhia in the same night as the Fool ability has worked as intended. So the Fool dying twice would give a 1 to the Mathematician for the Al-Hadikhia ability but not the Fool ability.

If only three players live, one of them being the Al-Hadikhia, and the game moves to the night, does the game end?

Almost certainly. The game ends as soon as an end condition is met, which can occur before a character ability has fully resolved. With just two players left alive the game ends so the game can end in the middle of the Al-Hadikhia's picks, which, as with the other multi-kill Demons, happen in order.

If the Al-Hadikhia chooses the three living players with herself last, she is guaranteed to win as long as she says "live": If any of the two players before her say die, they die immediately and the game is over with only two players left alive, evil wins. If all say "live" then they die in order, so the first player dies leaving just two players left alive, the game is over and evil wins.

If, instead to be safe, the Al-Hadikhia chooses the other two living players and a dead player, then if anyone says die the game is over, and if they all choose live, then they all die and, again, the game is over.

The ST still needs to prompt the Al-Hadikhia for her picks because she could still mess up, by choosing dead players that then resurrect: a dead pick will say live and at least one of other picks will say die so the game continues because there are now still more than two alive.

The Al-Hadikhia could get unlucky and end up in a final three with the Soldier and the unprocced Fool ...

An Al-Hadikhia and three other players are alive. The Al-Hadikhia picks two other players and themselves in the night, in that order. All three pick live, therefore all will die in the order they were picked. After the first two players are killed, there are two players alive before the Demon is scheduled to be killed. Does evil win right at that moment, or does this instance count as a tie, therefore giving good the win?

Evil wins in this scenario: Evil wins when there are two players alive, and unless an ability says otherwise (such as the Mastermind or the Evil Twin), the game immediately ends and abilities do not finish resolving first.

Al-Hadikhia picks A B C:
  • A is alive and picks live,
  • B is dead and picks die,
  • C is alive and picks live. Do A and C die?

No. "After waking the third player and taking their choice, if all three players are alive, all three die." So A and C do not die.

In a final four, if the Barber, the Farmer and the last good/evil player are picked by the Al-Hadikhia and all choose live, does the Barber and the Farmer stuff still happen?

Yes, in the order that they were picked.

The players would die in the order the Al-Had chose them, with any on death abilities handled as they trigger, but the ST will end the game as soon as end game condition is met, such as only two players left alive. So if the choices were the Farmer, the Barber, and another role in that order, the Farmer would die and someone would become the Farmer, then the player who was the Barber would die and the game would end.

If the Barber were first, the Al-Had would be offered the Barber swap, and if they swapped themselves then the rest of the kills would not happen. If they instead swapped the Barber with the Farmer, then the Farmer would not trigger and instead there would be another Barber swap. Theoretically there could be three Barber swaps.

How does the Barista doubled Al-Hadikhia work?

The entirety of the choosing and killing process happens twice: from the Al-Hadikhia choosing three players who decide to live/die to the end of the activation, then back to the start to do it again.

Does the Barista doubled target of the Al-Hadikhia get to choose to live or die twice?

No, it is only that player's ability that is doubled, not the Al-Hadikhia‚Äôs.

Why is the Courtier a bad idea in an Al-Hadikhia script?

On D2 everyone will know the Al-Hadikhia is in play. At that point the Courtier will drunk the Al-Had, which is completely unbluffable by the evil team. Thus the Courtier will always be confirmed and get to wipe out the Al-Hadikhia for three nights.

What happens when the Exorcist picks the Al-Hadikhia?

The Al-Hadikhia does not get to pick and there are no announcements. This would look no different to the Al-Hadikhia being drunked or poisoned, so the town would be unsure of the cause.

If the only Al-Hadikhia pick who chooses death is the unspent Fool, who dies?

The Fool initially survives due to her ability, then as all three are alive, all die in the order that they were picked. As this would now be the Fool's second death, she is killed outright. This all assumes no other sources of protection.

Arguably the unspent Fool should always say no to dying...

Does the Gambler know if they died to their own ability if they are resurrected the same night by the Al-Hadikhia?

The Gambler never knows whether they have died to their own ability. So, they could gamble incorrectly and die, then be chosen by the Al-Hadikhia and choose live and therefore be resurrected and would not know whether they gambled correctly or not as the net effect is the same.

If one of the Al-Hadikhia's targets is the unpicked Goon, what happens?

The Al-Hadikhia is drunked immediately, so there are no announcements or waking of any of the targets who all live.

If the evil Goon is resurrected by the Al-Hadikhia, are they still evil?

Yes. Resurrection does not change alignment.

What happens if the grandchild and the Grandmother are both in the same Al-Hadikhia selection?

If the grandchild dies to the Al-Hadikhia, the Grandmother dies too, but they can then be resurrected in the same night and therefore not know if their ability worked or not.

If the grandchild is the first Al-Hadikhia pick and chooses to die, also killing the Grandmother, and the Grandmother is the second pick and chooses to live so coming back to life, they should probably be given the same grandchild, as a new grandchild would give them too much confirmation.

The Al-Hadikhia picks the Innkeeper and the two Innkeeper targets. If all choose live, do all die, or just the Innkeeper? If all three die at the same time, does the Innkeeper protection kick in?

The Al-Had visits three players in an order over the night phase, offering them the choice to live or die. Any player picking die, dies instantly. Once all three are visited, a check is performed: are all three players alive? If they are all alive then, according to the current ruling, they are killed in the order that the Al-Had picked, and not simultaneously as some argue should be the case.

So in this example if the Innkeeper was picked first, all three would die. If the Innkeeper was not the first choice, then the protected player(s) chosen beforehand would stay alive.

Could the Al-Hadikhia be drunked if they are picked by the Innkeeper or the Sailor?

Yes, but don't.

Without other reasons for the Al-Hadikhia to be blocked it is likely that town will narrow the Demon candidates down to the Innkeeper / Sailor pick(s) ...

If the Klutz / Moonchild chooses death when woken for the Al-Hadikhia, when do they make their pick?

At the start of the next day.

Although the player might choose death on being woken for their Al-Hadikhia choice, she does not actually know if she died until it is announced in the morning as she could be protected by another character, so her pick happens publicly in the morning.

If the dead Klutz / Moonchild is picked by the Al-Hadikhia and chooses live but then dies because all picks were alive, does their ability trigger?

No.

Both the Moonchild and Klutz pick when they learn that they have died, but as nothing is ever announced by the ST when a player is resurrected and killed in the same night, they are never prompted to use their ability, even if they surmise that they must have been alive at some point.

Does the Demon learn who the Lunatic Al-Hadikhia chose?

Yes. If the actual Demon is not the Al-Hadikhia then the Lunatic will know straight away who they really are.

What is the Al-Hadikhia jinx with the Mastermind?

This is a hate jinx: only one of these characters can be in play. Additionally, evil players start knowing which player and character it is.

They are hate jinxed because a Mastermind day is pointless when the Demon announces its presence every night; everyone will know when they get the Demon and the Mastermind cannot really accomplish anything. It would go something like:

  1. the Al-Had is executed,
  2. there are no announcements the following night
  3. everyone realises the Demon must be dead,
  4. everyone realises that it must be the player that was just executed,
  5. everyone realises it must be a Mastermind day,
  6. the MM feels completely useless.

How does the Al-Hadikhia targeting the Mayor work?

The Mayor can bounce an Al-Hadikhia kill from themselves to another player if they choose to die. If all three picks are then still alive so all three must die, the Mayor can again bounce the kill.

As an extreme example:

  1. the Mayor and players A and B are chosen by the Al-Hadikhia and announced to town,
  2. only the Mayor says die and their kill bounces to C, who dies,
  3. all three picks are alive so all should die, and the Mayor bounces again to D,
  4. so players A, B, C and D die in the night despite only the Mayor, A and B being announced as Al-Hadikhia targets.

If the ST were do this though it would all but hard-confirm the Mayor and the Al-Hadikhia cannot easily stop them surviving to final three, but it is a fun interaction!

Does the Monk stop a player from being chosen by the Al-Hadikhia?

No, they are still picked and must make a choice.

How does the Pit-Hag interact with the Al-Hadikhia?

If the Pit-Hag creates a new Demon, and one of the two is the Al-Hadikhia who is not immediately killed before they awake, then the Al-Hadikhia can be woken and their choices taken, announced and processed, but the ST can choose to kill or protect anyone throughout the process using the Pit-Hag ability.

It is generally a good idea to kill the Al-Hadikhia if they or a second Demon in an Al-Hadikhia game are created by the Pit-Hag as otherwise they can resurrect the other Demon relatively easily and have two living evil Demons.

If the Pit-Hag turns the Demon into the Al-Hadikhia, deaths are arbitrary, but should the ST wake the Al-Hadikhia and her targets?

Deaths are arbitrary until the end of the night giving the ST a lot of freedom since Demons wake later than the Pit-Hag, but if the Al-Hadikhia is alive, sober and healthy then the waking up and announcing stuff is not optional: it must happen.

This potentially already informs good players that the Demon has changed, so the ST might choose not to interfere with anything and ignore the option for arbitrary deaths.

If the Poppy Grower dies in an Al-Hadikhia game, when should the evil team learn each other?

If the PG is killed by the Al-Hadikhia, the evil team learn each other immediately. Generally, if this is not going to affect the other Al-Hadikhia choices, then it is safe to wait until after the other choices to tell the evil players, but if a Minion or, worryingly, two, have been picked by the Al-Hadikhia along with the Poppy Grower, then the ST should tell them before waking them for their Al-Hadikhia choice as it will affect their decision.

If the Al-Hadikhia dies and the Scarlet Woman becomes a new Al-Hadikhia, could the new Al-Had resurrect the old Al-Had with their ability?

Yes, then the ex-SW would become the SW again (hence the Al-Had and SW jinx to prevent two alive demons).

What happens when the Al-Hadikhia targets the player favoured by the Storm Catcher?

The Storm Caught player can be picked by the Al-Hadikhia but cannot die. This can be a way to force a good player who does not want to die to do so, because it reduces the field to the Storm Caught player and two characters who do not want to die, one of whom is going to have to choose to do so or both of them will instead.

When does the Sweetheart drunk a player if they are killed by the Al-Hadikhia?

The Sweetheart drunks someone as soon as they die. So they could drunk a character that dies later within the Al-Hadikhia choices or even the Al-Hadikhia herself, immediately ending har activation at that moment but this is a probably a bad idea as it confirms the Sweetheart as good as well as wiping out the Demon ability.

What happens when the Tinker is one of the Al-Hadikhia‚Äôs picks?

The Tinker can choose to live for their Al-Hadikhia choice, then die before the other players have chosen to live or die, ensuring that one of the three is dead and preventing an "all three die" situation.

The ST probably would not do this because:

  • either the Tinker will generally be happy to say die
  • or it would be harsh on the Al-Hadikhia who was about to get a rare triple kill.

What happens if the Widow is resurrected by the Al-Hadikhia?

They immediately wake to see the Grimoire and choose a player to be poisoned. This does not have to happen in between the Al-Hadikhia kills, but should if their choice of poison could affect what happens when the other players selected by the Al-Hadikhia that night make their choices. A good player should also be told that the Widow is in play.

What should the ST respond if the Amnesiac says "I would like to claim Amnesiac and start a cult" when their ability has nothing to do with that? Just say no? Let the cult run? Something else?

ST choice.

Does the Amnesiac's ability act as soon as it can, or after they discover their ability?

Their ability is always working. Technically they could have an ability that does not do anything unless or until the Amne guesses their ability fully but that is unlikely to be fun.

How does the Apprentice work?

She will get the ability of a Townsfolk (if good) or a Minion (if evil).

Everyone will know that the player is a Traveller and that they are the Apprentice, but will not know her alignment or what ability she has, otherwise an evil Apprentice would just get instantly exiled.

Does the Fool die if targeted by the Assassin?

Yes. The Fool ability counts as something that would prevent them from dying, so the Assassin ignores it and actually kills them.

Can the Assassin kill the Lleech?

Yes.

Does the Lycanthrope stop an Assassin kill?

No. The Assassin can still kill if the Lycanthrope hits a good player.

Does the Assassin trump the Mayor?

Yes, the Mayor just dies. There can be no bounce, either to die instead of the Mayor or in addition to the Mayor.

Can the Assassin kill the storm caught Townsfolk?

No. The Storm Catcher's ability and the Assassin ability are at odds with one another and while fabled characters do not inherently trump other characters, it is the intention that the Storm Catcher does trump the Assassin.

If the Assassin picks the alive Zombuul, does the game end?

Yes.

In an Atheist game the ST can break the rules but in the instance of the Lunatic Kazali, can their picks be told that they are now Minions, while keeping their alignment as good?

Yes.

The only real restriction in an Atheist games is no evil players at setup. Arguably it is against the spirit of the Atheist to introduce Minions and Demons after setup, regardless of if they are good or not. But ultimately what is acceptable in an Atheist game is up to the ST and their group.

Can the Devil's Advocate protect the ST if there is an Atheist in the game?

ST choice.

RAW the ST is not a player so is never a valid target for abilities, but in an Atheist game the ST is free to break any rule so can allow it. However, as the Atheist only requires the ST's execution not their death, preventing them from dying would not accomplish anything.

Does the Atheist prevent new evil characters from being created after the game has begun?

No, in an Atheist game the ST can break all rules and turn people evil. However, this is usually not fun for the players and not advised; keep all players good and give fake information that they need to "solve" as intended.

Can puzzledrunking the Atheist mean evil roles can be included in the game?

No.

The Atheist has a setup ability, the Puzzlemaster does not, so no one is puzzledrunk until after the tokens go out.

The ST can make the Atheist the Drunk or the Marionette, otherwise when the Atheist is in the bag there must be no evil characters.

If the Philosopher chooses the Atheist in a game that started with the Mastermind, and the ST then dies, could the ST "break the rules" making themself be considered the Demon?

If the ST allowed the Philo-Atheist ability to remain in play, the ST can do whatever they want.

In an Atheist game the Alchemist has the Pit-Hag ability. If the Alchemist makes good a Demon that the town then executes, does the good team win or must the ST be executed?

With the Atheist the ST can decide if the good team wins.

Who wins if the Atheist was drunk when the ST was executed?

If the Atheist was drunk and there is no Demon in play then good would already have won. If there is a demon in play then evil would win.

Although, if there is no evil team usually the ST will break the rules to keep the Atheist sober and not end the game by them being drunk.

Can there be an Atheist game without anyone being shown the Atheist token?

Atheist "can" questions are almost certainly answerable with a "yes." Whether the ST should or not is debatable. So technically the ST can break the rules to do that, but probably should not.

Does the Engineer in an Atheist game create new evils or just not work?

The Engineer can only change the characters of existing Demons and Minions (without breaking the rules). In an Atheist game, the ST is reasonably likely to pretend that it has been effective, though, by changing what Demon/Minion abilities the town is hallucinating.

Does a nominated ST get a defence? In a non Atheist game (with it on the script of course) could the ST use game state information in their defence? (e.g. they think claiming the nominating player is evil helps balance)

If they want one, sure. They could say something funny like "ok‚Äù or "nooooo pleeeeaaaase I‚Äôm innoceeeeent‚Äù They would have to do that every time they were nominated to not give anything away though, probably too hard to balance and gives away too much info. "Go ahead, lose the game" is also an option.

Can the Philosopher choose Atheist?

Yes. Evil players are not removed from the game as that part of Atheist's ability is a setup ability, so it has no effect if entering play mid game. Good can now win the game be executing the ST. However, the ST can now do whatever they want, which typically will also include them uncreating the Atheist.

If Atheist is not on the script, can the Storyteller be executed?

No. Executing the ST is only allowed when the Atheist is on the script, otherwise even nominating the ST is not allowed.

Is it legal to have the Balloonist in play when the Kazali turns all the Outsiders into Minions?

Yes, the Kazali's [setup ability] means the setup is legal whatever the Outsider count.

The Balloonist saw the Minion that the Imp starpassed to. Do they later see the same Minion again as the Demon?

They can, or they can be shown the dead Imp.

Is it legal to have a Balloonist in a Legion game with no Outsiders?

Yes, but since the Balloonist will only receive three pings, they will likely learn that they are in a Legion game.

Can a single Legion player be shown to the Balloonist twice, once as a Minion and once as a Demon?

Yes.

Could a Minion holding Lil' Monsta be shown twice to the Balloonist - once as a Minion and once as a Demon?

Yes.

What happens when the Philosopher chooses Balloonist in a zero Outsider game?

They gain the ability. They do not add an Outsider though, and will end up only learning three names, unless an Outsider is introduced (Pit-Hag) before N4. Should an Outsider be created after N4, it would be too late; once they have learned one of every in play character type, they lose their ability.

After a Minion is chosen by the Preacher, can they still be seen as such by the Balloonist?

Yes, a preached Minion is still a Minion.

Could the Balloonist be shown the Recluse multiple times?

Yes. The Recluse can register three times to the Balloonist, as an Outsider, a Minion and the Demon.

If the Balloonist sees the Snake Charmer as a Townsfolk, could they see the same player again after they successfully charm the Demon?

Yes.

Could the Balloonist be shown the Spy multiple times?

Yes. The Spy can register three times to the Balloonist, as a Townsfolk, an Outsider and a Minion.

If the Spy ever holds Lil' Monsta then they could register as the Demon as well and be shown up to four times! But then as this would confirm them to be the Spy, potentially holding Lil' Monsta, this might not be a fun thing to do.

Can the Balloonist learn the name of a Traveller?

No, unless they are holding Lil' Monsta or they are an Apprentice Spy.

How does drunking and poisoning work with the Balloonist? e.g. the Balloonist is poisoned N1, the ST points at a Minion and, in the Grimoire, puts the Townsfolk reminder next to the Minion. If the Balloonist is no longer droisoned the next night, is the Townsfolk reminder still valid or does the Minion now count as a Minion? i.e. does the ST choose something to "consume" at the time they point to a player or do they reevaluate each night?

Once the Townsfolk reminder token is placed it is used, so the ST could show the same Minion again as a Minion if they wanted, but they could not show the sober Balloonist a Townsfolk anymore.

In a base zero Outsider game, with both the Balloonist and the Vigormortis in play, is one a legal amount of Outsiders? Or should it be net zero Outsiders? Is this ruling ST dependent?

ST choice. One Outsider is legal. Most players prefer the net total method as the most intuitive choice.

What happens if the Balloonist dies and is resurrected (Professor / Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia / ...) ?

They are a fresh incarnation of the Balloonist so their reminder tokens are cleared and they would restart their info from scratch.

Can the Balloonist get pings on dead players?

Yes.

If the dead Damsel gets swapped in to a living player from the Barber, is it random like it is for the Pit-Hag?

No.

Can the Barber change the good twin, if the Demon swaps one of the twins?

If the Demon chooses to Barber swap the good twin player, then they are still the good twin, and the Evil Twin gets updated about what character they are now. If the Demon chooses to Barber swap the Evil Twin, then there will be a new ET pair who will get woken that night to learn each other.

If a Farmer is Barber swapped with a Farmer does the ST have to tell the Farmers?

No, the rules say players always learn if their character changes and their character did not change.

The Barber dies in a Legion game. The ST wakes one Legion and they swap themselves with another Legion. Since neither player changed roles, does the ST tell the other Legion?

The Demon cannot use the Barber to swap with a second Demon.

Can the former Scarlet Woman who is now the Demon, use the Barber to swap the previous Demon with a living player?

No, the Barber's ability explicitly disallows choosing another Demon.

Is the Soldier safe when the Demon uses the Barber swap on them?

No.

The Barber is killed. Can alignment be changed, say by the Demon swapping herself?

Barber swaps do not change alignment, only character.

Could the Barber be swapped with a living player after they die and then the new Barber could get killed to trigger the swap again, repeatedly?

Yes.

Does the Barber interrupt multi-kill Demons (Al-Hadikhia / Po / Shabaloth)?

Yes. If the Barber is killed by the Demon, the Demon is woken and offered the swap. If the Demon swaps herself then the rest of her picks are skipped: no one dies / wakes to choose life or death.

Does Barber swapping two players make new instances of these characters, refreshing their abilities?

Yes.

Why is "not another demon" clarified on the Barber's ability?

If there is a dead Fang Gu, and that clause did not exist, a living Fang Gu could swap the dead Fang Gu with a Minion and get two living evil Fang Gus. This could also happen with the Pit-Hag creating multiple demons.

Can the current Demon kill the Barber and swap a dead Demon with a Minion, leading to two alive demons? Can the ST kill on of them and have kills be arbitrary?

Demons cannot choose other Demons with the Barber ability (it says so under the Barber's ability). The ST also cannot arbitrarily kill anyone with the Barber ability, only with the Pit-Hag ability when a new Demon is created.

Can a dead Demon (game continues due to the Evil Twin) revive the Demon with a Barber swap?

Yes. But only themselves, since it says "not another Demon" The extra Barber rule is to prevent two alive Demons.

If the Barber dies and no Demons are alive, who decides the swap? Can a dead Demon move the demonhood back to a living player?

If no Demons are alive, then a dead Demon gets the swap. They cannot swap another dead Demon into a living player, but they can swap their own demon ability back into play.

If the Barber dies in a game with no living Demons (Evil Twin in play, evil Demon executed) would the dead Demon still get to make the swap?

Yes, "the Demon" may be a dead Demon if there are no alive Demons.

Is the Barber able to swap a Traveller and a Townsfolk?

The ST can allow it but generally no.

If the Barista makes the Amnesiac act twice, do they get to guess their ability twice?

That would make sense, plus their Amne-ability functions twice.

How does the Barista doubled Barber work?

The Demon is woken to make a swap, goes to sleep, then immediately wakes again to make a second swap. If the Demon changes inbetween swaps, then it is the new Demon making the second swap.

How does the Barista doubled Boomdandy work?

If the Boomdandy is Barista-doubled on a day they are not executed, nothing happens.

On a day they are executed, they try to kill N (number of total players) minus 3, then try to kill N minus 3 players again (these do not need to be the same players), then when the pointing minute is complete, the player with the most pointing at them dies twice (if applicable). Note this means that the Barista doubled Boomdandy can kill the unused Fool before the pointing starts or the living Zombuul/unused Fool can be killed twice to end the game with the pointing.

If the Cannibal eats an evil player and then somehow becomes healthy (Barista / Amnesiac / ...), do they gain any ability?

They gain the ability. A Barista'd Cannibal who eats the Spy is interesting. A Barista'd Cannibal who eats the Widow is completely hilarious. The ST should probably avoid giving a Barista bonus to the Cannibal.

What does a Barista doubled Damsel do?

If the Damsel guess has already been used, then the Minions may attempt one more guess today. If the guess has not already been used, then they may attempt two guesses today.

However, as it is the Damsel that is told about the Barista doubling, the Minions will be unaware of the extra guess unless the Damsel announced it.

What does a Barista 1 Drunk / Marionette do?

ST choice:

  • as well as being sober and healthy, they would have to get true information if they think they are an info role,
  • they still should get arbirtary info.

The ST should clarify how they run this interaction when the Barista is in town and the Drunk or the Marionette are on the script.

What effect does Barista doubling the Fearmonger have?

The Fearmonger can pick two players that night and nominating and executing either of them the following day will end the game.

This could potentially result in two announcements of the Fearmonger selecting new players, so the Fearmonger will want to be careful in this situation not to reveal the Barista is evil and the Fearmonger has two selections that night.

How does the Barista doubled Fool work?

If they still have their ability, then they can die three times today, otherwise they can die twice.

What does a Barista 1 Fortune Teller learn if she chooses her Red Herring?

She would ignore their Red Herring. Also she would not see the Recluse as the Demon.

How does the Barista doubled Huntsman work?

If they have yet to guess then they can choose two players in one night, otherwise they can be woken to make another guess.

What effect does the Barista have on the King?

The Barista only has an effect when the dead outnumber the living. Once this is the case, Barista 1 gives the King true info and Barista doubling gives the King two character tokens to see.

How does the Barista doubled Lleech work?

If the Lleech is chosen on N1 then they choose two players, both of whom are poisoned from now on, and both must die in order for the Lleech to die. If the Lleech is chosen after N1 then they kill twice.

How does the Barista doubled Marionette work?

The Marionette would be deceived that they have two uses of the ability that they think they have. If they are Barista doubled N1 then technically the Demon should be told twice about them.

What does Barista doubling the Mezepheles do?

If doubled on the first night, the Mez learns two words and the first good player to say both turns evil.

On any other night, like with any once per game ability that is Barista doubled:

  • if they have already used their ability, that is turned someone evil, they can turn another player turned today by getting them to say the word;
  • if they have not already used it, then they can get two people to turn today.

How does the Barista doubled Nightwatchman work?

Two players can be picked and each is shown the Nightwatchman token. Each player is told once, not twice.

What does a Barista 1 Savant learn?

Two true statements.

How does the Barista work twice on the Savant?

The Savant prompts the ST twice, and receives two sets of statements; one true and one false each. They do not receive two true statements and then two false.

Does the Barista doubled Philosopher get to pick two abilities that night?

Yes, but the Barista doubled Philosopher is completely broken so best not to do it.

How does the Barista doubled Philosopher work?

If the Philo has yet to pick an ability, they gain two abilities, and potentially drunk two characters. If they have, they can gain an additional ability on top of their current one.

The ability/abilities gained are not doubled.

Does the Barista doubled Pit-Hag who uses their first pick to turn themselves into something else still get a second use of the Pit-Hag ability?

No, as they no longer have the Pit-Hag ability.

Does the Barista doubled Pit-Hag who with her last pick turns herself into a role that acts after the Pit-Hag, get to use their new role twice too?

Yes.

Does the Barista doubled Snake Charmer who hits the Demon get to make two kills as the Demon?

Yes.

The Witch is Barista doubled, and curses two players. If the Barista is exiled or travels away, are both of those players still cursed?

Yes, the doubling is a one time effect that cannot be retroactively undone.

Can the Barista let the Demon kill twice?

Yes.

Does Barista 1 have an effect on the Demon?

Only if they would have otherwise been poisoned or drunk.

When a once-per-use character is Barista doubled, can they choose to use their ability once to use the extra use and keep their original use? e.g. Slayer, Artist, Damsel (!?), ...

No.

With Barista, can the ST choose that a character is sober and healthy, if they were already sober and healthy?

Yes. That player would then be informed of the Barista choice so they would know for a fact they are sober and healthy, which is still pretty helpful, but not for start knowing roles where being sober and healthly now does not help them at all.

Do roles that receive info only on N1 benefit from being selected by the Barista on later nights?

Not a Barista 1 (sober + healthy + true), but a Barista 2 (ability works twice) could give them info again as their first night ability will work on a night other than the first.

Does a living Beggar without a vote still count for purposes of majority voting?

Yes.

Can the Beggar learn the Recluse as evil?

Yes.

How does the interaction between Judge and Bishop work? If the ST does not nominate a Bishop-opposed player first and the Judge ends it, then the day ends without the ST nominating an opposed player.

The Judge's ability wins out in that case. The day just ends without the ST nominating an opposing player. The players can account for the fact that the Judge may have interrupted a day's worth of alignment information.

Can the ST call for the exile of a Traveller when the Bishop is in play?

No.

If the Bone Collector picks the Marionette or the Drunk, what happens?

They get another day/night of the ability that they think they have.

Does the ST inform a player that the they have been chosen by the Bone Collector?

No. But they can probably infer this when their ability works again.

Does the Bone Collector give the Slayer another use of their ability?

Yes.

Can the Bone collector ability only be used once or every night?

It is a once per game ability.

The Artist is dead. The Bone Collector targets the Artist at night. The Pukka poisons the Bone Collector later that same night. The Artist tries to use their power the next day. Does it work?

No; the BC is the only reason the Artist would be able to use their ability while dead and they are poisoned, so their ability is not functioning.

What happens when the Klutz dies to the Boomdandy?

At whatever point the Klutz is declared dead, the Klutz should interject to choose an alive (at that point) player.

What happens when the Moonchild dies to the Boomdandy?

Like the Klutz, when the Moonchild is declared dead, they should interject to choose an alive (at that point) player. Unlike the Klutz though it is less critical for the game as to what they do.

Can the Apprentice have the Boomdandy ability?

The Apprentice should not be given the Boomdandy ability, as it does not do anything on exile.

Can the Butcher still nominate after the Boomdandy is executed?

Yes. This is usually the only way the good team can save themselves from an accidental tie in the Boomdandy pointing. However, this requires there to have been some other reason for more than three players to be alive after the Boomdandy kills as ordinarily if there was a Butcher and two others left alive, the game would end with an evil win.

Can the Deviant die when the Boomdandy explodes?

Yes as it is not an exile.

Can the Gangster still kill in the minute after the Boomdandy explodes?

Yes. However, this requires there to have been some other reason for more than three players to be alive after the Boomdandy kills as ordinarily if there was a Gangster and two others left alive, the game would end with an evil win.

Is the Doomsayer still active in the minute after the Boomdandy explodes?

The only time a player can Doomsay during the Boomdandy minute is if there are more than three players left alive for whatever reason as in all other cases there will only be three players living and therefore the Doomsayer has no ability.

Can the sober Sailor still die in the Boomdandy's explosion?

No, they would have to remain alive in the final three.

If the Slayer survives the Boomdandy's explosion, can she still take her shot?

Yes, she may act during the minute after the Boomdandy's kills are announced. As this is extraordinarily powerful in this context, the unused Slayer should probably die to the Boomdandy.

Could the Acrobat that survives when the Boomdandy explode die if any of their surviving neighbours is drunk or poisoned?

No, the Acrobat ability is only checked at night, so they would not die until that night.

Can the Demon die when the Boomdandy explodes and have their Scarlet Woman become the new Demon?

Yes, if the Boomdandy deaths happen in the right order, the SW can become the Demon, as long as the Demon dies with more than four alive.

After the Boomdandy explodes resulting in only three players left alive, can a player who is mad (Mutant / Cerenovus target / Harpy target / ...) still be executed for breaking madness?

Yes. This will almost certainly end the game as it will likely leave only two living players (the Boomdandy‚Äôs resulting three minus the mad player).

What happens when the Sweetheart dies when the Boomdandy explodes?

The Sweetheart makes someone drunk when they die. Usually this should be a player that is also dying to the Boomdandy ability. They could drunk the Boomdandy to immediately stop the killing and move the game straight to night without any pointing, but this is a terrible idea as it is using an Outsider to help the good team immensely, and confirming both a good and evil player in the process.

If the Tinker survives the Boomdandy, could they immediately die afterwards, ending the game with an evil win?

Yes, but don't.

Does the Boomdandy still trigger if they are executed but do not die (Devil's Advocate protection)?

Yes. As this hard-confirms them as the Boomdandy, it is a good idea for the Boomdandy to die in their explosion.

After the Boomdandy triggers, can the Cult Leader call for a cult?

Yes, but don't allow it.

RAW the Cult Leader can call for a cult in the one minute time if they are still alive and did not call for a cult earlier in the day, but this should be disallowed as it is either going to go over the time limit or take up a disproportionate amount of the time limit which is intended for discussion.

Can the unspent Fool die to the Boomdandy?

The Fool cannot be killed twice by the Boomdandy's boom, so if their ability is unused they will survive, but if they are "killed" once by the boom and then killed again by the pointing, they would die.

Can the Gossip still gossip if they have not already done so that day, after the Boomdandy triggers?

Yes, but this is probably pointless and not advised.

Can the Mayor win the game after the Boomdandy is triggered and no one dies after the pointing?

No. Even though there are three players left alive at the end of the day, the Boomdandy's execution earlier that day means that the Mayor ability cannot trigger.

If the Boomdandy is executed, would the in play Minstrel immediately drunk them, preventing their exploding?

Yes.

Does the protection / poisoning / drunking immediately end when the Boomdandy's explosion kills any sources of such (Innkeeper / Tea Lady / Philosopher / ...)?

Yes. The targets of such abilities immediately lose their protection / become healthy / sober.

Can the Pixie still gain their ability for the one minute after the Boomdandy explodes, killing their marked player?

Yes.

After the Boomdandy is triggered can the Artist still ask the ST their question, in the post-execution minute?

Yes, but this does not extend the time limit.

After the Boomdandy is triggered can the Fisherman still get their advice within the post-execution minute?

Yes, but this does not extend the time limit.

After the Boomdandy is triggered can the Savant still get their info within the post-execution minute?

Yes, but this does not extend the time limit.

What if there is a tie in a Boomdandy vote?

No one dies, the game goes to night, and the Demon presumably kills.

If the Boomdandy explodes in a Lleech game, the host must remain but does the Lleech need to remain alive as well?

The Lleech host must be alive and the Lleech too since they can only die with their host.

Can the Pacifist block deaths caused by the Boomdandy being executed?

No. The Pacifist saves good players specifically from execution, and Boomdandy deaths are not due to execution.

If the Saint is killed when the Boomdandy explodes, is that an evil win?

No. The Saint needs to die to execution for evil to win, and Boomdandy deaths are not due to execution.

Is a player protected by the Devil's Advocate safe from dying when the Boomdandy explodes?

No. The DA protects players from execution, and Boomdandy deaths are not due to execution.

If the Goblin player publically claims Goblin and dies when the Boomdandy explodes, is that an evil win?

No. The Goblin needs to be executed, and Boomdandy deaths are not due to execution.

If the Boomdandy explodes in a Leviathan game, do the deaths count towards the Leviathan's execution count?

No, as Boomdandy deaths are not due to execution.

If the Boomdandy explodes, is it okay to kill the Demon and have the game continue into a Mastermind day?

No that would be an evil loss. In order to trigger a Mastermind day the Demon must be executed, and Boomdandy deaths are not due to execution.

Can the Demon die when the Boomdandy goes off and the Scarlet Woman is in play?

Yes, that is legal, as long as there are five players alive when the Demon dies. The SW will reason that they are now the Demon.

If the Boomdandy is executed on final three, does the Boomdandy's ability still trigger and all players point to either of the last two players alive?

No. Two players alive is the evil team's win condition, so the game ends and evil wins.

Who should the ST kill when the Boomdandy triggers?

It is going to be very specific to the exact characters in play and alive. Some general guidelines and ideas:

  • In most cases, leave the Demon alive in the final three, otherwise the game ends in good‚Äôs favour using a Minion ability.
  • The Demon can be killed if there is an Evil Twin pair both still alive, leaving the choice for town to choose between the two twins with a non-Demon third player.
  • The final three cannot be the twins and the Demon as that is an automatic evil win.
  • It is a bad idea to leave hard-confirmed characters alive in final three. A final three that includes the proc'd Virgin and the Professor who resurrected a dead player would be unfair on evil who managed to get their Boomdandy executed.
  • If the Klutz killed by the Boomdandy chose a player between executions, the Klutz-picked player can be left alive to cast suspicion on the Klutz claim.
  • There is no mechanical problem to leave only evil left alive in final three as the Boomdandy kill does not require a nomination, just the pointing, but this can be very hard on good to have to work out exactly which of the evil players is actually the Demon.
  • There are some abilities that can prevent the Boomdandy coming down to a final three and instead having four or even five left alive. While this can be interesting, it should be used sparingly, as it soft-confirms a few players (the player claiming Sailor or Fool is almost certainly good / the Tea Lady and their neighbours / ... ).

Does the Drunk or the Marionette that sees the Bounty Hunter token turn a Townsfolk evil?

No. The ST must decide to make the Bounty Hunter the Drunk or the Marionette before a Townsfolk is woken and told that they are evil as a result of the Bounty Hunter ability.

If the Bounty Hunter sees the Fool do they need to die twice for the BH to learn another player?

Yes.

Is a Townsfolk still turned evil on N1 if the Bounty Hunter is drunked (Courtier / Sailor / ...) or poisoned (Lleech / ...)?

No, as this is a setup ability so will have happened before the tokens are sent out.

If the Lleech chooses the Bounty Hunter turned Townsfolk, are they still turned evil?

Yes, this is a [setup] ability and has already occurred.

Does the Cannibal gaining the Bounty Hunter ability see the same evil player the BH saw?

They do not have to.

How does a Barista 2 Bounty Hunter work?

They could learn two evil players in one night. They would learn another player when either of those two players died. This means the Bounty Hunter has two instances of their ability from that point on - when either ‚Äòclient‚Äô dies, they learn a new name. It is usually a good idea to show them the same player after both "client A" and "client B" die, to restore the Bounty Hunter to knowing only a single player at a time from then on.

Can the Bounty Hunter learn the currently evil Cult Leader?

The Bounty Hunter can learn any evil player, so yes, and the BH will only learn a new player when the Cult Leader dies regardless of any subsequent alignment change.

The BH would not be able to learn the CL on N1 as they can only change alignment at the end of the night, after the BH wakes, unless the BH themselves turned the CL at setup.

Can the Spy register as a good Townsfolk in order to be turned evil by the Bounty Hunter?

Yes, but this is not recommended.

Does the Bounty Hunter who learns the Zombuul still learn a different player after the Zombuul 'dies' for the first time?

Yes.

If the Bounty Hunter‚Äôs evil Townsfolk is turned into an Outsider, are they still evil or do they become good and a new Townsfolk turned evil?

They remain evil, as they were turned on setup and their alignment being evil is not an ongoing effect and not linked to their character.

Does the Bounty Hunter sitting next to the No Dashii still turn a Townsfolk evil?

Yes, because it is a setup effect.

Can the Bounty Hunter learn the Recluse?

Yes.

Are the Minions and the Demon informed of the Townsfolk turned evil by the Bounty Hunter?

No.

Can the Bounty Hunter be the evil Townsfolk?

Yes, but this is not recommended.

Can the Bounty Hunter learn a Vigor-killed Minion?

Yes, it is possible for them to learn any dead evil player. The only restriction is that they cannot learn the same player twice in a row. The ST will need to consider if this is a fair move, since the BH only gets a new name when their current target dies, and the dead cannot die (unless they are first resurrected somehow), so showing them a dead evil player probably means that they will get no more info for the rest of the game.

If the Bounty Hunter dies and then is resurrected (Professor / Al-Hadikhia / ...) do they learn a new evil player?

Yes, which can be the same previously learnt player or a new evil player.

If an evil player the Bounty Hunter see dies, a new evil player is shown. But if a previously seen evil player is resurrected (Al-Hadikhia) and dies again, does the BH learn another evil player?

No.

For example:

  • the BH sees the Godfather on N1
  • the Godfather is executed on D1
  • the BH sees the Mezepheles on N2 and the Godfather is resurrected by the Al-Hadikhia
  • the Godfather is executed again D2
  • N3 the BH does not get a new name, as their current known evil player is still the Mezepheles

If the Butler votes when their master does not, what happens?

Mechanically, nothing. Their vote is still counted, otherwise the total will be less than it should be, automatically hard confirming the Butler, which is unfair for the evil team. Also, mistakes happen, just play on for now.

Later, the ST should speak with them privately and remind them of the constraints of their ability, and let them know that it is considered cheating to purposefully vote without their master. Generally this is enough to keep a player paying more attention, because most people are not playing this game in bad faith nor looking to cheat.

If they keep doing it though, then deal with it however the group would like to deal with cheating. Ending the game early, letting it finish but talking about it after, not inviting that person back, etc. There is no prescriptive option for what to do with someone who is cheating, as that is a social issue for the group to handle.

If the butler thinks they are poisoned or drunk, can they attempt to vote when their master is not voting to test this? / Can the Butler vote without their master to test for drunking / poisoning?

No, their ability is a social contract that they should abide by always as they have no way of knowing if their ability is functioning or not. Voting without their master is cheating and should be dealt with appropriately.

Could the Cannibal (turned by the Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter) eat the Recluse and guess the Damsel?

No.

Evil or good, the Cannibal is not a Minion.

If the Cannibal is not sure whether they ate an info gatherer (Fisherman / Savant / ...) can the ST just give them false info if the Cannibal asks for it?

No. If the Cannibal privately asks to use an info ability that they do not have, the ST should tell them that they do not have that ability. If the Cannibal is poisoned because a player was evil, then the ST is allowed to give them false info, but should only do so if the evil player was bluffing as that role.

Publicly claimed abilties like the Slayer, should be entertained in the way that the ST does for anyone else, but obviously they would have no effect if the Cannibal did not have the ability.

Does the Cannibal gain the role of an executed player that does not die?

No.

The execution must cause the player to die in order for the Cannibal to gain their ability. So executing dead players or protected players means the Cannibal does not gain their ability.

What does the ST say to the Cannibal when they gain an ability? / Is the Cannibal told what ability they gained?

The ST never informs the Cannibal of which ability they gain, except for the Butler as per the jinx.

Instead, the ST does what they would do for the standard character with that ability. So they would prompt the player to choose player(s) or a character if that is part of their current ability.

The Cannibal may then infer what ability they have based on what the ST prompts them to do. Or they could just ask the most recent executee what they are.

What happens when the Cannibal eats the Snitch?

The Minions are woken that night and given three out of play characters which may or may not be the same ones they or the Demon received previously.

Could the player Cerenovus targetted to be mad as a certain character claim to be the Cannibal with the ability of that character and be safe from a madness break execution?

No, as the player is not claiming to actually be that character which is the Cerenovus requirement.

Does the Zombuul's execution register to the Cannibal?

Yes, the Cannibal would be poisoned.

If the Cannibal gains the Fortune Teller's ability, how would the ST gesture for them to pick two players at night?

The ST can prompt the Cannibal to choose a player, then wait for them to choose, and then choose a player.

Alternatively the ST can make the sweeping "choose a player" gesture and then hold two fingers.

If there is confusion and the ST cannot get them to start the choosing process, writing a note on a phone and showing it to the player is fine.

If the Cannibal eats the Alchemist and is shown the Scarlet Woman, do they become the good Demon when the Demon is executed the next day, or are they the poisoned Cannibal?

They become the good Demon; the SW ability triggers before the Cannibal can switch abilities.

If the Cannibal eats a role that gained another ability (Pixie / Philosopher) does she see both roles?

No, the Cannibal just eats the original role.

The Cannibal does not care what else someone might have gained, just what their token is.

What is the Butler jinx with the Cannibal?

If the Cannibal gains the Butler ability, the Cannibal learns this, otherwise they could break the Butler rules regarding voting without realising.

If the Cannibal eats the Spy who registers as a good Townsfolk with a mechanical ability, such as the Monk or the Gossip), what would happen?

The Cannibal has that ability so long as the Spy continues to register as good.

Can the Cannibal change alignment after eating and gaining the ability of the Goon or the Cult Leader?

Yes, and if another non-alignment changing player is executed before they change back again, the Cannibal can be locked in as their changed alignment.

If the Cannibal is picked by a character checking ability (Dreamer / Gambler / Grandmother / Ravenkeeper / Undertaker / ...) what are they seen as?

The Cannibal, regardless of the ability they may have gained.

The Cannibal gains the ability of the recently killed executee, but what happens if that character is resurrected (Professor / Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia / ...)?

The Cannibal keeps their ability, because they are still the recently killed executee even though they are alive again.

Does the Cannibal who is resurrected (Professor / Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia / ...) still gain the ability of the recently killed executee that night?

Yes, they immediately gain the relevant ability.

For example, the Chambermaid is executed and dies, then the Professor resurrects the Cannibal that night, the Cannibal will wake the same night to use the Chambermaid ability, even though the Cannibal was dead when the Chambermaid was executed.

If an evil Townsfolk or Outsider (Bounty Hunter turned / Mezepheles turned / Cult Leader sat next to an evil player / flipped Goon) is executed, is the Cannibal poisoned?

Yes, the Cannibal is poisoned by any evil role.

How is the Cannibal Juggler ever going to get their info?

In the case of the Cannibal Juggler, there would have to be no new deaths by execution the day they juggled, so that they maintain their Juggler ability to find out the results of their juggle the following night. Perhaps town could kindly execute a dead or protected player, instead of someone who is going to die ...

The Spy is executed. Tonight, can the Cannibal cause a player to learn that the Cannibal is the Nightwatchman?

Yes. If the Spy is executed, they may register as any good character and cause the Cannibal to gain any good ability.

If the Cannibal gains the Alchemist ability, are they told what Minion ability they have?

Yes, and that ability does not need to be the original Alchemist's ability, as long as it is also an out of play Minion ability.

An evil player is executed and the Cannibal is poisoned. What effect can a Barista 1 have?

The Cannibal would have the sober and healthy ability of the evil player. Sometimes best not done if, for example, the Widow was just executed.

If a good Demon is executed and there are no other Demons alive, but the Cannibal is in play, does the game immediately end or does it continue until the Cannibal no longer has the Demon's ability?

The Cannibal with a Demon ability still is not a Demon, so with no Demon alive, the game would end.

What happens when the Cannibal eats the Drunk?

They gain the ability of the Drunk, so the ST deceives the Cannibal that they have any Townsfolk ability, usually whatever the Drunk thought that they had.

Regardless of what ability the ST pretends they have gained, if it is mechanical it cannot have an effect on the game; if it is informational, the information is arbitrary.

After eating the Drunk, if somoene else dies, does the Cannibal get to eat them or do they stay 'the Drunk'?

The Cannibal gets to eat them. They have the ability of the Drunk, but they are not actually the Drunk so their main Cannibal ability works just fine.

If a player who is scheduled to be Mezepheles turned is executed that day, is the Cannibal still poisoned?

The Mez can turn a dead player and the Cannibal is a constant check, so the Cannibal would become poisoned as soon as the recently executed player turns evil.

If the Cannibal gains the Pixie ability, and the other player dies, does the Cannibal keep the ability after Cannibal swapping?

When a new player dies from execution, the Cannibal loses the Pixie ability, and in turn loses any other ability they might have gained (although it is very difficult in the first place for the Cannibal to gain an ability via the Pixie ability)

If a player gains the Nightwatchman ability (Philosopher / Cannibal / Pixie / Apprentice) what are they shown to other players as?

Nightwatchman.

The "you" in these kinds of abilities refers to the ability itself. As it is the Nightwatchman ability, their target is shown the Nightwatchman token, not the token of the player with the ability.

The Cannibal wants to ask their Artist question / get their Savant info, but the player that died was good but not actually the Artist/Savant. What does the ST answer to the Cannibal-Artist/ Cannibal-Savant question?

The ST could reply with something like "I cannot answer that" / "You cannot do that", just as they would to any non-Artist/non-Savant who tries to use a question / get info.

The Cannibal Preacher hits a minion. The next day, another player is executed and the Cannibal no longer has the Preacher ability. Does the Minion wake and use their ability as normal?

Yes, the Preacher ability that hampers the Minion is no longer in play.

If the Cannibal who was nominated earlier in the game gains the Virgin ability, do they cause a Townsfolk who nominates them to be immediately executed?

Yes, it is a new instance of the ability and the player has not been nominated since getting it, so if a Townsfolk noms them they will be executed.

Does the Cannibal with the Savant ability get any hint from the ST that she can get two pieces of information?

No it is the Cannibal's job to find out what ability she might have by talking to executed players.

If the Mutant is executed, could the Cannibal be executed if for some reason they claim that they are an Outsider?

Yes.

They can claim to be the Cannibal with the Mutant ability, because that is not claiming an Outsider, that is claiming to be the Cannibal (who is a Townsfolk), but they are at risk of execution for any Outsider claims.

Does the Demon learn the Cannibal after the Lunatic is executed?

Yes. The Cannibal would have the all of the Lunatic's ability, which means the Demon must know that player as their Lunatic, and their choices.

What happens when the Cannibal eats the Lunatic?

The Cannibal is told that they are one of the Demons on the script. Some STs will confirm that they are still good, but RAW this is unnecessary. The ST takes the Cannibal's kill choices and informs the actual Demon that the Cannibal player is their Lunatic and who they chose. The Demon will then immediately know who the Cannibal is.

If the Cannibal asks what character they are at any point while they have the Lunatic ability, they should be told that they are the Demon that they were shown.

If they lose the Lunatic ability through a further execution, then they are treated exactly as they would have been had that execution occurred without a Lunatic execution beforehand. They are not told about no longer being a Demon but if they ask what character they are, they should be told that they are the Cannibal, with nothing confirmed about why they were told that they were a Demon.

All of this assumes that the Cannibal is not droisoned. If they ate an evil player then they can be lied to about their ability. And on a script with the Pit-Hag or the Fang Gu and the Drunk, it is possible for the Cannibal to believe that they really are the Demon.

The Cannibal eats the Philosopher, then picks Cannibal so they become drunk. Does the drunkenness get removed because they are what drunks themselves?

Droison loops are resolved by the involved players being droisoned. So the Cannibal drunks herself until another player dies by execution.

Riot and Cannibal. It states that nominated deaths count as executions for the Cannibal. Does that mean that the Cannibal can potentially have multiple abilities functioning that night and they do not know which ones are being used each time they wake up to use them?

The Cannibal's ability is still the most recently killed executee, so they only have the one ability at a time, though it may change rapidly as players nominate one another.

If the Cannibal eats the Snitch, do Minions gain another three bluffs or do they get nothing?

They get another three, since there is a new Snitch ability in play.

Could the Spy register as good therefore letting the Cannibal see the Grimoire?

Yes.

How does the Cannibal interact with the Spy?

The Cannibal cannot legitimately be treated as sober/healthy and having gained the Spy ability without having a legitimately good Spy already. The Spy specifically registers as good and as a Townsfolk or Outsider, so if the Spy registers as good to the Cannibal, they must also register as a specific Townsfolk/Outsider and the Cannibal would gain that ability instead.

Still, if the Spy registers as evil, the Cannibal is poisoned and can technically be deceived about anything, including seeing an accurate Grimoire!

Could the Cannibal gain a random ability after the Spy dies?

Yes, the Cannibal could get any good ability, though most of the time it is going to make more sense to register the Spy as evil to poison the Cannibal and then making up whatever is relevant.

What happens when the Cannibal eats the Recluse?

The ST has several options:

  • The Recluse registers as a Demon: the Cannibal gains a demon ability! Do not do this.
  • The Recluse registers as evil: the Cannibal is poisoned so the ST can pretend that they have any ability.
  • The Recluse registers as the Recluse: the Cannibal gains the Recluse ability and can register as evil or as a Minion or the Demon to other abilities.

If the Cannibal eats the Slayer do they learn they have a shot?

No, as with the Artist or any other ability that does not wake at night.

If the Cannibal eats the Grandmother, when do they get their info?

After they have had the chance to be drunk, poisoned, and killed.

If the Scapegoat, a Traveller, is executed, can the Cannibal gain their ability?

Yes. Travellers can get executed due to their ability (the Scapegoat) or madness breaks. And if a Traveller instead of being exiled is executed then the Cannibal gets that (good) Traveller's ability. Unless they were an evil Traveller, in which case the Cannibal is poisoned.

If the Cannibal gets the Goon‚Äôs ability and then gets selected by an evil player turning them evil, then the next day a new player is executed and they get that power, do they stay evil?

Yes. Interactions with the likes of the Goon and the Cult Leader can make evil Cannibals, but does require that the executed role not be evil at the time of their execution, else the Cannibal would be poisoned.

The possibility of too many evils getting created is why the Spirit of Ivory exists.

Do executions for breaking Cerenovous madness occur immediately?

At any time the ST decides to execute, but it always ends the day if it happens during the day.

How does madness work if there is a hard confirmed player (Golem / Virgin / ...) and the Cerenovus makes another player mad as that player's role?

It is not necessary for the player be believed as their madness target. As long as they make a good show and reasonable effort to convince other players that they are that role and argue against the confirmed player, they cannot be executed. Should they back down then they can be executed for a madness break.

Can a player Cerenovus mad as the role that they actually have, claim this and be safe from a madness break execution?

Often it does lead to execution because of its use as code for "I am not actually this role".

But a player claiming to be Cerenovus mad as their role is fine if the player is making a sincere effort to convince other players that that is what happened; this is fulfilling madness.

A good player is Cerenovus mad and breaks madness. The ST decides to not execute for the madness break. The next day the good player is no longer Cerenovous mad. Can the ST on any subsequent day execute the good player for the previous madness break?

The madness due to the Cerenovus ability is in effect until the end of the following night, so once that time has passed, their target cannot be executed for breaking madness because it no longer applies to them.

This does mean that after the Cerenovus picks a new madness target, the previous player could still be executed for breaking madness before the end of the night phase, but most STs would not do this as night executions usually make little sense.

Can the self mad Cerenovus be executed for breaking madness?

Yes, but it is probably best not to if it is final three so as not be too harmful to the good team.

Can the Cerenovus mad player claim to be the Philosopher turned into a good role, or does the play need to directly claim the good role?

The player must try to convince people that they are that role, not that they just have that ability. Otherwise, they can be executed for a madness break. It is up to the ST if they want to execute for breaking madness it that way, since it can be viewed as a more minor break, but it is still going against madness.

If a player is Cerenovus mad, dies, and then breaks madness in death, can they be executed?

Yes.

If a player is Cerenovus mad as the Butler, but votes when their claimed master does not, can the voting be cut off and she be executed for breaking madness immediately?

If the ST thinks that she is not being mad as the Butler, she may be executed. It could happen immediately though it is almost certainly better to at least wait until the vote is finished.

Suppose the Cerenovus maddens a dead player, to either maintain confusion or waste an execution. Someone else is executed; is it allowed for the mad player to break madness immediately after the announcement? Technically they will remain mad until the Cere's night order, but there is no longer a downside in breaking it. Is it cheating (so the ST could punish it by executing them tomorrow anyway), or maybe maddening a dead player is strong and can be taken down a notch, or maybe Cere can counterplay by maddening them again?

Executions can occur at night and it is a legal way to punish good sometimes. But as they are already dead, this will cause them to simply die, or well, nothing will happen. It might be best for the ST to not execute them to confirm nothing.

Is a player claiming there is a Cerenovus while they are mad (but still pretending to be the character that they are supposed to be mad about) breaking madness?

Not inherently, but madness is really subjective and context dependent.

If the Slayer made Cerenovus mad as another character publically claims Slayer, can she be executed for a madness break before she shoots?

Yes.

What is the Al-Hadikhia jinx with the Chambermaid?
