The Al-Hadikhia's targets do not register as waking, if they would not otherwise wake, because it is due to the Al-Hadikhia ability that they are waking.

Does the Cannibal gaining a night-waking ability and waking to use it, register to the Chambermaid?

Yes.

Does the Damsel waking to learn that they have been turned into a Townsfolk register to the Chambermaid?

Only if they wake due to their new ability, since players waking to learn that they are a new character is is not waking due to their own ability.

Does waking a Minion to tell them the Damsel is in play register to the Chambermaid?

No, that is not waking due to their ability.

Do the Drunk, Marionette and the Lunatic, who in reality do not have the ability that they think they have, "wake at night due to their own ability" for the Chambermaid?

Yes.

If the Demon is selected by the Exorcist, their waking to learn the Exorcist is not reflected in the Chambermaid's number, since they are waking due to the Exorcist's ability. However, if the Recluse registering as the Demon is selected by the Exorcist, then them waking to see the Exorcist is caused by the Exorcist's ability or their own, since it was their own misregistration that allowed them to wake?

They woke to the Exorcist‚Äôs ability so it does not register to the Chambermaid. They are not being tricked into believing something fake (like the Lunatic for instance), so it is not their own ability. The Exorcist still did choose them and directly cause their waking.

Does a new instance of the Evil Twin learning their twin ping the Chambermaid?

Yes. Learning that they are now the Evil Twin does not ping the Chambermaid, but waking due to their ability to know their twin is a Chambermaid +1.

Do "start knowing" roles, like the Grandmother learning their grandchild, register on their first night to the Chambermaid?

Yes, they woke up to their own ability.

The Lunatic wakes up to falsely learn a player is the Exorcist that selected them. Does this ping the Chambermaid?

Yes, as the waking is due to their own ability.

Do Minions, the Demon and the Lunatic getting their N1 info count as waking to the Chambermaid?

Only in the case of the Lunatic.

The Chambermaid detects if a player woke up for their character ability, and Minion and Demon info are a function of character type, not character ability. In contrast, the Lunatic, who wakes up to receive Demon info is detected by the Chambermaid because they are not actually a Demon and did wake up due to their own ability.

Does the King register to the Chambermaid?

Not unitl the dead outnumber the living. After that point he begins to wake up to receive his info and will start to register to the Chambermaid.

If the good Mezepheles turns themselves evil that night, does that count as a +1 to the Chambermaid?

Yes, they woke up due to their own ability.

Does the player selected by the Nightwatchman register to the Chambermaid?

No, as they are waking to the Nightwatchman ability, not their own.

Does the Pit-Hag who turns himself into a non-waking character register to the Chambermaid?

Yes. That player woke to an ability that they had at some point that night.

What number does the Chambermaid learn if they pick the Demon and the Snaker Charmer on the night that they swapped roles?

1. The starting SC woke to charm the Demon, then as the new Demon they killed. The starting Demon did not wake to their own ability.

Does the Scarlet Woman only count for waking for the Chambermaid's ability when they become the Demon?

Yes. But the ST might consider their waking up when the Imp self-kills is due to the Imp's ability, not the SW's ability, and not ping the Chambermaid.

The Snake Charmer picks the Demon. The Chambermaid checks the new Demon, who did not wake as a part of the Demon's ability, but as a part of the Snake Charmer's ability. Is that a +1 to the Chambermaid?

Yes. They were at one point in the night the Snake Charmer who woke as the Snake Charmer, which counts as waking to your own ability, so it is a Chambermaid +1.

Who can the Chambermaid pick if they are alive in a final two, where the Zombuul is registering as dead? The Chambermaid must pick two alive players but cannot pick themselves and there is only one other alive player.

They do not get any info. There is no need to even wake them.

If the Chambermaid chooses someone who died that same night, are they told to choose another player?

Yes. That will reveal to the Chambermaid one of their picks died, but the death is declared in the morning before anyone else should be talking so it does not matter.

If someone wakes and chooses not to use their ability (Professor / Philosopher / Courtier / Nightwatchman / ...) does it register to the Chambermaid?

Yes, they still woke to their own ability. If a player has a once-per-game ability, they wake up each night for their own ability so that they can choose to use it or not. Once it is used, they stop waking up.

Under Tips and Tricks for the Chambermaid: "Pick players to verify their claims. If someone is claiming to be the Gambler, they will wake up every night - check them and see if they are being honest. As another example, someone claiming to be a Courtier will only wake up each night until they have used their ability - if they are claiming to have used their ability, you can check to see if that is true by seeing if they wake up the next night!"

Does a Minion learning they are now the Imp alert the Chambermaid?

No. They are not waking to their own ability.

Telling a player their character has changed is not an ability's action, it is game mechanics.

Does a Minion / the Demon waking up to learn their new role after an Engineer swap ping the Chambermaid?

Only if they wake due to their new ability.

Does any character waking to learn of a change in alignment count for the Chambermaid, or just the Goon and the Cult Leader?

The Chambermaid only learns if the character woke due to their own power. So the Mezepheles turning someone, for example, does not count for the Chambermaid.

Does the Goon waking to learn she switched alignment register to the Chambermaid? And if the Goon is already the same alignment as what she would have changed to, does it count for the Chambermaid?

If the Goon wakes to learn their alignment changed due to her ability, then this registers to the Chambermaid. If she did not change alignment because the first person to pick her has the same alignment, then she would not have woken so no registering to the Chambermaid. If the Goon changes alignment through other means than their ability, such as Mezepheles, then this waking does not register to the Chambermaid.

Can the Chambermaid ping falsely off of misregistering characters (Spy / Recluse)?

No, they correctly learn that the Spy wakes and the Recluse does not.

Misregistration does not grant the abilities nor the waking pattern of the misregistered role.

  • The Spy who is alive and sees the Grimoire woke to their own ability, and misregistration cannot change this fact or stop the Chambermaid from getting a correct ping.
  • The Recluse who misregisters as the Demon does not actually wake up to kill and does not incorrectly ping the Chambermaid.

With the seating of Demon-Recluse-Minion-Minion, what could the Chef be shown?

The Chef number could be any of 1, 2, or 3 with this seating, as the Recluse can register as good and evil for separate instances of the Chef ability.

What does the Choirboy learn in a Lil' Monsta game?

The Choirboy would be shown the person babysitting Lil‚Äô Monsta the rest of that night and the next day because Lil‚Äô Monsta‚Äôs kill and therefore the Choirboy‚Äôs information comes after the babysitter is chosen.

If the Pukka targets the King and then the following night picks the Choirboy, does the Choirboy get poisoned info?

Yes.

The King would die as the previously poisoned player after the Pukka makes their next pick. That pick being the Choirboy means that they are poisoned when they awake and can therefore receive arbitrary info, before dying the following night.

If the Spy is killed by the Demon, could they misregister as the King and cause the Choirboy to learn the Demon's identity?

Yes, but that would probably not be fun for anyone.

If a multi-kill Demon (Al-Hadikhia / Po / Shabaloth) chooses the Choirboy after the King as part of the same selection, can the Choirboy learn the Demon?

Yes. Order matters: if the King dies then the Choirboy is woken and told the Demon player, even if the Choirboy then dies later as part of the same selection.

What does the Choirboy see in a Legion game?

Any of the living Legion players.

Could the Choirboy be shown the Recluse after the King is killed by the Demon?

Yes, though that is unlikely to be a fair move, especially if the Choirboy‚Äôs convincingly bluffed something else so the Demon does not think the Choirboy is in play.

Can the King be the Drunk or the Marionette if the Choirboy is in play?

No, that would be an illegal setup.

If the player who thinks they are the King is actually the Drunk or the Marionette, then the King is out of play and the Choirboy's [setup ability] has not been satisfied.

To avoid situations where the Demon is sat between a Minion and the King, leaving no valid Marionette, the ST should use an alternative setup.

Can the Choirboy be the Drunk or the Marionette if the King is in play?

Yes, this is a legitimate setup, where the King has not been forced into play by the Choirboy, they are there by their own right.

If the Choirboy is in the game, the King is not allowed to be the Drunk or the Marionette, but is it possible to have the King turned evil by the Bounty Hunter?

Yes.

In a two Minion game on a script with the Marionette, the King, and the Choirboy, after the roles are randomly assigned, the Demon ends up neighbouring one Minion and the King, who must become the Marionette, but the Choirboy is still in play. An illegal setup! How can this be avoided? Remove the King from the bag and put it back later as you do in a three Minion game?

The better move is to not have the Demon in the bag. Switching someone's token to the King would let a good player know an out of play role.

If the King is killed then resurrected (Professor / Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia / ...) then dies again, does the Choirboy get their info each time?

The Choirboy learns the Demon each time the King is killed by the Demon.

If the King is Barber swapped with a dead player, does the Choirboy get their info?

No, the King was not killed by the Demon.

If the King is killed by a non Demon (Gossip / Lycanthrope / Virgin / Moonchild / Assassin / Cerenovus / Godfather / Pit-Hag / Witch / Apprentice / Butcher / Gunslinger / Harlot / Judge / ...), does the Choirboy learn the Demon?

No, except if the player that kills the King is holding Lil‚Äô Monsta at the time and so registers as the Demon.

The Demon kill bounces off the Mayor to the King. Does the Choirboy get their info?

Yes. A bounce off the Mayor is treated as full redirection of the entire ability, so it is as if the Demon directly chose the King.

Who does the Choirboy learn if the Vortox kills the King?

Any non-Demon player.

If the single Minion in a game is the Spy registering as a Townsfolk/Outsider, what is the Clockmaker told? / What is the Clockmaker told if the Kazali chooses as their single Minion the player who is the Soldier?

When there is no way to get a step count between the Minion and the Demon, the ST shakes their head to indicate that there is no valid info.

Can the Clockmaker learn a zero?

The only way for the Clockmaker to learn a zero is if they are poisoned, drunk, or Vortox‚Äôd, but it would be an immediate giveaway that they are one of those things due to it normally being impossible.

If the Clockmaker sees either no Demons or no Minions, the ST simply shakes their head to indicate there is no valid information to give and puts her back to sleep. Outside of SnV:

  • a one Minion game with the Spy can give the Clockmaker a no,
  • in a Legion game, they should get the number of steps between the two closest Legion players, which is usually one.
  • in a Lil' Monsta game, they should see the number of steps between the Minion holding the baby and the nearest other Minion.

What is the interaction between the Recluse and the Clockmaker?

The Recluse can register as a Minion or a Demon to make a smaller Clockmaker number than there should be, but if a Minion and a Demon were sat right next to each other the ST could not use the Recluse to give a larger number to the Clockmaker.

If the Clockmaker is created mid game (Philosopher / Pit-Hag / Barber / Pixie / Cannibal / ..), do dead players count as spaces?

Yes.

Does the Clockmaker count Travellers when calculating steps?

Yes, as the Clockmaker counts "the number of seated players".

Can an ability gaining character (Philosopher / Cannibal / Pixie) be drunked if the Courtier chooses the character whose ability was gained?

No. Gaining the ability of a character does not make a player that character, they remain the character on their token.

The Courtier chooses to drunk an out of play Minion. However the Alchemist has that Minion's ability. Is the Alchemist drunked?

No. The Courtier drunks a character and if they are out of play, no one is drunked. While the Alchemist has a Minion ability, they are not that Minion, they are the Alchemist, so they are not drunked.

If the Courtier drunked Demon dies turning the SW, is the new Demon also Courtier drunked?

No, the Courtier drunkenness does not migrate; it stays on the targeted player. Courtier essentially uses the character to choose the player.

What happens if the Courtier drunked player changes character?

They stay Courtier drunk as once it has happened, the drunkenness is tied to the player.

What is the interaction between the Courtier and the Lunatic?

The Lunatic is still deceived that they are the Demon, but the actual Demon does not learn the Lunatic's choices.

If there are multiple copies of the same character in play (Legion / Village Idiot / Imp / Fang Gu / ...) and the Courtier chooses that character, are they all drunked?

Just one. The ST chooses one player with that character to become drunk.

What happens when a Courtier is drunk or poisoned while their ability is active? Does the day still tick by, or is their ability effectively paused while droisoned?

If the Courtier was sober/healthy when they used their ability, then their token is placed down. If they become drunk/poisoned then, while they are droisoned, their target is no longer Courtier-drunk. If they become health/sober again before the three days run out, the target is once again drunk. While the Courtier is droisoned, the timer continues to count down, so if the timer runs out before they become sober/healthy again, the target is simply not going to be re-drunked by the Courtier.

The Courtier drunks an out of play character that then comes in to play (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Engineer / ...). Is the player with that character now drunked?

No. The Courtier's drunkenness is applied, or not, to a player at the time of the choice, and will not change after the fact even if characters are changed.

If the Courtier dies before the three days are over, does the drunkness end?

Yes, unless otherwise stated, players lose their ability on death, so any drunkenness caused by the Courtier ends when she dies.

The Courtier drunks the Leviathan and for three days players execute good players with no fear. What happens when the Leviathan becomes sober? Evil team wins?

Assuming the Courtier remains sober, healthy and alive then: If N1 the Courtier hits the Leviathan (at which point, town actually do not know it is a Leviathan game, because making the Leviathan drunk suppresses the announcement). then only on day 4 is the announcement made, and the Leviathan has seen nothing, meaning the good team has two chances left to hit the Leviathan, or loses because of time (since it will be the end of Day 5 after the second execution). If N2 the Leviathan is drunked, then she will need to be executed on day 5 or good will lose on time/executions. If the Leviathan is drunked any later point than that, then good loses as soon as the Levi is sober.

Can the Courtier drunk fabled characters?

No.

The Courtier drunks players with the character that they pick, and as no player can be assigned a fabled character, only those listed on the character sheet, the Courtier is unable to drunk a fabled character.

If the Cannibal Courtier chooses the Demon, but then a non-Courtier is executed, will the Demon become sober?

Yes.

Can the Recluse registering as evil turn the Cult Leader evil?

Yes.

On N1, could the Cult Leader sat between two good players be turned evil by the Bounty Hunter then turn good again due to their own ability?

Yes.

Is the Cult Leader locked as evil if they die evil?

Yes, unless their ability reactivates (Professor / Bone Collector / Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia).

By dawn, the sober, healthy Cult Leader, the Demon, and a Minion are alive. Mechanically, must the game be over?

No. The Cult Leader does not know who the Demon is for sure and could possibly still accidentally nominate the Demon and lose.

What happens when the Cult Leader says the Mezepheles word?

If the Cult Leader is evil, nothing happens.

If the Cult Leader is good and is the first good player to say the Mez word, she turns evil that night. The Cult Leader still has her own ability, so may turn good or evil according to her neighbours. Interestingly the Cult Leader acts after the Mez in the night order, so she may switch from good to evil, then back to good in the same night.

If the Cult Leader changes their alignment, do they learn that immediately that night?

Yes.

If the Cult Leader is turned evil by the Mezepheles, can they later turn good again with their own ability?

Yes.

Does a Minion created mid game learn that the Damsel is in play?

Yes, assuming the Damsel is alive, sober and healthy.

Can the Damsel player be seen by the Balloonist twice, first as an Outsider and then, post-Huntsman-transformation, as a Townsfolk?

Yes.

If the Courtier drunks the Damsel, what happens when the Damsel is chosen by the Huntsman?

The Damsel becomes a Townsfolk and, since they are no longer the Damsel, they are no longer Courtier drunked.

After the Damsel is transformed by the Huntsman, what do character checking abilities (Dreamer/Gambler/Ravenkeeper/Undertaker/Harlot/...) see?

The see the new character post-transformation, not the Damsel.

The Huntsman transforms the Damsel into a Townsfolk. The former Damsel is Barber swapped with another player. Does the other player become the Damsel?

No, they become what the character that the former Damsel became, as the Damsel has changed, not just gained an ability.

Can the Huntsman-transformed-Damsel be Fang Gu jumped?

No, as they are no longer an Outsider.

If the Huntsman-transformed-Damsel is executed, does the Godfather get a kill that night?

No, as they are no longer an Outsider.

Can the Damsel be the Marionette if the Huntsman is in play?

No, but the Huntsman is allowed to be the Marionette.

Can the Damsel who is hosting the Lleech still be transformed by the Huntsman?

Yes, and they continued to be poisoned.

Does a correctly guessed Damsel change character twice if they have been Barista doubled?

No.

If the Philosopher picks the ability of an out of play character, then the Damsel is turned by the Huntsman into that character, what happens?

The ex-Damsel is drunked by the Philo.

What happens when an evil Townsfolk or Outsider (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter / ...) guesses the Damsel?

Nothing, because they are not a Minion. The guess is not used.

The Huntsman guesses the Cannibal / Philosopher with the Damsel ability as the Damsel. Is that player turned?

No, having the Damsel ability does not make the player the Damsel.

If a new instance of the Damsel enters play (Cannibal / Philosopher / ...), do the Minions get a fresh Damsel Ping?

No, they already knew the Damsel was in play so they are not informed again; the announcement is once per game no matter how many instances of the Damsel or their ability are created.

If a new instance of the Damsel enters play (Cannibal / Philosopher / ...), can the Minions guess the Damsel again if they previously used their guess?

Yes. But as they are not reinformed of the Damsel being in play they may not realise they have a fresh guess.

What happens if, after the Cannibal eats the Damsel, a Minion guesses the Cannibal as the Damsel?

Evil wins.

In order to correctly guess the Philosopher Damsel or the Cannibal Damsel, what does a Minion have to say? "X is the Philo/Cannibal" or "X is the Damsel" or either?

A Minion must guess "X is the Damsel".

The "you" in abilities always refers to the player's ability, not their character.

If the Damsel is drunk (Puzzlemaster / Courtier / Sailor / ...) do the Minions not get informed?

Puzzlemaster drunking would prevent the Minions learning the Damsel, as the Damsel is drunked during N1 setup. Other sources of drunking act after the Minion info step in the night order so cannot prevent the Minions learning the Damsel.

With that understood, using the Puzzlemaster to drunk the Damsel is not recommended.

What stops players from insisting that everyone publicly guesses themselves as the Damsel to prove that they are not a Minion to to waste the Damsel guess?

The ST is advised to ignore any forced statements.

Does each Minion get an individual Damsel guess?

No. The Minions collectively get one guess.

In a base two Outsiders game with the Huntsman, and no other Outsider manipulation, how many Outsiders comprise a legal setup?

Two or three:

  • two if the Damsel is one of the regular base two Outsiders
  • three if the Damsel replaces a Townsfolk, i.e. adding the Damsel with the Huntsman on top of the normal Outsider count.

Most players prefer it if the Damsel replaces one of the regular Outsiders rather than a Townsfolk for fun and balance purposes, but it is fine to do it sometimes.

Can the evil Apprentice guess the Damsel.

No, they may have a Minion ability, but they are not a Minion.

What happens if the Damsel is resurrected (Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia / ...)?

The Minions are not reinformed about the Damsel, as it is a once per game announcement. However, if there is a new Minion who has not previously been informed they would be informed, in which case it is best to not resurrect the Damsel using the Shabaloth.

If guesses have been made previous to the Damsel resurrection, they do not count for this new instance of the Damsel ability, so the Minions have one more opportunity to guess the Damsel.

If the Damsel is chosen by the Bone-Collector, what happens?

The Minions are not reinformed about the Damsel, as it is a once per game announcement. However, if there is a new Minion who has not previously been informed they would be informed.

If guesses have been made previous to the Damsel's bones being collected, they do not count for this new instance of the Damsel ability, so the Minions have one more opportunity to guess the Damsel.

Does a Minion babysitting Lil' Monsta, therefore registering as the Demon, still learn if the Damsel is in play?

Yes.

Can a Minion babysitting Lil' Monsta's guess the Damsel?

Yes.

Can a Legion player guess the Damsel?

Yes, as Legion players register as Minions.

Can the Witch who has lost their ability at three players left alive still guess the Damsel?

Yes.

What is the Damsel jinx with the Spy?

This is a hate jinx: only one of these characters can be in play.

What is the Damsel jinx with the Widow?

This is a hate jinx: only one of these characters can be in play.

Can an Imp who was a Minion guess the Damsel?

No.

Can the Damsel be the good twin to the Evil Twin?

Yes ... but that could end the game very quickly! This might be a good idea if the Courtier or the Heretic are on the script, so that instantly guessing the Damsel is not the automatic best move to make.

If the Damsel is Barber swapped to another player, do the Minions get another Damsel announcement?

No, it is a once per game announcement.

However, if a player is swapped into having a Minion character and was not one previously, then they are told about the Damsel.

This can result in a very bad day for the evil team if the Damsel is swapped with a Minion, as the good ex-Damsel-now-Minion knows somewhere there is an evil Damsel and, based on whether they are told that the Damsel is in play, would know whether the evil now-Damsel is alive or not and whether they can therefore be guessed to win the game.

Does the Monk protecting the Damsel prevent an evil win should a Minion make a correct guess?

No, unless in the unlikely situation where the Minion is holding Lil' Monsta and guesses at night.

The Monk protects against the Demon, not Minions, and only at night, so Monk protection does not prevent a correct Minion guess of a Damsel ending the game.

Does the Poppy Grower stop the Minions learning that the Damsel is in the game?

No.

Can a preached Minion still make a successful Damsel guess?

Yes, a Minion with no ability is still a Minion.

Does the Magician learn that there is a Damsel in the game?

No, they are not actually a Minion, nor can they guessing the Damsel have any effect.

Can the dead Damsel still be chosen?

No, once they are dead they lose their ability. Conversely, a dead Minion could choose a living Damsel.

If the poisoned Damsel is correctly guessed by a Minion, does their team still lose?

No. If a Minion claims Minion and guesses the Damsel while the Damsel is drunk or poisoned, the game continues and the guess is used up.

Do Minions get informed of the drunk/poisoned Damsel during N1?

Yes.

If the Damsel is in play, when do Minions learn it?

During Minion info.

If a good Minion is created while the Damsel is in play, will they be informed that the Damsel is in play?

Yes.

If the Marionette thinks they are the Damsel, do the other Minions learn that the Damsel is in play?

No.

What is the Marionette/Damsel jinx?

The Marionette does not learn the Damsel is in play.

Can the Minions Damsel guess at night?

Yes.

Is the self-protecting Devil's Advocate who became the new Imp after the previous one self-killed, safe from execution tomorrow?

No. After becoming the Imp, the Devil's Advocate became out of play so the protection is gone.

Can the Devil‚Äôs Advocate protect from a execution due to breaking madness (Mutant / Cerenovus)?

Yes.

If the Devil‚Äôs Advocate protects the Zombuul and then the Zombuul kills themself the same night, does the protection remain or disappear?

It remains, so double tapping the Zombuul player that day will not end the game!

Is there a way for the Devil's Advocate to protect the same player for two days in a row?

A new instance of the DA, created via the Barber swap, is free to choose whomever they want, which could be the same player the previous DA chose.

There are three players alive at the end of the day: the Pukka, the Devil's Advocate and the Sailor. At night the Sailor chooses the DA and the ST makes the DA drunk. The DA chooses to protect the Pukka and the Pukka chooses the Sailor, making them poisoned. The next day the Pukka is executed. Does the Pukka die?

Yes, because at the time the DA chose to protect the Pukka the DA was drunk, so they did not protect the Pukka.

If the DA chooses the Goon and gets drunked, and then the Goon is removed from the game by the Pit-Hag, does the protection remain on the player, or not since DA was drunk at the moment?

Not, as the token was never placed down in the first place because the DA was drunk so there is nothing that can "come back" so to speak.

If the Devil's Advocate is drunk / poisoned at the time they choose who to protect, then become sober / healthy before dawn, is there pick safe from execution?

No. At their turn in the night order, the DA's ability fails to protect their pick, and no reminder token would have placed, so the fact that they became sober / healthy is immaterial.

There are four players left alive and the only living good player uses the Doomsayer. Is the game over?

Yes. If you are the only living player of your alignment and you doomsay, you die.

Can the Doomsayer kill the invoking player?

Yes.

Can the Spy invoking the Doomsayer kill a good player?

Yes, the Recluse and the Spy, due to registering as good or evil, can result in a Doomsayer death of any alignment. The Spy and the Recluse can also both die to anyone using the Doomsayer as well. The Storyteller can make use of this for game balance.

What are considered to be 'good' and 'evil' roles when the Dreamer targets an evil Townsfolk / Outsider or a good Minion / Demon (Bounty Hunter / Mezepheles / Pit-Hag / Barber / ...)?

"Good character" and "evil character" actually have definitions in the game that are not about the alignment of the player:

  • "Good" characters are Townsfolk and Outsiders - blue tokens.
  • "Evil" characters are Demons and Minions - red tokens.

So the Dreamer is always shown a Townsfolk / Outsider for one character and a Minion / Demon for the other:

  • the Mezepheles-turned Townsfolk is still Dreamer seen as that Townsfolk token correctly or any Minion/Demon token incorrectly, even though they are now evil;
  • a good Minion could be seen as any Townsfolk/Outsider incorrectly and their Minion token correctly.

Could the Dreamer who picked the Recluse see a character other than the Recluse for their good character?

Yes.

Can the Dreamer choose the same player repeatedly?

Yes, the Dreamer's only restriction is not themselves and not Travellers. Picking the same player would likely result in the ST giving them the same answers, unless the demon switches to/from the Vortox or drunking / poisoning is involved.

Must the Drunk believe that they are an out of play Townsfolk?

No.

The Drunk must be believe that they are a Townsfolk which at setup is achieved by substituting the Drunk token with another Townsfolk token. It is due to the physical limitations of the game that the Drunk tends to see an out of play Townsfolk; most roles only come with one token. Village Idiot is an exception. However, should the Drunk be created mid game they can legally see an in play token, although they probably should not.

Can an Outsider be the Drunk?

An Outsider can be drunk but they cannot be the Drunk, as the Drunk must believe that they are a Townsfolk.

Is the character that the Marionette or the Drunk thinks that they are considered "in play"?

No.

If the Philosopher chooses the Drunk, what happens with the philo-drunk Drunk? / What happens if the Drunk is poisoned or drunked?

Nothing.

Any drunk or poisoned player is deceived that their ability is still working. The Drunk's ability is that they believe that they are a Townsfolk, so they just get treated like the Townsfolk they think they are.

Does the dead Drunk have an ability? For example, the Drunk who thinks that they are the Ravenkeeper.

The Drunk who believes they are the Ravenkeeper is woken when they die.

Is the Drunk affected by the Vortox?

The Drunk is actually an Outsider, deceived into thinking that they are a Townsfolk, and Outsiders are not affected by the Vortox's ability. So the information the Drunk gets from the ability they think they have is not affected by Vortox, and can be true.

However, in a game with a (healthy, sober and alive) Vortox, the drunk or poison status of Townsfolk is irrelevant - their abilities must yield false info.

On a script with character changers (Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) it is legal to tell the Drunk that they have changed character to a different Townsfolk, because it still satisfies the "you think you are a Townsfolk" part of the Drunk's ability?

Yes, as long as the ST makes them still think that they are a Townsfolk, it is fine to deceive them into thinking they changed. It is real fun to make them think they got turned into the Farmer sometimes.

Can the ST tell the Drunk that they turned into another Townsfolk character to the one they currently believe they are, to simulate the Pit-Hag?

Yes.

The Drunk/Marionette thinks they are a Townsfolk, and wakes up to falsely to learn that they are the Farmer. Does this ping the Chambermaid?

Yes, as the waking is due to their own ability.

When does the ST decide who the Drunk character is? / Can the ST decide which character the Drunk is after the tokens are distributed?

If the character has setup abilities that could change the Outsiders (Huntsman / Balloonist) then it should be decided that they will be the Drunk before tokens go in the bag, because the Drunk does not have the setup ability that would change the Outsider count. This decision cannot then change after token distribution.

Otherwise it is up to the ST. Most STs assign the Drunk once tokens have been handed out and know the Grimoire, allowing them to balance the game much better. The entry for the Drunk states "while preparing the first night", which would be once tokens are already handed out. But it is also fine for the ST to decide beforehand to make the Drunk a specific character regardless of token distribution.

If the Drunk or the Marionette is Pit-Hagged into play, can they be shown an already in play character?

Yes, it is just on setup that the Drunk and the Marionette cannot see a role already in play.

Can the Drunk think that they are an in play character?

At the start of the game no, unless it is a Bootlegger game or a it is a character which can start with multiples in play (Village Idiot). A mid game created Drunk (Pit-Hag / Barber) can legally be shown an in play character, but probably should not.

Is the Drunk, drunk?

Yes. The Drunk registers as drunk to any abilities that are concerned with drunkeness. So the healthy and sober Acrobat that neighbours the living Drunk will die.

Does gaining the Drunk's ability (Cannibal / Philosopher) make the player drunk, triggering the Acrobat's death?

Yes.

As the Drunk registers as drunk for the Acrobat, any player gaining the Drunk ability does too.

Does the Empath learn their neighbour even if they die at night?

No, the Empath only learns their living neighbours at their turn in the night order.

What happens when there are multiple instances of the Demon (Fang Gu / Imp) when the Engineer picks the new Demon?

All Demon players change character.

Are evil Townsfolk or Outsiders (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter / ...) affected by the Engineer's picks?

No, only the Minions or the Demon.

Can the Recluse misregister when the Engineer is picking the Demon or the Minions?

Yes, but don't.

Registering the Recluse as a Minion or as the Demon could cause them to be changed by the Engineer, or affect which characters are changed. But the Recluse is an Outsider so it is best not to use their ability like this.

The Bounty Hunter is in play, and the Engineer is evil. The three Minions decide to pass Lil' Monsta to the Engineer. The Engineer changes the Demon. Does this game now have three Minions and one Demon?

Yes, the current babysitter becomes the Demon. Their alignment does not change, so they remain evil.

The Pit-Hag turns himself into an evil Townsfolk, then the Engineer chooses which Minions exist. Does the ex PH turn back into a Minion?

No, the ex PH remains an evil Townsfolk. The Engineer does not change character types; the ST accepts however many Minions she picks to not make it obvious, but only makes use of the first few. so the Engineer would simply fail to create whatever Minion she chose.

Can the Engineer affect the Alchemist's Minion ability?

If the Engineer causes the Alchemist to have an in play Minion ability, then the Alchemist will need to swap to an out of play one. Otherwise, the Alchemist is not affected by the Engineer, as they are not themselves a Minion, they just have a Minion ability.

What is the Legion jinx with the Engineer?

Legion and the Engineer cannot both be in play at the start of the game. If the Engineer creates Legion, most players (including all evil players) become evil Legion.

Can the Engineer choose Lil' Monsta to be in play?

Yes, the former Demon becomes an out of play Minion of the ST's choice and is babysitting Lil‚Äô Monsta.

What happens to the babysitter if the Engineer swaps Lil' Monsta to another Demon?

The current babysitter becomes that Demon instead of whatever character they were previously.

What does the Marionette learn if they are swapped to another Minion by the Engineer?

They would be shown the "you are" info token and their new Minion character. They would be told nothing about their alignment as it has not changed.

The Townsfolk neighbour sat next to the No Dashii is turned by the Pit-Hag into the Evil Twin. What info do they receive?

They are now a good Minion, so the No Dashii poisoning moves past them to the next Townsfolk player. As they are now no longer poisoned, they are correctly told their twin: an evil player and their role.

Does the game end if the only two players that are alive are the twins?

Yes, evil wins.

Although no win conditions have been met in that scenario STs usually end the game if the Demon and the two twins are still alive as it is basically impossible for good to win at that point. Evil does not explicitly require the Demon to survive to final two to win. They just usually do, since good wins if there are no alive Demons. But the Evil Twin specifically prevents that win from happening so long as both twins are alive. So despite the Demon being dead, as only two players left alive is evil's win condition, evil wins.

Could the twins ever get bad information? i.e. is it possible that they think the other twin is someone else other than their actual twin?

The Sweetheart drunked player who is turned into the Evil Twin would learn wrong info, but would not cause anyone else to wake though, so only the drunk ET would get wrong info in this scenario.

If the Evil Twin ability is not active (Courtier drunking / Preacher / ...) when the good twin is executed, do evil instantly win when the ET's ability resumes functioning?

No, the good twin was executed while the ET ability was malfunctioning and it does not trigger retroactively. However, re-executing the good twin would trigger the regained ET ability.

If the Demon dies and the game continues due to the Evil Twin, what happens if the ET loses their ability (Courtier / Preacher / ...)?

With no living Demon the good team instantly wins when the ET loses their ability.

The Evil Twin knows the role of a twinned good player. If the Pit-Hag turns a good player into the Evil Twin, does the resulting good aligned Evil Twin know the role of their twinned evil player?

Yes.

Does the Evil Twin find out if their twin changes character (Pit-Hag / Barber ?

Yes, the Evil Twin always knows the ability of their good twin, so should be immediately informed of their new character.

However, if the Evil Twin is turned into something else the good twin does not learn this.

The Pit-Hag turns a good player into the Evil Twin, who is then twinned with an evil player. If the evil player is killed does that cause another evil player to become the evil aligned twin, since the Evil Twin is still alive and needs a counterpart?

No. The twins only change if the alignment of one of them changes. It is allowable to have a dead twin.

The Evil Twin is N1 drunked / poisoned. How should the ST run this?

The ET is decieved as to their ability working, so they are told an arbitrary player and a character. The actual good twin learns nothing. When the ET is sober and healthy, if they learned incorrect info then they will learn the real info, and the good twin will learn the ET. While the ET is droisoned, executing the good twin does nothing.

In SnV where the droisoned ET is rare, and impossible N1, STs will often wake the twins together, and have them make eye contact. But on custom scripts where there is a chance of a droisoned ET it is best practice to wake the twins separately.

What happens if the good twin in an Evil Twin pair becomes evil (Mezepheles / Cult Leader / Goon / ...)?

If the Evil Twin is still alive then a new good twin would need to be assigned.

The twins must always be of opposing alignment, so if they are ever the same, the good twin has to become someone else. The Evil Twin would wake with their new good twin that night to each learn each other. The good twin token is moved to the new player and the former twin no longer has anything to do with the Evil Twin.

If a new Evil Twin is created (Pit-Hag / Hatter) how is it run?

Each twin wakes individually to learn who their twin is and their character. The good twin does not have to be alive and generally should not be if the Evil Twin is created late game, when the good team would not have enough executions to win.

Does the Exorcist picking the Demon stop all of their abilities?

No. Although the Demon does not wake to attack tonight, any other Demon abilities still work:

  • the Zombuul stays alive if they have fake died once,
  • the player poisoned by the Pukka the previous night still dies,
  • the Shabaloth can still regurgitate a player.

What happens if the Exorcist picks the Lunatic?

Nothing. The ST is free to simulate what happens when the actual Demon is picked or they can completely ignore it.

Can the Lunatic be told that the Exorcist chose them?

Yes. Anything that the Demon could be told based on the characters on the script can be told to the Lunatic to aid with their deception.

The Lunatic can be told that they were exorcised when the Exorcist:

  • picked them,
  • did not pick them,
  • is not even in play.

A fake exorcism means that the Demon does not learn of the Lunatic's choice(s), because the Lunatic did not make any. The Demon would not know why this is, as it is indistinguishable from the Lunatic just being drunk or poisoned that night.

The ST must be cautious: if the Exorcist is in play they might publicly claim who they picked, and if this differs to what the Lunatic was told, then this could be detrimental to the evil team.

Could the Recluse misregister as a Minion and just die if picked by the Fang Gu?

Yes.

If the Fang Gu picks the Philosopher who chose an Outsider ability, does the Philo become the Fang Gu?

No. The Philosopher gains an Outsider ability, but does not become an Outsider.

Does the ST wake up the Outsider when the Fang Gu targets them?

If the Fang Gu kills an Outsider without a jump being possible, the Outsider just dies and does not wake. If the Fang Gu jumps, the Outsider is woken and informed of their new alignment and character.

Is there anything in the game that can grant another Fang Gu jump?

No, the Fang Gu jump is a hard once per game, no way around it.

No amount of Pit-Hag transformations, Barber swaps, Hatter switches or Snake Charmer antics can change this. The Fang Gu has a unique reminder token that is placed in the middle of the Grimoire if a jump happens and remains there even if the Fang Gu goes out of play and comes back in play.

What happens when a Fang Gu is protected (Monk / Innkeeper) and kills an Outsider for first time?

The Fang Gu jump is a "package deal" so if they cannot die there is no jump and the Outsider dies.

The once per game jump is not used up so if the FG later choose another Outsider while both are able to die, a jump can occur.

If the Pit-Hag turns himself into an Outsider and the Fang Gu kills him, does the jump happen?

If it is the first Outsider the Fang Gu has killed, then yes.

The Spirit of Ivory with the Bounty Hunter and Fang Gu. The BH adds one evil on setup. What happens if the Fang Gu attacks the first Outsider? A good Fang Gu?

The Outsider just dies.

If the Fang Gu hits the droisoned Recluse does she still jump?

In that instance, the Fang Gu has to jump, because the Recluse would be unable to register as anything other than the Recluse, an Outsider.

The Fang Gu is protected (Innkeeper / Monk). They choose to kill the Barber (first Outsider picked). What happens?

The jump is blocked so the Barber dies, and the ST offers the Barber swap to the (probably confused) Fang Gu.

If the Fang Gu picks the Barber what happens?

If the Fang Gu has yet to jump this game, and the Fang Gu can die, then the Fang Gu dies and the Barber becomes the evil Fang Gu and there is no Barber swap.

Otherwise the Barber dies and the Fang Gu can then swap two people's characters.

What happens if the Farmer is the last good player who dies in the night but there is a Marionette and an evil turned Townsfolk who might still pick the Demon, so the game cannot be called yet?

No one becomes a Farmer.

If the evil Farmer (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter / ...) dies in the night, who becomes the Farmer?

It is still an alive good player.

If the Farmer dies to the Demon creating a new Farmer but is then resurrected (Professor / Al-Hadikhia / Shabaloth / ...) could there be multiple living Farmers?

Yes.

If the grandchild Farmer is killed, could the Grandmother become a Farmer and not die?

Yes, because they are now a Farmer and therefore no longer have the Grandmother ability causing them to die. If the Grandmother instead dies to her ability then she is no longer a legitimate new Farmer choice.

What does a Barista doubled Farmer do?

The Farmer dying would cause two good living players to become Farmers.

What is the Leviathan jinx with the Farmer?

If the Leviathan is in play and a Farmer dies by execution, a good player becomes a Farmer that night.

If the Lycanthrope kills the Farmer and then becomes the Farmer, can there be other deaths that night?

Yes, as there is no longer a Lycanthrope ability in play preventing deaths.

Does the Mathematician get a +1 if a player becomes a Farmer, preventing them from using their previous ability?

No. As far as the Mathematician is concerned that player is the Farmer and their ability is working fine.

Can the Mayor bounce a kill on to the Farmer, triggering the Farmer's ability?

Yes. This could even cause the Mayor to become a Farmer.

Can the good Goon become a Farmer when the Farmer dies?

Yes. The previous Farmer player is not drunked as they are not themselves choosing the Goon with the Farmer ability, the ST is.

Does a player waking at night to learn that they are now the Farmer register to the Chambermaid?

Only if that player woke up due to their ability prior to becoming the Farmer, otherwise no, as changing character is not waking to their ability.

Can the Gambler who gambled wrong and died become the Farmer later the same night?

No, as they are already dead.

If a non-Farmer gains the Farmer ability (Cannibal / Philosopher / Pixie / ...) and dies at night, what do they turn another alive good player into?

They become a Farmer, it does not matter what their actual character was.

Suppose, due to the Farmer ability, there are two Farmers in the game and a Washerwoman is created after. Can the Washerwoman be shown both Farmer players as the Farmer?

Yes.

If all good players are Farmers and one is killed by the Demon, is one of the Farmers still woken up and told that they are a Farmer?

Yes, it is part of the Farmer's ability.

When does the Farmer proc at night, right after the kill or at their night order spot?

As soon as they are dead.

If a multi-kill Demon (Shabaloth / Al-Hadikhia / Po) kills the Farmer as their first pick, can their next choices be woken up and told that they are Farmers before their deaths are processed?

Yes. Probably best not to though.

Does a successful Fearmonger-execution of an evil Townsfolk or Outsider (Bounty Hunter turned / flipped Cult Leader / flipped Goon / Mezepheles turned / ...) or Minion or Demon (Poppygrower game) result in a loss for evil.

Yes. Sometimes the Fearmonger is better off not nominating until they know more about their target.

If the Recluse is Fearmonger-executed, who wins?

The ST can pick a side, but since Fearmonger wins are rare, it should be an evil win.

Can the Spy register as good and be Fearmonger-executed, resulting in an evil win?

Yes but don't.

The ST can pick which side wins, but it would be harsh on the good team to have the Fearmonger-executed Spy misregister, so it would be best to have evil lose.

If a player in a Revolutionary pair is Fearmonger-executed, could they register falsely?

Yes but don't, as this is then the ST picking the winner.

If the Witch cursed Fearmonger nominates and dies but gets their target executed, does their ability still trigger?

No, they are dead and have no ability.

If the Sweetheart is Fearmonger-executed, can they drunk the Fearmonger and prevent their win?

No. The Sweetheart's team loses before the drunking happens.

If the Fearmonger is successful in executing their target, could the Scapegoat be executed instead, preventing the game from ending?

Yes, but the ST should not do this as presumably the evil team worked hard to get the Fearmonger target executed and deserve the win!

If a player targeted and nominated by the Fearmonger survives the vote but is the same day executed for a madness break or nominating the Virgin, is the Fearmonger's win condition triggered?

No, their choice needs to be executed as a result of the Fearmonger‚Äôs nomination.

Can the Fearmonger win trigger if the Bishop is in play?

No.

The Fearmonger is completely neutralised since they cannot nominate in order to satisfy their ability. This combination of characters is best avoided.

Who wins when the Alchemist Fearmonger chooses and successfully executes the public Goblin?

Good wins.

If both the Goblin's and the Fearmonger's abilities are satisfied causing both a good and evil win, then the result is a good win as good wins on ties.

What happens if the Fearmonger chooses herself, then nominates herself and is executed?

The Fearmonger's team loses.

If the Fearmonger nominates and executes the Lleech host which team will win?

Evil wins.

The Fearmonger ability trumps the executing the Demon win condition, as ability wins, usually, trump normal game wins.

Usually, because exceptions are made in rulings if, for example, good could never win otherwise.

If the Fearmonger ability enters mid game (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Plague Doctor) how is it run?

If a player gains the Fearmonger ability, any choices they made as their previous character are not relevant to the Fearmonger announcement; their first pick will cause an announcement regardless of who it is.

Does the Fiddler override the Evil Twin's "good cannot win" ability?

Yes, the Fiddler overrides everything.

If the Fiddler is in play, can the Demon choose the Spy?

No.

If there is a circle where the Demon does not kill and the town does not nominate, what happens?

The ST can use the Fiddler, a Fabled character. At night, the ST wakes the Demon who must choose one good player. The next day, the town votes between the two on who should win. Everyone can vote, it uses no ghost votes, abilities cannot affect this vote, etc.

Does Fisherman advice have to be specific and can it be affected by the Vortox and misregistration?

The Fisherman gets whatever the ST wants to give them which can be as specific or vague as they want. Misregistration can affect it if the ST wants, and the Vortox must affect it.

If the Flowergirl is dead during the day and resurrected the next night (Al-Hadikhia / Professor / ...), are they told if the Demon voted the previous day?

Yes.

Does the Tea Lady protected Fool get spent when attacked?

No, any protection ability lets the Fool keep their ability.

Can the Pit-Hag's deaths are arbitrary ability kill the unspent Fool / Zombuul?

Yes. Effectively they were targeted twice so it appears that they were one-shot.

Does a dead player turned into the Fool come back to life as the once killed Fool?

No, they stay dead.

The Fortune Teller's Red Herring is any good player. What happens if that player is turned evil (Mezepheles / ...)?

The ST moves the RH token to a good player.

The Fortune Teller's Red Herring is any good player. What happens if that player is turned into a Minion or a Demon?

Nothing, as character type is unimportant. The RH must be a good player, so as long as that player remains good, the RH token stays put.

If the Fortune Teller checks an Imp who just starpassed and they are not a Red Herring will they show up as a Demon ?

Yes. Starpassing does not change the Imp‚Äôs character, just makes them dead and creates a new Imp. The FT just checks if any of the two players is a Demon, or registering as one, and a dead Imp is still a Demon. Some abilities specify 'the' Demon, which refers to the actual Demon, and these abilities target any alive Demons first, or players registering as one, and only if no Demon is alive do they target dead Demons.

If the drunked or poisoned Fortune Teller picks their Red Herring, do they have to get a yes?

If the FT is poisoned, they can get either yes or no, regardless of who is picked, unless it is a Vortox game.

Does the Barista 1 Fortune Teller receiving a 'no' on their Red Herring ping the Mathematician?

Yes, their ability worked abnormally.

Does the Gambler die immediately at the time of the gamble or at the end of the night?

They die at their turn in the night order. Generally deaths are immediate, just only announced at dawn, assuming they are still dead then.

Can the Gambler die from gambling the Recluse as the Recluse?

Yes.

The Deviant was funny today so cannot be exiled, but can the Gangster still kill them?

Yes.

Can the Gangster kill the Lleech?

No.

If the unspent Fool is attacked by the Gangster, are they safe?

Yes, and their ability is used.

What happens if the Gangster is holding Lil‚Äô Monsta and kills the grandchild with their ability during the day?

The Grandmother dies immediately too.

What happens if the Gangster is holding Lil‚Äô Monsta and kills the King with their ability during the day?

The Choirboy learns the Gangster is the Demon that night.

What happens if the Gangster is holding Lil‚Äô Monsta and kills the Sage with their ability during the day?

The Sage learns two players including the Gangster that night.

Can the Gangster kill a Tea Lady protected player?

No.

Is the sober Sailor safe from the Gangster?

Yes.

What happens if the Gangster is holding Lil‚Äô Monsta and picks the Soldier with their ability?

The Soldier does not die.

Can the Gangster kill their neighbour who is favoured by the Storm Catcher?

No.

Can the Gangster trigger the Virgin's ability?

No, the Gangster's choice is not a nomination.

Does the Witch-cursed Gangster die if they use their ability?

No, the Gangster's choice is not a nomination.

Can the Scapegoat die instead of the Gangster's target?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

Do Gangster kills prevent the Vortox's win condition?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

Are Gangster kills included in the Leviathan's execution count?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

If the Gangster kills the Demon in a Mastermind game, does the game continue?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution, so the Mastermind's ability is not triggered and the good team wins.

If the Goblin publicly claims to be the Goblin and is then Gangster killed, do evil win?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

If the Gangster kills the Evil Twin's good twin, do evil win?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution, and the good twin must be executed to trigger evil's win condition.

Can the Devil's Advocate prevent the Gangster's kill?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

If the Gangster kills the Saint, do evil win?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution, and the Saint must die by execution to trigger evil's win condition.

If the Gangster kills a Minion, does that trigger the Minstrel?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution, and the Minion needs to have died by execution to trigger the Minstrel's ability.

Can the Cannibal gain the ability of the Gangster's kill?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

Can the Pacifist prevent the Gangster's kill?

No, the Gangster's kill is not an execution.

Can the Undertaker see who the Gangster killed?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

Is a Gangster kill an execution?

No, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

If the public Goblin is executed while protected by the Devil's Advocate, does their team still win?

Yes, the Goblin does not need to die as a result of the execution to trigger their win condition.

If the public Vigormortis-killed Goblin is executed, does their team win?

Yes, they still have their ability through the Vigormortis and the Goblin ability does not require the Goblin to die from the execution.

If there are no Outsiders, what does the Godfather learn?

The ST wakes them and shakes their head to indicate a no. A zero would also work but that's not RAW.

In a base zero Outsider game, can the Godfather's Outsider modifier by -1?

Yes, just as the Vigormortis's modifier is -1 in a base zero Outsider game.

Can the Spy register as an Outsider to the Godfather?

Yes. Doing this during setup would be an Outsider ability hurting evil so not recommended. But the ST might want to do this after the Spy is executed to give the evil team an extra Godfather kill.

Can the Recluse register as the Spy who registers as an Outsider to the Godfather?

The Recluse who does not misregister as another role would ping the Godfather. If the Recluse registered as the Spy then she would not show up to the Godfather, which would be an Outsider ability hurting evil, so usually not recommended.

The Godfather and the Recluse are in play. Must the ST show the Recluse token to the Godfather or can she skip them due to their ability to register as a Minion/Demon?

The ST could do that, but STs should generally not use Outsiders to hinder evil, at least not during N1.

The GF could probably figure out that that means the Recluse is in play, unless there is other Outsider manipulation in play, or they might suspect that they are poisoned, perhaps accidentally by the Poisoner in a Poppy Grower game, so mistrust their info.

If the Pit-Hag creates Outsiders that the Godfather did not see at the start, does the Godfather get to kill, if one of the new Outsiders dies?

The Godfather gets to kill if any Outsider died, even one that did not exist at the start of the game.

If an Outsider is executed and the following night the Godfather is either resurrected (Al-Hadikhia) or created (Pit-Hag / Hatter) do they get a kill?

Yes, the Godfather is backward-looking so can potentially get a kill. They should be woken at their turn in the night order for their choice.

Does the Hatter's death leading to a mid game Godfather give the new Godfather a kill that same night?

Yes.

Does a Godfather created mid game (Pit-Hag / Hatter) learn the in play Outsiders?

Yes. Wake her up, inform her of her new character and the in play Outsiders regardless of their living status, then put her back to sleep.

Can the Pacifist protect the Golem's nominee?

No, the Golem's nominee is not dying as a result of an execution.

Can the Devil's Advocate protect the Golem's nominee?

No, the Golem's nominee is not dying as a result of an execution.

Can the Recluse registering as the Demon survive the Golem's nomination.

Yes.

Could an evil player bluffing as the Golem nominate the Tinker cause them to die?

Yes, successfully simulating the Golem.

Does Barista doubling the Golem have any effect?

The Golem is still limited to only nominating once per game, but when they nominate, that player dies twice. So the Barista-doubled Golem could kill an unused Fool completely in one nomination.

If the Golem has already used their one nomination, the Barista has no effect on them.

Can the unspent Fool survive the Golem's nomination?

Yes, and their ability is used.

If the Tea Lady's neighbours are both good do they survive the Golem's nomination?

Yes.

If the Golem nominates the player favoured by the Storm Catcher, do they die?

No, they can only die by execution, and a Golem nomination is not an execution.

Can the Golem kill the sober Sailor by nominating them?

No.

If the Golem nominates and kills a player, then the Pit-Hag changes them from the Golem and then back to the Golem, do they get to nominate again?

Yes, as it is a new instance of the ability.

Can a player that has previously nominated and becomes the Golem, nominate?

Yes.

Can the Golem kill the Vizier?

No. The Vizier's ability states that they cannot die during the day.

Can the poisoned Golem nominate again?

No, this is cheating.

The Golem nominates the unproced Virgin. Who is executed? Both are sober/healthy and the Virgin has their ability.

The Golem is an Outsider so does not proc the Virgin. The Virgin dies to the Golem's nomination because they are not the Demon. This is not an execution though, as the Golem's ability just causes a death. If it were instead a Philosopher Golem or a Cannibal Golem, the ST could let both abilities resolve.

Does the Witch-cursed Golem still get to kill?

If the Golem is cursed by the Witch, is sober and healthy and nominates a non-Demon, both players would die immediately. This includes if the Witch is nominated.

If the Devil's Advocate protects someone who is not the Demon, and the Golem nominates them, do they die?

Yes. The Devil's Advocate protects against death by execution, but the Golem's nomination kills someone but it is not an execution, so there will be no protection there.

Can the Golem trigger the Goon's ability?

No.

The Golem is not selecting the Goon at night, so is not drunked. They simply kill the Goon who dies with whatever alignment they are at the time.

If the Assassin picks the Goon first, the Goon dies, but do they also become evil?

Yes, the Goon dies and becomes evil.

Can the Goon drunk the Balloonist?

No. The Goon is not chosen by the Balloonist, merely shown to the Balloonist, so does not make the Balloonist drunk and is a valid player for the ST to show.

What happens if the Barber dies and the Demon chooses two players, one of whom is the good Goon?

The Barber swap happens normally with no alignment flipping or drunking.

The Goon's ability is unactivated; it reads "the first player to choose you with their ability", and the Demon player is picking them with the Barber's ability.

If the player selecting the Goon to die is made sober and healthy by the Barista, does the Goon still change alignment, or does the death override this?

Yes, the Goon changes alignment irrespective of whether they manage to drunk the responsible player.

If the Goon dies to the Boomdandy, are they turned evil?

No, nor do they cause any drunking, as the Boomdandy is not choosing the Goon with their ability.

If the Bounty Hunter learns the Goon as evil, can the Goon's ability trigger?

No. The BH being shown the Goon is not choosing the Goon with their ability, so they cannot be made drunk or flip the Goon.

In the almanac for Goon it says if the Courtier chooses the character Goon, they become Goon drunk, and turn the Goon good if they are the first person interacting with the Goon. The text for Courtier is "choose a character". Now the text for Cerenovus is "choose a player and a character". So rules as written, if the Cerenovus attempts to make a player mad as the Goon, the Goon character is chosen and the Cerenovus would be made Goon drunk and turn the Goon evil, correct?

No. The Courtier is targeting a player by way of choosing a character - only the player with that character token could possibly become Courtier drunk. (it is kind of like even though they are not pointing at the Goon player, their ability still is)

The Cerenovus is not choosing the Goon in the same sense. They are not interacting with the Goon player just by pointing at Goon on the character list.

The Courtier targets the Goon. What happens?

If the Courtier is the first to pick the Goon that night, then the Goon turns good and the Courtier is drunk. Ôªø

What happens if the Fang Gu picks the Goon?

If they are the first to pick the Goon that night, the Goon becomes evil and the Fang Gu becomes drunk. If someone already picked the Goon, and the Fang Gu has yet to jump this game, the Goon becomes the evil Fang Gu and the current Fang Gu dies. if someone already picked the Goon and there has already been a Fang Gu jump, then the Goon just dies.

If the Gambler gambles the Goon, does this make the Gambler drunk and the Goon turn good, or does the Gambler ability not trigger the Goon's ability?

If the Gambler picks the player with the Goon ability (what they gamble them as is not relevant), the Gambler is drunked, and the Goon, if the Gambler was the first to pick them that night, is turned good. If the Gambler gambles another player as the Goon, the Goon would have no effect on the Gambler.

Can the Goon drunk the Gossip?

No. Gossip kills are chosen by the ST not a player, so if the Gossip makes a true statement and the ST kills off the Goon with the Gossip ability, no part of the Goon's ability is triggered (drunking or alignment flipping), the Goon just dies.

The Innkeeper picks player X and the unpicked Goon, becoming Goon drunk. That night the Shabaloth picks the Goon and then player X in that order. Does player X die?

Yes.

The moment the Innkeeper chose the Goon, they were drunked, and no protection was placed - the ST does not place their reminder tokens in the Grimoire. When the Goon dies first, the Innkeeper sobers - the ST removes the Goon drunk reminder token. But no one is protected tonight - the Innkeeper tokens were never placed in the Grimoire.

If the King learns the Goon, could they trigger the Goon's ability?

No, as the King is not actively choosing the Goon with their ability.

What happens if the Lleech picks the unpicked Goon as their host?

The Lleech is Goon drunk and the Goon turns evil, but is still the host. Being drunked the Lleech fails to poison the Goon, so the Goon‚Äôs ability then continues to function normally throughout the game, despite being the host.

What happens if the Goon says the Mezepheles word? / Can the Goon drunk the Mezepheles?

If the Goon says the Mez word during the day, they turn evil that night, independently of their own ability. This does not drunk the Mez as they have not actively chosen the Goon player with their ability; it is the Goon that has actively triggered the Mez ability.

The now evil Goon can still be turned good the same night if a good player is the first to pick them, thereby flipping the Goon's alignment twice in the same night.

If the Nightwatchman chooses the unpicked Goon, what happens?

The Nightwatchman is drunked and the Goon does not learn who the Nightwatchman is.

Does the Ojo choosing the unpicked Goon cause no deaths?

Yes, additionally the Ojo is drunked and the Goon flipped / remains evil. This is consistent with other characters choosing the Goon (Philosopher / Courtier / ...)

If the Philosopher chooses the Goon ability, and there is an actual Goon in play, what happens?

The Goon drunks the Philo, becomes their alignment, and then the Philo is left with no ability.

If the Pit-Hag turns a good player into the Goon, do they become evil?

No, because the Goon was out of play at the time of the pick so was not targeted. So they would stay good, at least until another evil player chooses them first in the night. And that does include if a different evil player chooses the new Goon that same night, before any good players do.

If the Pit-Hag selects the Goon and tries to turn them into a role that is already in play, what happens?

If the PH is the first player to target the Goon that night, then the PH is drunked and the Goon turns/stays evil. Whether the chosen role would have worked does not matter, the Goon‚Äôs ability is about a player choosing them not whether the choice has an effect.

If the Pukka selects the Goon first, is the Goon still poisoned and dies after the Pukka becomes sober?

No, in this instance the Goon will turn evil, the Pukka-poison is not applied and the Pukka is Goon-drunk. No one will die to the Pukka this night, and the previously poisoned player is temporarily unpoisoned from the Pukka. When the Pukka becomes sober and healthy (next night probably), the player who was poisoned prior to choosing the Goon will be poisoned again and die later that night after the Pukka chooses a new target (so long as that new target is not the unchosen Goon again!).

How does the whole interaction between the Pukka and the Goon work?

If the Goon has been picked already that night -> Goon becomes poisoned, and dies next night If the Goon has not been picked yet -> Pukka becomes drunk, Goon becomes evil, no one dies tonight to the Demon. previously Pukka poisoned player is temporarily unpoisoned for as long as the Pukka has lost their ability When the Pukka regains their ability, the previously Pukka poisoned player dies after the Pukka picks again.

If the unpicked Goon is targeted by an evil player but cannot flip, because the Spirit of Ivory is in play and there is already one extra evil player, do they still drunk the chooser?

Yes.

What happens when the Widow poisons the Goon?

If the Widow chooses the Goon, the Widow is drunk and the Goon turns evil but remains healthy so can be turned good again on future nights. No one is told that the Widow is in play on N1. On N2, when the Widow is now sober, a good player is told the Widow is in play, but the Widow has no ongoing poison.

The Goon specifies that a player has to choose them in order for their ability to trigger, but if the ST picks them (Lil' Monsta kill / Legion kill / Gossip kill / Mayor bounce / Ojo picks an out of play character / ...), can they be flipped or drunk anyone?

The Goon just dies, drunking no one and no possible alignment changes.

The Goon ability is triggered only by the first player to pick them at night, and since the ST is not a player the ability is untriggered and the kill processes normally.

If the charged Po happens to select the Goon as the third kill and the Goon has not been selected yet and causes the Po to become drunk, do the first two kills happen or would they fail because the Po becomes drunk before dawn?

They happen. Except for the Al-Hadikhia, which has different mechanics to other Demons, players die the moment a Demon chooses them.

What happens when a multi-kill Demon (Shabaloth / charged Po / Al-Hadikhia / ...) targets the unpicked Goon?

Kills always happen in the order that they were picked. So, except for the Al-Hadikhia which has different mechanics, the previous targets, if unprotected, will die.

If the Po picks the Pacifist, the Goon and the Minstrel in that order, would only the Pacifist die, since the Goon makes the Po drunk saving themselves and the Minstrel? Or would all of them survive because of the Goon?

If the Goon has not been picked yet in that night, only the Pacifist dies.

If the Poisoner targets the Goon and the Pit-Hag changes the Goon into a Demon is the result an evil Demon or a good Demon?

If the Poisoner was the first person to target the Goon at night, the Goon turns evil, the Poisoner is Goon-drunk and the Goon is unpoisoned. If the Pit-Hag hits the Goon afterwards, the Goon just changes character, not alignment. So they would be an evil Demon and the Poisoner is no longer Goon-drunk.

Is the Goon awakened to learn they switch alignment?

Yes, every time. When the Goon changes alignment, they wake straight after the player who triggers them to learn this. Note, that this also registers to the Chambermaid.

Does the drunk or poisoned evil Goon stay evil?

Yes.

Can a Minion guessing the Goon is the Damsel, flip the Goon's alignment?

No, the Minion is not choosing the Goon with their ability.

Can a drunk or poisoned player or the Marionette, the Drunk or the Lunatic flip the Goon?

Yes. The player is still choosing, which is what the Goon cares about, not whether that choosing would actually do anything. The alignment change comes from the Goon's ability, so the Goon is the only player that needs to be healthy and sober for it to happen.

Remember that the Marionette would flip the Goon evil and the Lunatic would flip them good, which is opposite to what these characters believe should happen.

The Gossip gossips that someone is the Demon. The following night that player becomes the Demon (Pit-Hag / Barber / Engineer / Hatter / Fang Gu / ...). Is there a gossip kill?

No, the gossip is either true or not at the time the statement is made.

Is the Gossip allowed to make a compound gossip, i.e. "I gossip X or Y."?

Yes. The ST might prompt the player to specify if they intend it to be an exclusive or, i.e. exactly one thing is true.

If the dead Gossip made a true gossip during the day, then is resurrected (Al-Hadikhia / Professor), will there be a Gossip kill?

There is if the Gossip is resurrected before their turn in the night order.

If a non-Gossip during the day makes a correct gossip and then that night becomes the Gossip (Pixie / Philosopher / Cannibal / Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) does the new Gossip kill at their turn in the night order?

Yes. It is recommended that the ST tracks any player's gossips who could potentially become the Gossip.

If the Gossip makes a correct gossip during the day but that night is swapped to a different role (Pit-Hag / Barber swap / turned into the Farmer / ...) is there a Gossip kill that night?

No.

Could the Gossip making a correct gossip kill the Farmer, triggering the Farmer's ability?

Yes. The Gossip could even become the Farmer themselves.

Can the Gossip's kill target a player that cannot die, either because they are protected by an ability or are already dead?

Yes, but this is not recommended since the idea is that the extra kill tells the Gossip something.

Can "there are two Demons" be a correct Gossip statement when the Recluse is in play?

Yes, if the Recluse is registering as a Demon for it.

How is the Gossip affected by drunking and poisoning?

The Gossip is a backwards-checking ability. During the previous day, even if they were drunk or poisoned, if the Gossip made a correct statement, the ST would have placed the Gossip's dead reminder in the Grimoire. Then that night, as long as they are sober, healthy and alive, the Gossip kill goes through.

Can the Spy registering as good be seen by the Grandmother?

Yes.

Can the grandchild be a Townsfolk / Outsider turned evil (Mezepheles / Cult Leader / Goon / Bounty Hunter / ...)?

At the start of the game the Grandmother must be shown a good player. As the Grandmother is a 'you start knowing' character, not a 'you know' character, if their grandchild subsequently turns evil, she does not get a new grandchild and still dies if he is killed by the Demon.

A Grandmother created mid game cannot be shown the player turned evil.

If the Grandmother is created late into the game, can their grandchild be a dead player?

Yes.

The only restriction on the grandchild is that they are a good player. Showing a dead good player is allowed and doing so protects the Grandmother from being able to trigger their own death.

Does the Grandmother learn if their grandchild changes (Damsel / Pixie / Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) character?

No. The Grandmother only "starts knowing" their character, not "knows" throughout the game.

If the grandchild dies when the Grandmother is protected, drunk or poisoned, what happens the next night when the grandchild is still dead and Gran is no longer protected/droisoned?

They remain alive.

The Demon kills the grandchild at night while the Monk protects the Grandmother. Does the Grandmother die, or is she safe enough from the demon?

The Grandmother dies. They die to their own ability, not the Demon's. Now if Grandmother was Innkeeper protected, they would be safe.

If the Demon picks the grandchild Gambler who has died to their own gamble, does the Grandmother survive?

Yes. The Demon must kill the Grandchild in order for the Grandmother to attack themselves. In this case, the Gambler is dead and cannot be killed again.

Could the drunk or poisoned Grandmother learn on their first night a player's correct role, but their grandchild be another player?

Yes.

What happens if the Grandmother is poisoned on N1?

The ST still marks a good player as the grandchild and can then show a different player to the poisoned Grandmother. If the real grandchild dies to the Demon then the Grandmother, as long as she is not droisoned, will die regardless of if that is who she saw.

Can the Grandmother learn as their grandchild the Townsfolk turned evil by the Bounty Hunter?

No, the Grandmother's ability is that they start knowing a good player.

The Gunslinger may kill anyone that voted during the first vote of the day, but what if no player voted?

Then they cannot kill anyone.

A tally of zero votes during the first vote still means that there was a vote, so the Gunslinger does not get to wait to another vote where votes are actually cast.

If a vote to exile the Gunslinger does not succeed, can the Gunslinger use their power?

No, supporting an exile is not a vote, and calling for exile is not a nomination.

Can the Gunslinger kill the Lleech?

No.

Can the Lleech die if they reveal to the Harlot?

No.

If the Mayor agrees to be seen by the Harlot, could the ST kill the Harlot and use the Mayor bounce to kill another character?

Yes.

When do Harpy targets die?

At any point during the day or night until the Harpy picks again.

Do the Harpy targets die in order?

The order of deaths due to the Harpy ability can be chosen by the Storyteller, should that be important.

Do deaths caused by the Harpy count as executions?

No, the text says "dead", not "executed", so the day continues, unlike deaths caused by the Cerenovus.

If the Hatter is killed at night by the Demon, and one of the Minions chooses Poisoner, do they act that night?

No, as the Poisoner's spot in the night order will have already passed, since the Demon acts after the Poisoner.

When the Hatter is triggered, is there any standard to who should be prompted to choose first after waking the evil team together, or is it random?

No, the order is whatever the ST decides.

Living evils should probably choose before dead. As the evils wake together the ST could allow whoever wants to change first to do so.

If the Recluse misregisters, can they change character when the Hatter dies?

Yes, but don't as this is unlikely to be fun.

If the Hatter dies does can the evil Apprentice change their Minion ability?

No, they are not a Minion so unaffected by the Hatter.

If the Hatter dies does can an evil Townsfolk (Bounty Hunter / Mezepheles / Cult Leader) or the evil Goon choose a new character?

No, only Minions and Demons are affected by the Hatter.

Does a Minion or a Demon waking to make a choice after the Hatter dies register to the Chambermaid?

No, it is not their own ability causing them to wake.

If the Hatter dies and the Minions change characters, can they have a new Damsel guess?

No.

If the Hatter dies and a Minion or the Demon is drunk / poisoned, do they still change character?

Yes, they become the drunk / poisoned role that they chose, as the change is due to the Hatter's ability, not their own.

How is the Hatter ability run? / When does the Hatter ability activate?

The Hatter ability is immediate, similar to the Barber:

  • If the Hatter dies during the day, they use their ability before any other character.
  • If the Hatter dies at night, they use their ability immediately. The night order is only a reminder.
