Each Minion and Demon chooses their role, one after the other, knowing the previous choices.

What happens if the Hatter dies in a Legion game?

Nothing, as per the jinx.

What happens if the Hatter dies in a non Legion game and an evil player picks Legion?

All evil players become Legion, as per the jinx.

If Lil' Monsta kills the Hatter (and the variant rule is not being used), does the babysitting Minion choose from the Minions list, the Demons list, or either list?

The babysitter chooses a different Demon to become or they can opt to remain as Lil' Monsta by picking a Minion.

What is the Hatter jinx with Lil' Monsta?

If the Demon chooses Lil' Monsta then they also choose a Minion to become and babysit Lil' Monsta tonight.

Does a good Minion or Demon wake due to the Hatter dying?

Yes.

How does the Hatter and Poppy Grower interact?

The ST should probably wake the affected players separately.

If the Hatter dies on or after day five, can the Demon choose to become the Leviathan, instantly winning the game?

No, as per the jinx.

Can the ST be executed on a script with the Atheist to win via the Heretic?

No.

Why does the Baron have a possible +1 to Outsiders when the Heretic is on the script?

Because otherwise in a base two Outsiders game with the Baron and only four Outsiders on the script, the evil team can know for sure that the Heretic is in play, and then the Demon can kill themselves and win.

The Fearmonger executes the good Lleech host in a Heretic game. Who wins?

Good wins.

Abilities trump normal win conditions. So although the Demon died (good win) the Fearmonger win condition takes precedence (evil win), then the Heretic flips this to a good win.

In a final three of the Heretic, the Demon, and the Poisoner who is poisoning the Heretic, if the Poisoner is executed, does good win?

Yes. The Poisoner being executed means the Heretic is no longer poisoned, and since the evil win condition is satisfied in a Heretic game, good wins.

The evil twinned Saint and the Heretic are in play. The Saint gets executed. Who wins?

The Heretic applies last, so the Saint being executed (assuming they are the good Saint) would cause evil to win, then the Heretic flips it to a good win, unaffected by the Evil Twin. This means that evil cannot win in a Heretic game so long as the twins are both alive.

Why are the Godfather and the Heretic jinxed?

The Godfather knows which Outsiders are in play. If they learnt that the Heretic is in play, they could tell the Demon to kill themselves, resulting in a free win for evil.

As per the jinx, the Godfather in play means there can be no Heretic in play. Does this also apply to the Alchemist Godfather?

Yes. Jinxes apply to abilities not characters so an Alchemist Godfather means the Heretic must be out of play.

If the Heretic is drunk or poisoned what happens?

If the Heretic, regardless of living status, is drunk or poisoned when the game ends, then her ability does not function so the win conditions are not reversed.

What happens if there are two Heretic abilites in play, due to the Cannibal or the Philosopher?

Two sober and healthy Heretic abilities would cancel each other out, making win conditions normal again.

Does an alive Philosopher Heretic drunking the actual Heretic cause win conditions to be flipped?

Yes. But should the Philosopher die, both Heretic abilities would then function, cancelling each other out.

Does the Cannibal or the Philosopher with an "even while dead" ability, such as the Heretic's, keep that ability when they die?

Yes, they lose the Cannibal/Philosopher ability but keep any "even while dead" ability.

Does the good wins ties rule apply before or after the Heretic's ability?

The Heretic flips the winning team after the game has ended. So if two win conditions are satisfied at once, good wins on ties, which is then flipped by the Heretic causing evil to win.

For example, in a final three of the Heretic, the Vortox and the Mayor the day ends without execution results in an evil win: No execution with three alive with both Vortox and Mayor in play means a good character win condition competing with an evil character win condition, so good wins. The Heretic ability is then applied, so evil wins.

If the Demon killed themselves in a Heretic game but the Heretic became drunk afterwards (but in the same night), would that be a good win?

No. The game would end instantly as the Demon dies; nothing would happen later in the night. The Heretic would have to be drunk or poisoned before the Demon dies.

Can you show the High Priestess themselves?

Yes.

Can the High Priestess only receive living players?

No, you show them dead players too.

Who does the drunk / poisoned High Priestess see?

Anyone.

Who does the High Priestess see in a Vortox game?

The only restriction is that the ST does not give the one player that they would have given if it was not a Vortox game. It does not have to be the least helpful player to talk to.

Can the Pixie see the Huntsman?

Yes. This would confirm to the Pixie that both the Huntsman and the Damsel are in play.

Does the Huntsman actually change the outsider count? Or does it turn an already existing outsider into the Damsel?

ST choice.

Adding an Outsider does sound like a terrible Townsfolk ability, but it is a legal move. The players will not know for sure if the ST added the Damsel on top of the base Outsider count, but generally the Huntsman does not. The decision could depend on how weak or strong the good and evil characters that are in play. Players would likely prefer you swap an existing Outsider, as the other option is far too much of a downside for good and essentially removes two Townsfolk for nothing.

Could the Huntsman add the Damsel and then the Godfather or the Vigormortis remove it?

No, the end result is an illegal setup.

In a base two Outsiders game, if both the Godfather and the Huntsman are in play, does the Huntsman modify the base two outsiders or can the Damsel be the +1 outsider added by the Godfather?

With the Huntsman's ability, the ST: either changes a Townsfolk into the Damsel (so +1 Outsider), or changes instead an existing Outsider into the Damsel (no change in the Outsider count). Note however that the Huntsman cannot add a second Damsel while there is already one in play.

In a Huntsman Godfather game, the Outsider count could be anywhere between one and four in a base two Outsider game: 1 Outsider: The Damsel. The Godfather removed an Outsider 2 Outsiders: The Godfather removed an Outsider and the Huntsman changed a Townsfolk into the Damsel. 3 Outsiders: The Damsel is already in play and the Godfather added an Outsider. 4 Outsiders: Godfather added an Outsider and the Huntsman changed a Townsfolk into the Damsel. Probably some of them are unbalanced, but all of there are technically allowed.

The Monk protected player is safe from the Demon. Does this mean a Monk protected Minion cannot become the Demon if the Imp self-kills?

Safe means harmful effects like death, poison, or turning evil. Changing characters, including becoming the Demon, is not a harmful effect so the Imp can successfully pass to a Minion even when Monk protected.

If the Monk protects the Imp about to self-kill however then the jump is blocked.

If the Imp self-kills, do they remain an Imp for character checkers (Fortune Teller / Ravenkeeper / Dreamer / ...)?

Yes.

When an Imp self-kills, and there are several Minions alive, is there a priority order for who should become the new Demon?

The Scarlet Woman must become the Demon if their ability is active (alive, not drunk or poisoned, 5+ alive players), as that is the entire point of their ability. Otherwise, it is the ST's choice which living Minion becomes the Imp from the Imp's ability.

When an Imp self-kills turning a Minion into a new Imp, are the entire evil team notified about the identity of the new Demon?

No, only the new Imp. The other evils are not notified, but they will know that it happened since their Demon died.

If an Imp self-kills do they get to choose which Minion becomes the new Imp assuming there is no Scarlet Woman?

No, that is the ST's choice. The evil team can of course inform the ST of a plan they have involving the starpass landing on a specific Minion, and the ST may choose to aid that plan, but the ST is not obligated to do so.

If the Imp kills the Mayor, can the ST use the Mayor to bounce the kill back to the Imp, forcing the starpass?

Yes.

Can multiple Imps self-kill in one game? / Can the Imp change more than once in the same game?

Yes, it is part of the Imp's ability and is not a once per game action like the Fang Gu jump.

The physical game comes with four Imp tokens, since (not including Recluse hijinks) that is how many Imps there could end up being.

The Shabaloth picks the Innkeeper first, then one of the Innkeeper's picks second. Who dies and how is the Innkeeper drunking affected?

The order of the Shab's choices matters and characters die, if they can, as they are chosen. So the Innkeeper dies the moment they are chosen and any protection and drunking they are the source of leaves the Grimoire immediately.

If the unpicked Goon is targeted last by a multi-kill Demon (charged Po / Shabaloth), the Demon's previous picks still die. However, if the Innkeeper chooses to protect the unpicked Goon second, their first pick is unprotected. Why?

The difference between a multi-kill Demon and the Innkeeper is that kills are instant and are not retroactively undone if the Demon loses their ability, while the Innkeeper needs their ability to protect players.

Can the Spy in a single Minion game misregister to the Investigator, giving them a 'no' or a '0'?

Yes, it is a legal move, if not necessarily a fun one.

Can the Investigator see the Recluse as a certain Minion?

Yes, and this is a common occurrence.

Can the Librarian or Investigator ping on themselves? Such as when seeing a Drunk or Marionette respectively?

The Librarian or Investigator player is "a player", so they can see themselves. So it is a legal move, if not necessarily a fun one.

Why are the Evil Judge and the Fearmonger a broken combination?

The Judge can force through whatever nomination the Fearmonger makes even if it gets zero votes. For this reason it is no recommended to have the Judge as a Traveller option on a Fearmonger script.

How does a a mid game created Juggler (Philosopher / Cannibal / Damsel / Barber / Pit-Hag / Pixie / ...) work?

It is the first day with the Juggler ability that a player can juggle. So they would juggle the day after they become the Juggler and learn their info the following night.

The Juggler can juggle someone as multiple characters but can they juggle a player as the same character multiple times?

Yes.

This is a legal tactic to tell their info apart, although not everyone considers it a useful move. Using this strategy the Juggler can juggle one person once and and another person twice, using the resulting 0, 1, 2, or 3 to narrow down their info.

If the Juggler does not Juggle, do they still get a number?

This can be ruled either way:

  • Some STs rule that even if they do not claim Juggler they can still get information.
  • Some STs rule that the "public" aspect of Juggler requires an actual claim in Town Square and no claim means no info.

These are both legitimate rulings, and can make a difference in a Vortox game.

When does the Philosopher Juggler have to juggle to get their info?

The day after they picked the Juggler ability. They are then woken the following night to gain their info.

When the Juggler gets her info, is it the info at the moment she wakes? Or is it at the time she juggled?

The info is tied to what was true at the time of the juggle; any role changes since the juggle are ignored.

If the Juggler is changed into something else by the Pit-Hag on the night she would have received her number, does she still receive info of her juggles?

No.

The Bone Collector picks the dead Juggler. When does the Juggler need to juggle?

They must juggle during the day, when they are dead and have no ability, and then the following night when they are bone collected they get their info.

How does a dead Juggler that is resurrected (Professor / Al-Hadikhia / ...) work?

She gets a completely fresh ability, so can she juggle the following day and get answers that night.

How does a Barista 2 Juggler work?

The ST would have to decide how they would want that to work.

If the Kazali were made drunk by the Puzzlemaster, would they still be able to make Minions?

Yes, because the setup brackets occur before start of game effects such as the Puzzlemaster, the Poppygrower etc. The same way the Bounty Hunter cannot be made puzzledrunk to not add an extra evil Townsfolk.

Does the Demon learn who the Lunatic Kazali chose as their Minions?

Technically the Lunatic ability requires this, but the ST is free to choose that they do not.

What info is there to hide from the Kazali in a game with the Poppy Grower?

During Demon info the Kazali is not told who their Minions are, even though they just picked them. They do learn their bluffs and any other relevant info to the Demon (Marionette, King, Lunatic).

The Minions are told their new character and any other relevant information (Damsel) but do not learn the Kazali. When running in person games, the ST should put the Kazali to sleep and wake each Minion separately.

Most of the time it is not that important as the Kazali can just gather the evil team together and get them up to speed, though it is more relevant if the Goon or the Soldier are on the script which can disrupt the Kazali's picks.

Can the ST give a new Minion‚Äôs previous role to the Kazali as a bluff?

Yes, but that might be considered nerfing the power of the Kazali.

When the Kazali picks the Baron, are two extra Outsiders added?

No, nothing happens.

What does the Kazali's [-? or +? Outsiders] setup modifier mean exactly?

It works as a wild card so that no matter what Minions the Kazali creates, and what number of Outsiders or Townsfolk are replaced, the result will always be a valid setup.

If the Kazali chose an Outsider, then their setup was [-1 Outsider]. If an extra Outsider was added to the base count but then the Kazali chose none, their setup was [+1 Outsider].

The players have to keep that in mind when the Outsider count is not aligning with what should be in play.

What happens when the Kazali picks the Goon to be a Minion?

As per the jinx, the Goon becomes evil and the Minion the Kazali chose. The Kazali is now drunk for the rest of N1 so any remaining Minion picks are ignored by the ST who decides the rest of the evil team herself. During Minion info, when the Kazali is told their true Minions, they will likely guess what happened.

As per the jinx the Kazali cannot choose the King to become a Minion if the Choirboy is in play. How is this run, since the Demon does not yet know who the King is?

If the King and Choirboy are both in play and the Kazali happens to randomly choose the King, the ST shakes their head no and forces them to choose again. If after all of their picks the King still exists, the Kazali is told who the King is.

When does the Kazali learn the King?

After she has picked her Minions.

Can the Kazali choose to make the Marionette?

Yes, she must choose one of her neighbours though.

What happens if the Soldier is N1 selected by the Kazali?

The Soldier does not become a Minion so the Kazali is down one Minion for the game. She will realise this if she pays attention during the Demon info step.

How does the Magician work in a Kazali game?

The ST should put the Kazali to sleep when waking each Minion to tell them their character has changed, then show both the Demon and the Magician during the Minion info step.

Does a Townsfolk player still turn evil if the Kazali turns the Bounty Hunter into a Minion?

No. As per the jinx, an evil Townsfolk is only created if the BH remains in play after the Kazali acts.

Does waking to learn that you are now a Minion in a Kazali game register to the Chambermaid?

No, as that is not waking due to their ability, but the Kazali's.

What is the Kazali jinx with the Huntsman?

If the Kazali chooses the Damsel to become a Minion, and the Huntsman is in play, a good player becomes the Damsel.

Do the Minions still learn about the Damsel if the Damsel was picked by the Kazali to be a Minion?

No, they would only learn about the Damsel if they remain unpicked, and after the Kazali has made all her Minion picks.

How is the Alchemist affected by the Kazali's picks?

Once the Kazali has chosen her Minions, the ST will give the Alchemist an out of play Minion ability.

Apart from the Goon, is there any other way for the Kazali to be affected by poisoning or drunking characters on N1?

No, the Kazali acts before all such characters.

How is the game affected if the Balloonist is turned into a Minion by the Kazali?

The Balloonist's setup effect can be duplicated by the Kazali's, so the Balloonist is a valid pick.

What happens when a new instance of the King is created mid game (Pit-Hag / Barber / Damsel / Philosopher / Cannibal / Pixie / ...)?

If there are enough dead, the player can get information that night.

Also the Demon learns the player as the King immediately, and if she did not learn of a King on N1, then she will reason that the Choirboy is out of play, and that she can kill the now-King with impunity.

Does the Zombuul who is registering as dead count towards the King's "dead outnumber the living" requirement?

Yes.

Does the Demon learn of the Apprentice King?

Yes.

If the King is resurrected (Professor / Shabaloth / Bone Collector) is the Demon told again who the King is?

Yes.

What does the King learn in a Vortox game?

Characters that are out of play or already dead.

Can "the King" for the Choirboy ability refer to any character with the King ability?

No, the King only. Philosopher King, Drunk King, Marionette King, Cannibal King, Pixie King - none of these would count for the Choirboy ability.

Does the Demon learn the Drunk who believes that they are the King?

No. The Drunk believing that they are the King is not the King. On the other hand, the King who N1 is drunk, or poisoned, does not alert the Demon until they are sober / healthy.

Does the Demon learn the Marionette who believes that they are the King?

No. The Marionette believing that they are the King is not the King.

Does a newly created Demon learn who the King is?

Yes. The King's ability, which is a constant check, says "the Demon knows" so new Demons learn who the King is.

Does the King include Travellers in the 'dead outnumber the living'?

Yes. If they were were not, the ability would say so, like Scarlet Woman does.

The Pukka kills the Klutz. Is the Klutz poisoned when they must pick someone the following morning?

No.

The Klutz gets nominated in a Riot game and dies. Do they have to pick someone before (optionally) nominating?

Yes. Their countdown will restart if the game is continuing. So it would look like this:

  1. ST: dies. 3... 2...
  2. Klutz: I claim Klutz and pick x.
  3. ST: The game continues. 3... 2...

Can the Knight see Legion?

No, they must see two non-Legion players as each Legion player is a Demon and cannot be seen by the Knight even when registering as a Minion.

Can the Knight see the ST if Atheist is on the script?

No, the ST is not a player. However, if the Atheist is in play then the ST breaking the rules can be shown.

Can the Knight see the Recluse?

ST choice; it depends on how the Recluse registers.

Can Legion register as a Minion to the Slayer?

Yes, but this would be in addition to registering as a Demon, not instead of, so the Legion player will stay die.

Legion registers as both Legion and an arbitrary Minion at all times, with said Minion misregistration only overriding their normal registration if an ability forces a collapse into one state or the other. In the case of the Slayer, it has no effect since the Slayer ability does not have any exclusive interactions with Minions; as such, they still get killed for registering as the Demon.

If the Puzzlemaster correctly figures out who is drunk in a Legion game, what do they learn?

The ST chooses one Legion player to show them.

What does the Balloonist see in a Legion game?

A Townsfolk, an Outsider and two Legions as each Legion also registers as a Minion.

Does an evil Townsfolk (turned by Bounty Hunter / flipped Cult Leader) vote count in a Legion game?

No. Votes still need a good player to pass.

Does Legion register to the Chambermaid?

No, Legion players never wake from their own ability.

What do character checkers (Dreamer/Juggler/Gambler/Ravenkeeper/Undertaker) see when they pick a Legion player?

They can see a Minion since Legion registers as a Minion in the same way that the Recluse does.

How does the Exorcist interact with Legion?

When the Exorcist picks a Legion player, that player learns the Exorcist, but deaths due to Legion are not prevented that night as Legion does not wake.

Do Legion learn the King?

The ST can show as many Legion as she wishes that the King is in play. At least one Legion player is recommended.

Can there be the same number of Legion as there are good players?

No, that be an illegal setup. 'Most players are Legion' requires Legion to outnumber the good players.

What happens if Legion kill the Sage?

The Sage learns "two players, one of which is the Demon who killed them". So the ST can show any Legion player as the one that killed the Sage and any other player (including another Legion). The only illegal option is to show two non-Legion players

If the Recluse and all Legion vote, can the ST count it as zero votes?

Yes but don't. The evil team would not appreciate an Outsider ability being used to expose everyone who voted.

In a Legion game, what can the Investigator see? Can they see a Legion token?

The Investigator would not see a Legion token, as that is a Demon token. They would see the token of a Minion from the script. Each Legion can register as a Minion, as well a a Demon, so the Investigator / Undertaker / .. can see a Minion token instead of a Legion, which is recommended given that the ST typically wants to help Legion deceive town as to whether Legion is in play.

Legion do not know other Legions, right?

Legion learn other Demons/Minions like normal.

All alive Legion can potentially kill one player, right?

Yes, though Legion should usually never kill more than two, and if they do multi-kill it should be multiple Legions. Multi-kill is usually done to support a world pushed by the Legions so it balances out. For example, if a Legion is bluffing Gossip and asks the ST to kill an extra player tonight, the ST will typically comply and kill one more Legion.

Does the Juggler juggling a Legion as a Minion always get a 1?

No, the Legion player can register as a specific Minion that is not the one juggled.

Do Legions learn each other in a Teensyville game?

No.

Can the drunk Investigator learn of a Legion who is out of play?

No, the Investigator can never see Legion; Legion registers as a Minion, but the Legion character is not a Minion character.

What can the Investigator see in a Legion game?

They can be shown a Legion and any other player and any Minion token.

Can the Fortune Teller receive a yes on any Legion player?

Yes, plus they still have a Red Herring.

Does any Legion player voting in a nomination register to the Flower Girl?

Yes, regardless of whether the vote tally ends up being zero.

A Minion is executed on D5 of a Leviathan game. Does the Minstrel activate, allowing for good to win by executing the Leviathan on D6?

Yes.

The Leviathan will be drunk until the end of the next day at dusk, so their win condition cannot trigger until they sober up. Any execution will happen before this time giving the good team the chance to execute the Leviathan.

If the Leviathan becomes drunk or poisoned after the first dusk, are the players told that the Leviathan is in play when they become sober and healthy?

No, all players already know the Leviathan is in play if they have been already announced it. The extra day notifications are just there for the players to remember the day count.

On N1 the Poisoner learns two players as the Demon. Could she poison one to confirm who is the Leviathan and who is the Magician?

Yes.

If the Leviathan is drunk or poisoned then no announcement goes out until they are sober and healthy. So, unless the ST runs the Leviathan differently, the Poisoner could use this to confirm the real Demon.

If the Leviathan becomes another Demon (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Engineer / ...) does everybody learn that the Leviathan is no longer in play?

No. There is no active ability letting players know the Leviathan‚Äôs state, so there is no mechanical reason to tell the town the Leviathan is out of play. Some STs will announce the Leviathan is in play every day in which case they would have to stop saying that, but it is not required.

This is similar to how:

  • the good twin is not informend if the Evil Twin becomes a different character,
  • the Vizier is not announced as no longer being the Vizier when swapped to another character, etc.

Can the Leviathan kill at night?

No, that is not part of their ability.

The Pit-Hag creates a Leviathan and the ST kills the old Leviathan. If a good player has already been executed, would executing the good Leviathan lose the game for the good team or win it? Does the "two good executions" counter reset?

The Pit-Hag cannot turn someone into a character that is in play so this cannot happen. Any individual Leviathan does have its own good player executed counter though, if it was not alive and sober to see an execution, it did not count to them.

With the Leviathan, if the Recluse is the second good player to be executed can they register as evil to continue the game, then later change how they register to make evil win at any time?

No, it is only looked at at the time of execution.

Can the Recluse register as evil so that their death not count towards the Leviathan's win condition?

Yes.

The Choirboy is useless in a Leviathan game or is there a special rule like with the Ravenkeeper, the Sage, etc.?

There is no jinx. The King is also usually useless with the Leviathan because the dead will not outnumber the living unless there are a lot of other killing roles.

If the Leviathan is executed on day five, and the Scarlet Woman is in the game, what happens?

The SW becomes the new Levi and the game ends with an evil win. Despite it being a new instance of the Levi, the day count is universal and does not reset, so the Levi's wincon is met.

Is a Pit-Hag making a Leviathan after day 5 an automatic win for evil?

No, there is a jinx preventing the PH from creating the Levi after day 5.

D1 a good player is executed. N2 the Courtier drunks the Leviathan and the next day the Courtier is executed. Does the game end immediately?

No. The Leviathan was drunk when the Courtier was executed, so they did not see the second execution.

The Widow poisons the Leviathan permanently. During the first four days, town executes 2+ good players. On day 5, the Widow is executed. Does the sober Leviathan need to see two more good players executed, or does evil win after the Widow is executed?

The poisoned Leviathan did not "see" any good executions so when she becomes healthy her count is at zero, but the healthy and sober Leviathan does win the game because day 5 is over.

Can the Leviathan win the game as a regular Demon wincon? where there are lots of nightkilling characters in the script, and the Leviathan stays alive with only one remaining alive player?

Yes, evil's normal win condition of two players alive always applies and ends the game.

If the Leviathan gets drunk or poisioned, do the days reset?

No, the days are universal. However, any good executions while the Leviathan is drunk or poisoned do not count towards their win condition.

If the only Outsider in play is the Recluse, could the Librarian learn a zero?

Yes.

Does the Alchemist wake up with the Minions to decide who babysits Lil' Monsta?

No, the Alchemist is not a Minion, they merely have the ability of an out of play one.

If a player holding Lil' Monsta Barber swaps herself with a different player, does the Lil' Monsta token stay where it is or does it follow the swap?

(Standard caveat: there is no write up for Lil' Monsta) Best guess: since the Barber only swaps characters, and no player is Lil' Monsta, the Lil' Monsta token likely stays put.

If the Courtier drunks Lil' Monsta, what happens?

For three nights:

  • the Minions do not wake to choose who holds LM; the ST does not wake the Minions to deceive them that they are working normally as no player is LM.
  • nobody dies due to LM.
  • LM cannot move; whoever was holding LM before the Courtier picked will keeping holding LM
  • the player holding LM is not themselves drunk so can still use their ability

Good wins as normal if the babysitter dies.

(Standard caveat: there is no write up for Lil' Monsta)

If the Exorcist picks the Minion holding Lil' Monsta, does the Minion still get their ability, or any player holding it for that matter?

Unknown.

If the Exorcist picks the player holding Lil' Monsta what happens?

The Exorcist only ever stops the Demon, if selected, waking up to use their own ability, but Lil' Monsta never wakes in order to kill so if the babysitter is selected the LM kill still goes through. However, as the babysitter is registering as "the Demon", they do not wake to use their own ability. In LM games the Exorcist is essentially a really bad Preacher.

If the good twin babysitting Lil' Monsta is executed while the Evil Twin is alive, which team wins?

Evil.

Character abilities trump normal game win conditions, except in some situations, including some where LM is involved ...

Does the player holding the Lil' Monsta token register as the Demon to the Flowergirl?

Yes. The Flowergirl looks back so would learn if the player holding the token in the day voted even if the token moved that night.

Does the player holding Lil' Monsta register as the Demon to the Fortune Teller?

Yes.

If the Gambler gambles a player as Lil' Monsta, does she die everytime?

Yes, a player is never LM.

What happens if the public Goblin holding Lil' Monsta is executed?

Good wins, as it would be impossible for good to win otherwise.

The Lunatic, the Marionette and the King are all "the Demon knows who you are" abilities. How does this work in a Lil' Monsta game?

Each time the player holding Lil' Monsta changes they become "the Demon" and, the first time they become the babysitter, they are told who those characters are.

If the Marionette babysits Lil' Monsta, while they still learn the Lunatic and the King, they do not learn that they are the Marionette because of the Marionette jinx with Lil' Monsta.

If the Lunatic is for real given Lil' Monsta (as opposed to the ST simulating this) then, as well as learning that they are the babysitter and being shown the King and the Marionette, they learn that they are their own Lunatic, and are told their own Lunatic choices, because the real Demon learns the Lunatic's choices.

Does a Lil' Monsta Lunatic work? Would the Lunatic think they are a Minion?

No, it would need another Demon on the script for the Lunatic to think they are.

How is Lil' Monsta affected by the Minstrel triggering?

Unknown. Either:

  • Lil‚Äô Monsta is not affected by the Minstrel; it can kill and change babysitters, even though the Minions are drunk.
  • There are no deaths and the Minions do not wake together.

Most likely it is the first option, since the Minstrel ability specifies that players are drunked, not characters.

Does the Preacher affect Lil' Monsta because a Minion most of the time holds the baby.

The Preacher stops the Minion's ability but not LM's ability to kill and move around. "Lil‚Äô Monsta: A Minion who is selected by the Preacher while holding the Lil‚Äô Monsta token loses their Minion ability, but retains their Lil‚Äô Monsta Demon ability."

Can the Psychopath holding Lil' Monsta kill the Soldier?

(Standard caveat: there is no write up for Lil' Monsta) The concensus is no.

Does the Recluse registering as a Minion and waking with the regular Minions to decide who babysits LM register to the Mathematician?

Yes.

If the good Saint is holding Lil' Monsta and is executed, which team wins?

Good, because in a tie good wins.

Can the Scarlet Woman holding the Lil' Monsta Barber swap with the previous Minion that was holding the Lil' Monsta?

Yes.

Is the Scarlet Woman‚Äôs ability "reusable‚Äù in a Lil' Monsta game?

Yes, probably, but there is no official LM write up yet so who knows?

If the Snake Charmer picks the Lil' Monsta's babysitter, what happens?

They swap characters and alignment. Do they swap babysitter? Unknown, but does it matter? Whether the SC now holds LM is irrelevant since the SC picks before the LM does, so the Minions, which might include the former SC, will wake up after the swap to pick the next babysitter anyhow.

Can the Soldier hold Lil' Monsta? Or is being the Demon considered a negative effect?

The Soldier can hold LM.

Could the Spy babysitting the Lil' Monsta misregister as non-Demon?

(Standard caveat: there is no write up for Lil' Monsta)

To be fair to the good team and their abilities, perhaps treat the misregistering Spy as if they were a good Townsfolk or Outsider holding LM so that abilities that ask "is this a Demon" should still yield a yes.

Can anyone babysit Lil' Monsta?

Yes. LM can be given to any player, as long as the majority of the Minions agree. The person is then informed that they are babysitting. Giving the LM to a good player will usually result in that player announcing such so is not always a good idea. Giving the LM to a Traveller who leaves will cause the game to end.

Can the ST sink a kill in a Lil' Monsta game? / In a Lil' Monsta game can there be no deaths at night, perhaps simulating a Mastermind day?

Yes. The ST is free to target any player with the LM ability, including:

  • dead players,
  • protected players that cannot die (Innkeeper / Soldier / Monk / ...),
  • evil players.

Do evil Townsfolk or Outsiders (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter / ...) or evil Travellers wake to choose who babysits Lil' Monsta?

No, only Minions.

Is a good player holding Lil' Monsta informed that they are the babysitter?

Yes, they get woken and told that they are holding Lil' Monsta and, as applicable, learns the King, Lunatic and Marionette. Except when the Marionette holds LM as they do not learn that they are the Marionette.

If the babysitter dies in a Lil' Monsta game that continues (Mastermind / Evil Twin), do the Minions get to choose a new babysitter?

No, if the babysitter dies so does Lil' Monsta, so the ability cannot continue.

Do dead Minions get woken up to decide who babysits Lil' Monsta?

Yes.

Can other killing roles add on to Lil' Monsta's kill? Or does LM's ability 'a player dies each night' mean only one player can die each night?

There can be extra kills due to other abilities on top of Lil' Monsta's kill.

In a Lil' Monsta game, what is an evil Traveller told?

Whoever is currently babysitting. If they are present from the start of the game, probably best wait until the babysitter has been decided.

Would a good Minion (Pit-Hag / Barber) learn who all the other Minions are in a Lil' Monsta game?

Yes. This could be prevented with a house rule that only evil Minions wake.

What do character checkers (Dreamer / Undertaker / Ravenkeeper / ...) see the Minion holding Lil' Monsta as?

As their Minion character. No player is ever Lil' Monsta so no player can be seen as LM by any character checking abilities.

Can Travellers hold Lil' Monsta?

Yes.

In a Teensyville Lil' Monsta game, do the Minions learn each other?

Yes.

In five and six player games, the Minion and Demon info steps do not happen, but character abilities still work as normal. So the Lil' Monsta ability still allows the evil team to learn each other, at the point that they wake up together to choose who babysits.

What happens if the Lleech host is the good twin?

In order for good to win, the Evil Twin must be killed first and then the good twin.

Evil always wins if the good twin is ever executed while the Evil Twin is alive. So while executing the good twin does kill the Lleech, the living Evil Twin's wincon would trigger, giving evil the win.

What happens if the Exorcist chooses the Lleech?

The Lleech does not wake but their host remains poisoned and must die in order for the Lleech to die.

What happens if the Lleech host is the Heretic?

As per the jinx, the Heretic remains poisoned when the Lleech dies so good can win by executing the Heretic.

If the Lleech poisons his Marionette/Lunatic on N1, does he still learn that that player is his Marionette/Lunatic?

Yes, he will have already learned that player before he picked his host.

If the Lycanthrope attacks and kills the Lleech's good host, does the Lleech die despite the Lycanthrope's no other player can die ability?

The Lleech should probably die too. Lleech and Lycanthrope may be a problematic pair.

Can the Mayor N1 bounce the Lleech to avoid being the host?

No, they become the host. They are therefore poisoned and without an ability, unable to win in final 3 or bounce kills at night.

Does the Lleech host protected by the Monk become unpoisoned?

For that night, yes.

If the Monk protects the Lleech, is the Lleech prevented from dying with their host tonight?

Yes, but as per the drunk or poisoned Lleech host dying rule the Lleech should probably die despite the protection.

What happens if a new Lleech is created (Scarlet Woman / Engineer / Pit-Hag / Barber / Hatter / ...) and they select as their host the Monk protected player?

They still become the host, but for that night they are unaffected by the Lleech poison.

If the Lleech is in play and the Pit-Hag makes a second Demon, what happens?

Deaths are arbitrary, so the ST should pick whichever option makes the most sense for that particular game at that particular moment: Ôªø * kill the Lleech, which means the host must also die (poisoned but then become healthy);

  • kill the newly created Demon instead.

Does resurrecting the Lleech host (Professor) also resurrect the Lleech?

No.

In a final five that includes the Lleech, their host and the Scarlet Woman, the host is executed and dies, so the Lleech dies, does the SW become the Lleech?

RAW the SW becomes the Lleech, chooses their host, then kills that night, resulting in a loss for the good team. Some STs houserule this interaction to avoid situations where good cannot win, such as not allowing the SW to kill the same night that they become the new Lleech.

There is a similar conflict between the Shabaloth and the SW.

What is the Slayer jinx with the Lleech?

If the Slayer slays the Lleech's host, the host dies, and the Lleech dies too if they are sober and healthy.

Can the Soldier, who is safe from the all the harmful effects of the Demon, be the Lleech host?

Yes.

Dying, being poisoned, and turning evil are examples of harmful effects. Being the Lleech host is not a harmful effect, because when the host dies so does the Demon, and that benefits the good team.

So the Soldier is not poisoned by the Lleech, but they are still their host.

Does the Lleech's host die poisoned, should the game continue for some reason (Scarlet Woman / Mastermind / Evil Twin / ...)?

Yes.

Does the Lleech host register as evil?

Only if they are already evil, because they are a Minion or where turned evil (Goon / Cult Leader / Bounty Hunter / ...). If the host is good, then they will register as good to alignment checkers like the Empath.

When there is a new Lleech (Scarlet Woman / Hatter / Barber / Snake Charmer / ...), is another host chosen?

Yes. The same host can be chosen, depending on how the new Lleech is created.

Can the Lleech host be a Traveller?

Yes, although they rarely make good hosts: if the Traveller host is exiled or they leave, then they die, so the Lleech dies too.

What is the ruling for the Lleech being drunked or poisoned when either they or their host is executed?

If the Lleech is drunk:

  1. they die when executed
  2. they do not die when the host dies
  3. they become immortal if the second point happens even when they become sober again, unless the recommended ruling is run that the Lleech dies even if drunk when the host dies.

Can the Lleech self-host?

Yes. They are self-poisoned for the rest of the game meaning they cannot kill at night and can die.

If the Lleech becomes a different Demon (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Engineer / ...), does the Lleech host become healthy?

Yes.

If the Lleech makes it to final three, is that an instant evil win? Since if the host is executed, that would create a final two before the Lleech dies.

If the Lleech host is executed in final three, the good team wins, as the Lleech and the host die simultaneously. This is a rare example of simultaneous death in Clocktower.

If a new Lleech is made (Scarlet Woman / Pit-Hag / Engineer / Hatter / ...) when do they select a host?

A new Lleech chooses their host as soon as possible, then follows that by choosing a kill.

If the Courtier drinks with the Lunatic, does the Lunatic still believe that they are the Demon?

Yes. The Lunatic will have pulled their Demon token out of the bag and learned fake info before the Courtier would be able to drink with them.

While the Lunatic is drunk (by Courtier or otherwise) the ST treats them like the Demon that they think they are, waking them up to get their choices, but the actual Demon is not informed of their picks.

If the Courtier drinks with the Lunatic on day one, would the Demon learn of the Lunatic?

Yes. N1 both the Lunatic waking to learn their fake information and the Demon waking to learn their real information happens before the Courtier acts.

However, if a droisoned player is turned into the Lunatic, the Demon would not learn about them until the Lunatic is sober and healthy. When the new Lunatic does become sober and healthy the Demon would be informed as soon as possible.

What does the Demon learn if the Lunatic Fang Gu picks an Outsider?

The Demon learns who the Lunatic chose. The Lunatic has no interaction with Outsiders just because they saw the Fang Gu token.

If the Lunatic thinks that they are the Fang Gu and the Fang Gu jumps to them, what are they told?

They woken and told that they are the Fang Gu and are evil.

Their character and alignment changed, and they no longer have the Lunatic ability that allows the ST to lie about it. Ôªø

If the Lunatic-Fang Gu is Fang Gu-jumped, is she told that she is now evil?

The ST informs the new Demon of their character and alignment as it changed and they no longer have the Lunatic ability.

If the Fang Gu jumps into the Lunatic who sees himself as the Fang Gu, does the ST still tell the Lunatic again that he is the Fang Gu?

Yes. Players learn when their character and alignment have changed, and the Lunatic will be a real Fang Gu meaning they no longer any character ability that allows some deception with that anymore. They are actually changing character and alignment even though it is to what they may have already thought.

So the ST would wake them up and inform tell them "You are the Fang Gu, you are evil."

Can the ST make the Lunatic who has figured out what they are believe that they have been Fang Gu jumped?

Yes.

What happens when the Lunatic picks the Goon?

If the Lunatic is the first to pick the Goon at night then:

  • the Goon is flipped to good / stays good
  • the Lunatic is drunked, so the ST deceives them that their ability, that they belive they are the Demon, is still working
  • the Demon is not informed of the Lunatic's picks that night

When a player is drunk or poisoned, they are deceived into believing that their ability is working normally. The first part of the Lunatic's ability is a "you think" ability, which means deceiving the player about what they are. So a drunk or poisoned Lunatic is deceived into believing that their ability is working normally ... which is to believe that they are some other character. So nothing has changed.

However, drunkeness or poisoning does shut down the other mechanical part of their ability, which is to inform the Demon of their picks.

If the Hatter dies, can the Lunatic be given the choice to change characters?

Yes, this does not even need the actual Hatter to die.

Does the Demon learn who the Lunatic Lleech chose as their host?

The Demon learns who their Lunatic picks on N1 but does not learn what Demon they believe they are, so from the Demon's perspective they could be learning who the Lunatic Pukka picked to poison.

The Lleech picks the Lunatic N1. Does the Lleech learn who the Lunatic picks at night?

No, the Lunatic is poisoned.

If the Lunatic thinks that they are the Lleech, does the Demon learn who they picked N1?

Yes. The Lunatic ability reads "and who you choose at night", so the Demon learns who they picked. But the Demon does not learn why they picked, so if the Pukka and the Lleech are on the script, then the Demon would not know which token the Lunatic saw, which might cause issues on N2 when deciding who to kill.

Does the Lunatic learn that they are evil if they are turned by the Mezepheles?

All players learn if they change alignment, even the Lunatic.

Does the Demon learn what character the Lunatic Ojo targeted?

No, they are shown the player who the Lunatic Ojo functionally targeted, i.e. the player with that character.

What is the Demon shown when the Lunatic Ojo picks an out of play role?

Nothing.

The Lunatic says the Demon learns who they picked, and the Ojo says picking an out of play character is the ST's choice not the player's, so the Lunatic Ojo did not pick anyone.

If the Lunatic is Pit-Hagged into the Demon she already thinks she is, what is she told?

The new Demon is reinformed of her character, as it changed and she no longer has the Lunatic ability.

If the Lunatic is Pit-Hagged into another role, they are told their new role, but are they told that they are in fact good?

No, their role has changed, but not their alignment, and players should only be informed of their alignment when it changes.

The Lunatic is good but believes they are an evil Demon. If the Pit-Hag turns the Lunatic into a Demon, will the Lunatic learn, along with their new role, that they are actually good?

No, they do not learn their alignment because their alignment has not changed.

When the Lunatic is Pit-Hagged into a Demon, they only have to be told their new role. They were good and are still good, so their alignment has not changed. If it is a new player, it might be helpful for the ST to tell them their alignment, but for experienced players this is not necessary. If the Lunatic actually turned evil due to a Fang Gu jump then they would learn they are now evil.

In general, players only learn when their alignment changes, and if a player were to enquire about their alignment should be told something like "your alignment has not changed".

A similar scenario to the pithagged Lunatic is the Marionette who when catching a star pass is not informed they are evil because their alignment has not changed.

If the Pit-Hag turns a player into the Lunatic, does the ST tell that player that they are evil?

No. The Lunatic's ability is "You think you are a Demon, but you are not. The Demon knows who you are and who you choose at night.". With the Pit-Hag on the script it is very believable someone could be made a good Demon, and that is all that is required of the Lunatic, to believe they are a Demon of some kind.

The Pit-Hag changes a player into the Lunatic. Would it be valid to first wake them, tell them they are an Outsider of some type, put them to sleep and pretend to continue with the night order, then wake them telling them they were Fang Gu jumped?

No, their ability does not make them think that they are an Outsider.

What does the Demon learn if their Lunatic Po charges / Lunatic Zombuul does not wake?

Nothing.

The Demon learns who the Lunatic chooses, and if they do not choose anyone for whatever reason then they learn nothing.

Can you tell the Lunatic that they have been snake charmed?

No, because the Lunatic's ability is that they think that they are the Demon, not that they were the Demon. If they are told that they are the good Snake Charmer then they are no longer being deceived that they are the Demon.

What does the Demon learn when the Lunatic thinks that they are the Yaggababble?

Just who the Lunatic is.

The Demon learns who the Lunatic picks, and if the Lunatic does not or cannot pick anyone, the Demon learns nothing.

Can the Lunatic be told that another player is the Lunatic?

Yes, but this can lead to the ST controlling the kills:

  • the ST chooses a kill for the fake Lunatic and informs the Lunatic,
  • the Lunatic attacks the fake Lunatic's target to keep up the lie,
  • the Demon attacks the same target to keep up the lie.

The ST can do this if their group is cool with the idea or perhaps to ensure seeing the Lunatic token does not confirm someone as the Demon.

How to simulate the Lunatic to the Lunatic without dictating the kills:

  • have the Lunatic think that they are, for example, the Po
  • the actual Demon is the Pukka, and is shown to the Lunatic as their fake Lunatic (Demons never know what Demon their Lunatic thinks they are)
  • N1, the Pukka (actual Demon) picks player X
  • N2, the ST tells the Lunatic that their Lunatic (actual Demon) just tried to kill player X
  • and so on. Because the Pukka kills out of sync, the issue is solved.

Can the ST fake the Poppy Grower is in play and not show fake Minions to the Lunatic?

Yes.

The ST is already lying to the player that they are the Demon, so they can lie about them being affected by the Poppy Grower, even when they are not in the game.

Anything on the script that could happen or be told to the Demon can be simulated for the Lunatic:

  • fake Magician, by showing an extra "Minion"
  • fake King,
  • fake Marionette,
  • fake Exorcist, ...

The ST is also free to give the Lunatic correct info when these characters are really in play.

Does a drunk or poisoned Lunatic's pick(s) get shown to the Demon?

No. They are still deceived into thinking their ability is working, so they are woken to choose if they normally would be, but the Demon will not learn their choices.

Does the Lunatic have to think they are an evil Demon?

No, if it is believable that there is a troll Pit-Hag in the game, and someone becomes the Lunatic on a later night, a good Demon is reasonable. However, the starting Lunatic needs to think they are the evil Demon character because there is almost no way anything else could happen. It would need a skilled ST to convince the Lunatic that an Amnesiac ability put a good Demon in the bag.

Does the Demon learn the Lunatic in Teensyville?

Yes, that is a function of the Lunatic ability, and all character abilities function normally in a game with five or six players.

If the Lycanthrope is drunk or poisoned, does none of their ability take effect?

Correct, they cannot kill and other deaths are not prevented.

If the Lycanthrope self-kills are they the only death this night?

No, the dead Lycanthrope has no ability so they are unable to prevent other deaths tonight.

What happens when the Lycanthrope successfully kills a good player in an Al-Hadikhia game?

No one can die to the Al-Hadikhia regardless of their live/die choices but players can still be resurrected.

If the Lycanthrope chooses a good player and a Godfather chooses to use their ability, does the Godfather ability get wasted?

The Godfather does not choose when they use it, but the Godfather kill also does not go through when the Lycan picks a good player. This is unlike the Assassin, which kills despite the Lycan protection.

The Lycanthrope attacks a good player, then the Pit-Hag creates a new Demon. How many deaths can occur that night?

The Pit-Hag acts first in the night order so deaths are completely arbitrary which can include blocking the Lycanthrope kill.

If the Lycanthrope attacks a good player who does not die (sober Soldier / Tea Lady protection / Innkeeper protection / unspent Fool / ...) is it a no death night?

No, other players can still die tonight due to other characters‚Äô abilities.

The killing a good player and the no one else can die are directly linked, and if the first does not happen then the second does not activate.

If the Lycanthrope attacks the Mayor who bounces the kill, what happens?

The ST has a choice of who to bounce the kill to:

  • a good player who dies, meaning no further deaths that night;
  • a good player who cannot die, meaning other kills can happen that night,
  • an evil player, who cannot die since the source of the attack is still considered to be the Lycan, so other deaths can happen tonight.

Can the Lycanthrope kill the Lleech host, ending the game?

Yes, assuming the Lleech chose a good player as their host (the Lleech does occasionally pick Minions).

How does the Pukka interact with the Lycanthrope? If the Lycan prevents the death of a Pukka poisoned target, do they remain poisoned? Or, in other words, does a Pukka chosen target have to die in order to become healthy?

No, the Lycan-protected and Pukka-poisoned player becomes a healthy (and living) player.

The order of events would look something like this:

  • N1 - The Pukka poisons player A.
  • N2 - The Lycanthrope kills a good player and the Pukka chooses player B. Player B is poisoned and player A becomes healthy and does not die since the Lycanthrope ability worked successfully.

What is the Gambler jinx with the Lycanthrope?

If the Gambler gambles someone incorrectly and dies while there is an alive Lycan ability, they are the only player who can die that night, just like if the Lycan chose them.

  • the alignment of the Lycan's pick is irrelevant
  • no other deaths due to other abilities go through, which includes the Lycan's and the Demon's picks
  • whether the Lycan is drunk or poisoned is RAW irrelevant

If the Lycanthrope kills a good player, and the Demon picks the Lycanthrope, does only the good player die?

Yes.

What impact on the game would a mid game created Magician or Poppy Grower (Damsel / Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) have?

Almost certainly none. The Damsel gaining such an ability would not have any fun.

Can the Evil Twin be twinned with the Magician?

Yes. The Evil Twin would see the Demon token as the Magician's character... which would immediately expose the Magician.

Does a N1 Barista 1 have an effect on the Demon or a Minion when there is a Magician in play?

Yes, that player would not be shown the Magician. A Barista 1 Evil Twin paired with the Magician would see them as the Magician instead of the Demon, and cause a +1 to the Mathematician.

If the Magician neighbours the No Dashii, do they affect the Demon / Minion info stages?

No, they are poisoned.

How is the Magician run in a Legion game?

The Magician's vote counts as a good vote and causes an execution to pass if sufficient.

Each Legion must be woken up individually to be told their other Demon players in order to maintain the Magician illusion, so any time the Magician is on the script with Legion, all Legion players should wake separately to see their fellow "Legion" players so that Legion players cannot tell if the Magician is in play or not.

If the Mastermind or the Scarlet Woman thinks that the Magician is the Demon, does their ability trigger when the Magician is executed?

No.

While the Mastermind/SW player will think the Magician is the Demon, their ability does not register the Magician as the Demon, so it is not triggered on the Magician‚Äôs execution.

Can the Marionette be sat next to the Magician rather than the Demon?

No.

The Minions only think the Magician is the Demon, the Magician does not register as the Demon. However, a Magician sat next to the Demon can be shown to the Demon as the Marionette.

What is the Magician jinx with Lil' Monsta?

They follow the hate jinx rule: only one jinxed character can be in play.

Is the Magician's ability affected by the Vortox?

No.

How does the Magician work when there the Spy or the Widow are in play?

As per the jinx: "When the Spy/Widow sees the Grimoire, the Demon and Magician's character tokens are removed." The ST also removes any relevant reminder tokens as well so that it is not obvious despite the lack of character token.

Can the Imp starpass to the Magician?

No.

Do evil Townsfolk or Outsiders (Bounty Hunter / Mezepheles) or evil Travellers see the Magician?

No, only Minions or Demons.

How does the Magician work in a Poppy Grower game?

If the Magician is alive when the Poppy Grower dies then it affects the Minion/Demon info step exactly how it would have done N1.

If the Magician ability comes into play after N1, do Demons and Minions learn information on the player with the Magician ability?

In a Poppy Grower game they might, otherwise no.

The Minions and the Demon learn of the Magician during the info phase which happens N1. So unless the Poppy Grower was in play from the start of the game and delayed the info phase until after the Magician's creation, the evil team would not learn about the mid game Magician.

If the Philosopher drunks the Magician N1, does the actual Magician‚Äôs ability happen when the Philo dies? Does Demon and Minion info happen again midway through the game?

No, because by that time the deception has already failed. Similarly, a Pit-Hag creating a Magician mid game would not cause the Minions and Demon to redo their info steps.

Does the Demon immediately know who one of her Minions is if the Marionette and the Magician are in the same game? Can the Demon think the Magician is their Marionette?

When the Magician and the Marionette are in the game together, the Demon will learn one Minion as her Marionette and the rest as non-Marionette Minions. She will immediately figure out the Magician is in the game, but if the Magician is sat next to the Demon or the Recluse then the Demon can be told the Magician is her Marionette, so learning the Marionette does not immediately mean the Demon knows for sure who one of her Minions is.

In a one minion game, with the Marionette and the Magician in play, does the Demon just learn both players without learning one is the Marionette?

They would learn both as Minions, and learn the Marionette as the Marionette, but they would not know for sure if their Marionette was actually the Magician and the other Minion was a non-Marionette.

The Magician's ability is that the Demon thinks they are a Minion, and that can include a specific Minion if relevant similar to how the Lunatic can be lied to about different things in order to keep up the ruse that they are the Demon.

If the Magician was in the game and the Minion was not the Marionette, then, if the Magician was sat next to the Demon or the Recluse, the Demon could learn the Magician as the Marionette.

If the Marionette Artist asks if they are the Marionette, can the ST answer 'yes'?

Yes.

Could the Marionette believe that she is the Atheist?

Yes, though it might require an alternate setup to make that happen.

What is the Balloonist jinx with the Marionette?

If the Marionette thinks that they are the Balloonist, +1 Outsider was added.

If the Bounty Hunter is the Marionette, is a Townsfolk player still made evil?

No.

What happens when the Cannibal eats the Marionette?

The Cannibal is poisoned and is usually deceived that they have the ability the Marionette thought they had.

Can the Marionette Choirboy be woken up and told the Demon when there is no King in the game?

Yes, but getting that setup is tricky as the Choirboy requires the King and you do not know at setup that they will be the Marionette.

What happens if the Courtier picks the Marionette?

Nothing.

N1 the Marionette ability of thinking they are good and neighbouring the Demon has already happened. On other nights the ST still deceives a drunk Marionette that their ability is working, that is they think that they are a good character.

Can the Marionette Damsel be woken up and told that they became a Townsfolk when there is no Huntsman in the game?

Yes.

What happens if a player chooses the Marionette with the Hatter ability?

The ST informs that player that they are a good character and tells the Demon who their Marionette is.

After the Hatter dies, is the Marionette woken and given a choice?

Yes. This hard confirms to them that they are the Marionette, similar to if the Preacher picks them.

Who learns the Marionette in a Lil' Monsta game?

Anyone, except the Marionette (jinx), who babysits LM learns the Marionette.

What is the Marionette jinx with Lil' Monsta?

The Marionette neighbours a Minion. The Marionette is not woken to choose who takes the Lil' Monsta token.

Can the Lunatic be the Marionette?

ST choice.

The TPI consider 'yes, they can' and 'no, they cannot' to both be valid rulings, so the ST should pick their preference and inform their players which they run:

  1. The Marionette cannot think they are the Lunatic as the Lunatic thinks they are evil, which contradicts the Marionette thinking they are good, so the Lunatic cannot be the Marionette.
  2. The Marionette can think they are a good character that themselves thinks they are the Demon.

If the preference is 'no they cannot' and the Demon lands between the Lunatic and a Minion then, if there is no Recluse in the game, that would need a rerack. To prevent this from happening an alternative setup should be used, such as placing an extra Townsfolk token in the bag instead of the Lunatic, then after the tokens are distributed, deciding which of the Townsfolk players to make the Lunatic, informing that they are a Demon from the script and showing them the Townsfolk token that they received as one of their bluffs.

Does the Marionette ping the Mathematician every time they use the ability that they think they have?

No; the Marionette‚Äôs supposed good ability works abnormally due to their own ability, so does not register to the Mathematician.

Can the Marionette be shown a fake Nightwatchman ping?

General consensus is no, because deceiving them about that is not part of the Marionette's "think" ability.

Unlike for example deceiving the Lunatic that they were picked by the Exorcist, which is part of them thinking that they are the Demon.

Does the Preacher on N1 picking the Marionette block the Demon from learning about them?

No.

The Marionette ability happens before the Preacher picks on N1 so cannot stop the Marionette placement or prevent the Demon from knowing about the Marionette. The Marionette is woken as usual to be told that they have been preached.

What happens when the Preacher selects the Marionette?

The Marionette is woken and learns the Preacher chose them. They are not explicitly told that they are evil or the Marionette, but will probably be able to figure it out.

As they lose their ability that makes them "think they are a good character", the ST stops deceiving them: they are no longer woken if they previously believed that they had a Townsfolk ability that acted at night.

Can the Recluse next to the Demon be the actual Marionette?

Yes.

Can the Marionette in setup be placed next to the Recluse, and not the Demon?

Yes. And it is a N1 +1 to the Mathematician too.

Can the Marionette neighbour the Recluse registering as the Demon?

Yes. It is still best to inform the actual Demon of the Marionette, not the Recluse, otherwise that would out a player who does not even know that they are evil to a good player. This also tells the Demon that one of the Marionette's neighbours is the Recluse.

What are the restrictions on who can be the Marionette?

Anyone can be the Marionette except:

  • the Damsel, when the Huntsman is in play;
  • the King, when the Choirboy is in play.

The Marionette must neighbour the Demon, or the Recluse who is registering as the Demon.

If the Demon moves mid game (Snake Charmer / Barber / Pit-Hag / Fang Gu / Imp / Lil‚Äô Monsta / Matron / Hatter / ... ), does the Marionette stay where they are?

Yes, the Marionette does not move with the Demon, as neighbouring the Demon is a setup ability that has no effect later in the game.

The new Demon would, however, be told who the Marionette is.

Do the other Minions learn of the Marionette?

No.

During Minion info they are told one fewer Minion, from which they will deduce that the Marionette is in play. To find out who that is, they will need to talk to their Demon.

Does the Demon learn the Marionette in Teensyville games?

Yes, that is a function of the Marionette ability, and all character abilities function normally in a game with five or six players.

The Marionette is the only Minion the Demon will learn in a Teensyville, unless the Toymaker fabled is in play, as the Demon and Minion info steps are skipped.

Can the Marionette think that she is an Outsider?

Yes.

The restrictions on the Marionette at setup, namely that they are evil believing they are a good player and they are sat either next to the Demon or the Recluse registering as the Demon ... do they apply mid game for the purposes of the Barber / Pit-Hag / Engineer / Hatter / ...?

No. The new Marionette:

  • does not need to neighbour the Demon, or a player registering as the Demon
  • is allowed to be a good player

If the Engineer is responsible for the new Marionette then the ST can pick any of the existing Minions to swap.

What happens when a new Marionette is created mid game (Barber / Pit-Hag / Engineer / Hatter / ...)?

The ST:

  • informs the Demon of the new Marionette;
  • does not tell the new Mario anything about their alignment as it has not changed.

The player is not informed that they are the Marionette, instead the ST either shows the player:

  • the "you are" info token and any Townsfolk or Outsider token,
  • nothing, if they were previously were a Townsfolk or Outsider.

Effectively the player is now like the Drunk and the ST will now treat the Marionette as the character that they saw.

The starting Marionette believes that they are a good role. But if they swap character (Imp self-kills / Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) and so no longer have an ability that deceives them about their alignment, are they informed that they are evil?

RAW no, as players are only notified of their alignment when it changes. So the ST only informs them of their new character.

If they became a Demon and directly ask the ST what their alignment is, the ST can reply "you are evil" or "you have not been informed of an alignment change." For newer players who are confused it may be best to clarify that they are evil, whereas the second response could be given to more experienced players who know how the Marionette works.

Does a Marionette Townsfolk receive misinformation?

The Marionette is not actually a Townsfolk, and so is unaffected by the Vortox. The ST can treat them as if they were drunk or poisoned, but they are not. They can be given any information, good or bad, in order to deceive them in to thinking that they are the Townsfolk character that they saw.

In a 13+ player game, there are three Minions. If one Minion is going to be the Marionette, only two Minion tokens are put in the bag. If once the roles are given out both Minion tokens are drawn by the two players neighbouring the Demon, what can the ST do?

Options are:

  1. Change a player to a Minion,
  2. seat the Marionette next to the Reluse if there is one,
  3. scrap the Marionette from the game and instead change a good player into the remaining Minion (but remember to still respect character type counts),
  4. rerack.

One possible way to avoid this scenario:

  1. When preparing the bag the ST places two Minion tokens and no Demon token.
  2. Choose two adjacent players who drew good tokens to be the Demon and the Marionette.
  3. Give the Demon the character that they drew as one of their bluffs, to avoid giving them a free fourth bluff

Some players dislike this method as it amounts to the ST assigning characters rather than letting the players.

If an Outsider is made into the Marionette, which would make one less Outsider in the game than it is supposed to be, is it still a legal setup?

Yes. In this scenario the Marionette has acted like a soft -1 Outsider modifier.

If a dead player becomes the Marionette (Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) does the Demon still learn them?

No, the dead Marionette has no ability.

Do character checkers (Juggler / Gambler / Dreamer / Undertaker / Ravenkeeper / Harlot / ...) see the Marionette as the Marionette?

Yes, as this is their true character.

On a Mastermind day nobody is executed. What happens?

If no one is executed on a Mastermind day, the normal victory conditions kick back in, which usually means good wins.

But the game can continue if for example:

  • another Demon enters play
  • the Evil Twin is still alive

What happens in a game with the Mastermind when the Lleech's host is executed?

The Lleech does not die, but they no longer have any ability; that night they do not kill. The next day, if a good player is executed evil wins. Otherwise good wins.

If the Demon is executed and the following day the Apprentice Mastermind is exiled, does good win?

Yes.

On a Mastermind day after the Demon is killed, when either the Spy or the Recluse is executed, is the winner completely up to the ST?

Mechanically, the ST can make either team lose if either a Spy or Recluse is executed via misregistration. But the recommendation is not to have any misregistering on a Mastermind day; killing the Recluse would be an evil win, and killing the Spy would be a good win.

Fearmonger and Mastermind do not play well with the misregistration abilities because if the ST uses the misregistration abilities players will feel like the ST entirely decided which team won.

If the Demon is executed and dies in F3 with the Mastermind and one good player still alive, does the game continue into a F2 day?

Yes. The Mastermind's ability is to "play for 1 more day", and character abilities override normal game rules. A F2 day with Mastermind and a "dead" Zombuul is also a typical situation so the players will need to figure out what happened.

If there is a Mastermind ability in play and the Demon is executed ending the game, a Mastermind day triggers. If a new demon is created or some other mechanic would allow the game to otherwise continue after the Mastermind day has triggered, does the Mastermind day continue?

The Mastermind's ability is still in effect even though the game can now continue without it: If no one is executed the game would continue but if someone is executed that player loses

If, upon the execution of a Demon, causing there to be a ‚ÄòMastermind day‚Äô, another Demon comes into play, or another character that causes the game to continue comes into play, the game can continue beyond the ‚ÄòMastermind day‚Äô, however the Mastermind ability still functions upon an execution on said ‚ÄòMastermind day‚Äô.

If the Demon is executed, causing the Mastermind ability to function and cause a proceeding ‚ÄòMastermind day‚Äô, then another Demon comes into play, an execution will end the game, with the team of the player being executed losing.

An Evil Twin being brought into play would allow the evil team to win upon the execution of a good player on a ‚ÄòMastermind day‚Äô, however if an evil player were executed (or no execution occurred) on said ‚ÄòMastermind day‚Äô then the game would continue with the Evil Twin ability needing to be resolved

Does the Mastermind trigger after the Zombuul dies for a second time?

Yes. This is the only time the MM does trigger with the Zombuul.

On a Mastermind day, if the Politician was nominated and determined to have done enough to flip, would evil win or would good win? i.e. does the Politician alignment change happen after the Mastermind had resolved the game?

The Politician flips after the game ends, so evil wins.

If the Demon is killed by another way than execution, such as to the Gunslinger, the Mastermind cannot use its ability, right?

Correct.

If the Al-Hadikhia chooses the Soldier, the sober Sailor, and the Tea Lady protected player, and they all choose death, would that register as a six for the Mathematician?

It registers as a one.

The Mathematician counts the number of abilities that work abnormally, not how many times they malfunctioned.

Does the Assassin bypassing another character's protection (Fool / Sailor / Tea Lady / Innkeeper / ...) give a +1 to the Mathematician?

Yes, the Assassin's ability is causing another player's protection ability to work abnormally.

The drunk or poisoned (not self-poisoned) Cannibal uses an info gathering ability during the day, receiving false info. After that day's execution, the Cannibal gains a new protection ability that she uses that night on another player who is attacked and dies. One player with two abilities that malfunctioned. How many times is the Mathematician pinged?

Once, it is the Cannibal ability that has malfunctioned.

Does the Cannibal being poisoned after an evil player (Minion / Demon / evil turned Townsfolk / ...) is executed ping the Mathematician?

No, as it is the Cannibal's own ability that is poisoning them. If another character is poisoning them then the Mathematician would be pinged.

The Cannibal eats the Drunk. Does that count to the Mathematician?

No, the Cannibal is working as intended.

Does the drunk / poisoned Cult Leader that could have changed alignments ping the Mathematician?

If both of the droisoned Cult Leader's neighbours are the opposite alignment to the CL's, then the Mathematician is pinged. If one neighbour is good and the other evil, then although they could technically ping the Mathematician, they probably should not.

The Exorcist picks the Demon. Is this +1 for the Mathematician?

If the Demon should be waking up to use their ability, and they are not because of the Exorcist, then the Demon ability has malfunctioned and it counts.

Does the Exorcist preventing the Demon from waking up lead to a +1 for the Mathematician?

Yes, the Demon's ability is working abnormally due to the Exorcist.

If the Barista 1 Townsfolk targeting the unpicked Goon is not made drunk ... does this register to the Mathematician?

Yes. The Goon failing to drunk the first player to pick her means that her ability worked abnormally.

If the Juggler does not juggle on the first day and the ST decides not to show a number, is the Mathematician pinged?

No, since the Juggler not receiving a number is not due to another character ability.

If the Juggler juggles but the next night she is turned by the Pit-Hag, she does not get her info. Does this register to the Mathematician?

No. Her ability did not function abnormally at any point; which ability she had simply changed.

If the Lunatic believes she is a multi-kill Demon when the Demon is a single kill Demon (or vice versa), would the Mathematician inherently be pinged every night?

Yes.

The Lunatic's jinx with the Mathematician is that the Mathematician learns if the Lunatic attacks a different player(s) than the real Demon attacks, and this would include attacking different numbers of players

If either the Lunatic or the Demon is the Po that charges while the other attacks, does that alert the Mathematician?

Yes.

The Lunatic's jinx with the Mathematician is that the Mathematician learns if the Lunatic attacks a different player(s) than the real Demon attacks, and attacking no one is different to attacking someone.

What is the interaction between the Mathematician and the Magician? Does the Mathematician pick up on the Demons' and Minions' abilities "not working properly", as it does whenever the Spy or the Recluse interacts with a character?

No, because the Mathematician counts how many abilities malfunctioned, and Demon and Minion info is not happening due to their character abilities, rather due to their character type and game rules.

Although, interestingly, in a game with the Poppy Grower and the Magician, the Poppy Grower dying and giving the Demon and Minions their info is considered part of the Poppy Grower ability, meaning that the Mathematician would detect if the Magician ability caused the Demon and Minions to learn an extra player from the Poppy Grower ability.

If the Ojo picks a character that is out of play, would that trigger the Mathematician's number?

No. The consequences are part of her own ability, unless the character actually was in play but misregistered (Spy / Recluse) as an out of play character.

If the Philosopher picks an ability while poisoned, do they register a single abnormality to the Mathematician and then never again, or do they register an abnormality each time they think they use their ability and it functions improperly?

They would ping the Mathematician every time they attempted to use the ability they think they gained and it produces a wrong result, because the ST is only able to do that while the Philosopher is continuously drunk or poisoned, so it is still due to another character's ability that such deception is even possible.

After the Pit-Hag creates a Demon and deaths are arbitrary, is the Demon's kill being blocked a +1 to the Mathematician?

Yes.

How do Pit-Hag arbitrary deaths register to the Mathematician?

The Pit-Hag‚Äôs arbitrary death ability allows the ST to kill any player and protect any player from death. So if the Demon's target does not die due to the PH allowing the ST to protect that player, that is +1 to the Mathematician (place an abnormal token on the Demon). If the ST uses the Pit-Hag‚Äôs ability to kill additional players, then that is the PH's ability functioning normally, so that is not a +1 to the Mathematician.

Does the Pit-Hag picking a character that is in play register to the Mathematician?

No, because their ability is working normally according to their own ability text. Besides, even if this was classified as a malfunction, it is due to their own ability, and not another character's ability.

The ST Poisoner, made by the Plague Doctor dying, poisons a Townsfolk whose ability then malfunctions. Does it ping the Mathematician?

Yes. Even though the ST is not a player, a player has an ability malfunctioning, and it was technically caused by the Plague Doctor player.

Do Minions targeted by the Preacher register to the Mathematician?

The Mathematician is only pinged if the Minion would have done something or woken to use their ability that night.

For example after preaching:

  • the Baron never wakes for any reason: no pings, there is nothing to work abnormally;
  • the Poisoner no longer wakes up each night to poison someone: pings the Mathematician every night they are alive and preached;
  • the Evil Twin, when the twin info has already gone out, and the good twin is not executed: no ping tonight;
  • the Evil Twin is not woken to be informed of the good twin's new character: ping for the Mathematician tonight;
  • the evil team does not win after the good twin is executed: ping for the Mathematician tonight.

Does a poisoned Snake Charmer choosing the Demon cause a Mathematician ping?

Depends on the source of the poisoning:

  • a self-poisoning SC means no ping, since the malfunction is not due to another character‚Äôs ability
