  • another character poisoning the SC is a Mathematician ping

Does the self poisoning Widow trigger the Mathematician?

No, the Mathematician only detects abnormalities due to other players' abilities.

If a new Mathematician is created (Pit-Hag / Barber / ...) would they read the "abnormal" tokens placed the previous day, or does the new ability instance mean they only "see" malfunctionings that happen after they entered play?

They would see all abnormalities from the day.

Does the Mathematician detect players affected by drunking / poisoning / misregistration?

Only if the player's ability works differently to what their ability states.

The Mathematician is pinged when, for example:

  • the Grandmother sees the Spy who misregistered as a good role,
  • the Recluse misregistering as a Minion poisons the Cannibal,
  • the Recluse misregisters as evil to the Chef,
  • the poisoned Slayer targets the Demon who does not die,
  • the drunk Fisherman receives bad advice,
  • the poisoned Soldier dies to the Demon's attack,
  • the poisoned, but not self-poisoned, Snake Charmer chooses the Demon,
  • the Poisoner fails to poison the Goon who drunks them instead.

If a player still gets true info despite drunking / poisoning / misregistration, then their ability has functioned exactly as it should and the Mathematician is not pinged:

  • the poisoned Artist receives a correct answer,
  • the Empath sat between the Recluse misregistering as evil and the Spy registering as a Townsfolk correctly received a one.

The Mathematician is not pinged if a drunked / poisoned mechanical ability is not used, or does nothing which is the expected result:

  • the drunk Slayer targets a non-Demon,
  • the target of the drunk Devil's Advocate protection is executed.

Does the Dreamer seeing a good role and a Minion role when checking a Legion player ping the Mathematician?

Yes. The Dreamer is not seeing the correct character, due to another character‚Äôs ability.

Does the No Dashii poisoned Sailor failing to drunk someone ping the Mathematician?

Yes.

While the Mathematician does not necessarily detect if a player is drunk or poisoned, she does detect any players whose abilities malfunction since the previous dawn due to those states.

If a role that acts during the day (Slayer / Fisherman / ...) is poisoned at night, when is the Mathematician pinged?

Not on the night of the poisoning but the following night and only if the player attempted to use their ability during the day and it worked abnormally.

Do Djinn jinxes register as abnormalities to the Mathematician? For example:
  • the Pit-Hag creating the Damsel and then the ST picking who to be the Damsel;
  • the Spy not seeing the Grimoire due to the Poppy Grower; ...

There is no official stance or concensus on Djinn jinxes and the Mathematician. One opinion is that those are rules for how the characters work together so are not abnormalities.

Does the Demon's target being protected ping the Mathematician?

Yes, the Demon's ability worked abnormally due to another character's ability, so that counts for the Mathematician. This includes when the ST picks the kill for the Demon (Yaggababble / Legion / Lil' Monsta / Ojo / ...).

What happens when the evil Mayor (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter) convinces the town to not execute in final three?

Evil wins.

Can the Mayor win still trigger after the Gangster kills one of their living neighbours?

Yes, a Gangster kill is not an execution.

Does the Zombuul register as dead to the Mayor?

Yes, meaning that if only the registering as dead Zombuul, the Mayor and one other player are left alive, then the Mayor win cannot happen as from the Mayor's perspective there are only two left alive.

In order to trigger the Mayor win when the Zombuul is registering as dead, the town must not execute when the Mayor and two other players are left alive.

If the Demon kills the Mayor, can the Mayor bounce kill the sober Soldier?

No, as the source of the bounced kill is still considered to be the Demon, not the Mayor, so the Soldier is safe.

Who wins in final three with the Mayor and the Vortox with no executions?

The good team. Both abilities would trigger and since it is a tie between two character abilities good would win.

Can the protected Mayor (Tea Lady / Monk / Innkeeper) still bounce an attempted kill?

No. The Mayor's ability is "if you die". If they are protected, they cannot die so there can be no bounce.

If the Spirit of Ivory is in play and there is already an extra evil, what happens when a good player says the Mezepheles word?

The good player does not turn evil and, strictly applying the rules, the Mez loses their ability.

Can a good Mezepheles say the word and turn themselves evil?

Yes, assuming they are the first good player to say the word.

Does the Preacher picking the Mezepheles turn the evil turned player good?

No, the turned player stays evil. But if the Mez is preached on the same night when a player would turn evil, then they have no ability and no one turns.

Could the Recluse register as evil when they say the Mezepheles word, so not turn evil?

Yes, then it would be the next good player that says the word that turns evil that night.

Could the Spy register as good when they say the Mezepheles word, triggering the Mez's ability, so using it up?

Yes, if they were feeling mean.

What happens if a good player says the Mezepheles‚Äôs secret word during N1, after the Mez‚Äôs point in the night order where they learn the word but before D1 starts?

The good player turns on N2.

If the Mezepheles gets someone to say the word but they die by execution, does the person turn?

No, because the Mezepheles' ability can no longer work in death. Note if the target instead is dead, they can still turn.

Does the drunk or poisoned Mezepheles still turn a good player evil at night?

If they are drunk at their spot in the night order, no. If they were drunk when the word was said but sober at their place in the night order, yes.

Can the Mezepheles turn the Magician evil?

Yes. While the Mezepheles player thinks that the Magician player is the Demon, their Mezepheles ability registers the Magician as good, and therefore would turn them that night if they say the word.

Does a mid game Minstrel created (Damsel / Pit-Hag / Barber / Philosopher / ...) the night after a Minion execution immediately drunk everybody?

No, the Minstrel ability must be in play when the Minion "dies by execution" (present tense), so coming into play after the fact has no effect.

If the public Goblin is executed while the Minstrel is in play, does the Minstrel immediately activate and block the Goblin's wincon?

No, the Goblin win is triggered before the Minstrel can drunk them.

If it is a Minstrel day with the alive Scarlet Woman does the game end if the Demon is executed?

Yes.

Does the Minstrel drunking also affect dead players for the purposes of situations like Vigor-killed Minions, the Plague Doctor ability, etc?

The Minstel's ability reads "all other players (except Travellers)", so yes, dead players are still players. As per the ability text the only ones not hit are Travellers and the Minstrel themselves. Additionally, any Minion ability gained by the ST through the PD is not turned off as the ST is not a player.

Can the Demon still Barber swap a Monk protected player?

Yes. Changing characters is not considered a harmful effect, and even if it was, the character changing is happening because of the Barber‚Äôs ability, not the Demon's.

Does a Vigormortis killed Minion lose their ability for the night if they are protected by the Monk?

No; having an ability is not considered a harmful effect.

If a dead Monk-protected player is targeted by the Al-Hadikhia, can they be resurrected if they chose live?

Yes, living and resurrections are not considered harmful.

Does the Monk protected, No Dashii poisoned, Minstrel proc after a Minion is executed?

The Monk is not protecting the Minstrel when the Minion dies since the Monk only works during the night. So the No Dashii poisoned Minstrel does not proc.

Is the Monk protected player and the Soldier safe at night from the Minion holding Lil' Monsta?

Yes, so they cannot

  • be turned evil by the Mezepheles;
  • die to the Godfather;
  • be poisoned by the Poisoner or the Widow;
  • be made mad by the Cerenovus or the Harpy.

However they can:

  • be transformed by the Pit-Hag as swapping character is not considered a harmful effect.

Does the Monk ability protect from positive Demon effects: regurgitating, resurrecting, etc.

No, it specifically protects from harmful effects. Regurgitation and resurrection are not considered to be harmful.

Is a Monk protected Minion blocked from becoming the Imp when the Imp self-kills?

No, becoming the Demon is not consider a harmful effect.

The Pukka picks the Moonchild N1. The Moonchild is executed D1 and, while poisoned, picks a good player. N2 the Pukka picks another player so the dead Moonchild is now healthy at their their turn in the night order. Does the good player die N2?

Yes. As soon as a good player is picked by the Moonchild, they are marked to die, regardless of the status of the Moonchild. As long as the Moonchild is sober and healthy at their turn in the night order, the scheduled death happens.

When does the Moonchild need to be drunk or poisoned for their ability to fail?

They would need to be drunk or poisoned at the time in the night order when their ability is resolved, potentially killing someone.

If the Moonchild dies and chooses the Demon who is the same night snake charmered, does the former Demon now poisoned Snake Charmer die?

No. The ex Demon was evil at the time of the Moonchild pick, so no kill was "scheduled" to hit her that night. The Moonchild ability, at their turn in the night order, simply ignores her.

What happens if the Moonchild picks a player that later flips alignment (Goon due to their own ability / Mezepheles turned / ...) before the Moonchild's turn in the night order?

If the player is good at the time of the Moonchild's pick then they are marked with the Moonchild's reminder token, and die at the Moonchild's spot in the night order, regardless of whether they have become evil.

If the player was evil at the time of the pick and became good at night, such as when the Goon is flipped, then they do not die.

Can the Mutant be executed for a madness break after they are dead?

No, the dead Mutant has no ability. Generally characters have no abilities when dead unless otherwise specified.

This means:

  • they are free to claim Mutant now that they are dead,
  • they can no longer be punished if they had claimed to be an Outsider while alive and died from another cause.

Can the ST execute the drunk or poisoned Mutant for breaking madness?

No, the Mutant ability to self execute would not work if they are drunk or poisoned.

What happens if the Philosopher with the Mutant ability claims to be the Philo-Mutant?

Madness is always contextual, but if a player is claiming to be the Philosopher who chose the Mutant ability they are not claiming to be the Mutant, or an Outsider... unless this becomes a group's code for actually being the Mutant... which reiterates the point, that madness is entirely contextual.

Is a Townsfolk poisoned by the No Dashii still poisoned after they die?

Yes. The No Dashii does not care about living or dead status, only that the player is a Townsfolk. So any while dead or on death triggered ability will be poisoned. If the player ceases to be a Townsfolk then the poisoning must move.

Does the No Dashii still poison a neighbouring Townsfolk if they are evil (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter)?

Yes, their ability does not care about alignment.

If a No Dashii poisoned Townsfolk gets protected by the Monk they become unpoisoned. Does the next neighbour then get poisoned?

No. The No Dashii poison does not skip over safe players, it only skips over non-Townsfolk. So just the one Townsfolk on the other side of the No Dashii would be poisoned.

Does the No Dashii poisoning move if one of her Townsfolk neighbours becomes a non-Townsfolk, due to the Pit-Hag for example?

Yes. It also moves if someone closer than their current Townsfolk neighbour becomes a Townsfolk. It is constantly checking for who is the closest Townsfolk to the No Dashii's left and right, and poisoning those two players.

Does the Ojo picking the character that the Philosopher chose the ability of, cause the Philo to die?

No.

If the Ojo targets the Village Idiot, do they all die or just one?

Whenever there are multiples of a role in play, the Ojo kills one instance of them and it is the ST's choice.

What happens when the Ojo picks the Soldier?

Nothing. The Soldier is targeted but cannot die so there are no Ojo deaths that night.

If the Ojo picks an out of play role, are kills arbitary, meaning there can be two kills, especially if there are multi-kill demons on the script?

Sort of. The ST can choose any number of people to die to the Ojo, with or without a multi-kill Demon on the script, but deaths are not arbitrary so the ST cannot save people who die from other abilities. There can be mulitple kills or none but one kill is still the recommended number most of the time.

Can the ST choose to sink a missed Ojo kill?

Yes.

If a character has died and in the night the Ojo names them, does the ST kill them again or kill someone else? Is there a rule or is it just up to the ST because is not that character technically in play?

The character is in play, so it would target the dead player and there would be no death from the Ojo that night.

What are the ST's options if the Ojo targets the Recluse?

The ST has several options:

  • If the Recluse registers as the Recluse then the Recluse dies.
  • If the Recluse is drunk or poisoned at the time then they have no choice but to register as the Recluse.
  • If the Recluse registers as anything else then there is no Recluse in play as far as the Ojo is concerned and so the ST chooses kills.

The Organ Grinder is nominated but does not vote on herself, so the votes do not count. Does this mean that any dead vote that was used is not spent?

No, any ghost votes were still used and are removed at the end of the day.

The ST gains the Organ Grinder ability via the Plague Doctor in a non-Atheist game. As the ST cannot vote, does this mean that the good team cannot lose by executing the ST?

Yes.

In an Organ Grinder game, where the OG is alive, healthy and sober, when exactly are the ghost votes taken away?

Ghost votes are removed at the end of the day, so after all nominations and votes have happened, not after every vote as it is typically conducted. This is so that players cannot tell where ghost votes were used. It is the players' responsibility not to vote twice until then.

What is the reasoning for the Organ Grinder/Minstrel and Organ Grinder/Preacher jinxes?

Those abilities do not play well together. It is a hard confirmed Minstrel day after a Minion is executed if there is no death at night and then no need to close your eyes for the vote. It is basically hard confirmed that the Preacher picked the Organ Grinder if one day there is no need to close your eyes when previously you had to, or if you started off not needing to and then suddenly you do because the Preacher died.

Abilities are not meant to be that hard confirmable most of the time. It is unbalanced to the point of broken so they are simply not allowed to be in play together.

Does the Organ Grinder affect exile votes?

No, exile "votes" are not votes. Ôªø

What happens to the Philosopher Cannibal when the philo-drunk Cannibal is executed?

Nothing.

The Philosopher has the Cannibal ability so they eat the Cannibal, gaining the Cannibal ability. After the next execution, the Philosopher Cannibal gains a new ability.

If the dead Philosopher who has used their ability is resurrected, what happens?

They are treated as a new instance of the Philosopher, with an unused Philosopher ability, and do not maintain any other previously gained ability.

If the Philo died while they had an "even if dead" ability, then that ability was maintained while they were dead, then lost upon resurrection. Otherwise, any gained ability was lost when they died.

Does the Philosopher drunk the role or the player?

The role. If the player becomes another role (Pit-Hag / Barber swap / ...) then they become sober.

If the sober and healthy Philosopher chooses an info gathering Townsfolk ability and is later drunked or poisoned the same night, what happens?

The Philosopher's once per game ability is used up. As they act before any poisoning and drunking roles they succeed in gaining the Townsfolk ability. While they are sober and healthy the respective Townsfolk is drunked. When they become drunked or poisoned, the respective Townsfolk is temporarily sober and their ability functions normally tonight.

If the Philosopher had acted on later night while drunk or poisoned then they would not have gained the ability, and the ST would lie to them for as long as they were drunk or poisoned.

The Philosopher chooses an out of play role. Later the Pit-Hag creates this role. Does the player with the new role come into the game already drunk?

Yes, the drunking is a constant check for if the character is in play.

If the Philosopher chooses Snake Charmer and becomes the Demon does the actual Snake Charmer becomes sober?

Yes, they are immediately sober as the Philosopher who was drunking them is no longer in play. Additionally the former Demon is now the self-poisoned Philosopher.

Could the Recluse not register as the Recluse so avoiding drunking by the Philosopher so that both the Recluse and the Philo-Recluse can both be working?

Yes.

Can the Philosopher pick Philosopher and gain the ability of the Philosopher, turning them into the 'Philo-Philo', effectively doing nothing other than creating a paradox on whether or not they get Philo-drunk?

Yes, but that just results in a self drunking Philo. Droisoning paradoxes are mostly resolved as "everyone involved is droisoned". The ST could check in on the player in the morning and make sure they wanted to do that instead of trying to save their ability because they might have misunderstood the Philosopher.

If the Philosopher Poppy Grower is poisoned N1 what happens?

That depends on the source of the poisoning, as the Philo goes before roles like the Poisoner that choose. If the Poisoner chose the Philo it would not stop their ability, but the No Dashii would.

What happens when the Philosopher tries to gain the ability of a character that is in a hate jinx with another already in play character?

The ST should shake their head no, show the Philosopher the in play role that the ability is hard jinxed with and put them back to sleep.

The ability is not gained and the Philosopher's once per game ability is now spent, but the trade off is they have learnt an in play role. For example, attempting to gain the Engineer role when Legion is in play will alert the Philosopher to it being a Legion game.

If the Philosopher dies before the character they chose does, does the Philo-drunkeness go away?

Yes.

The poisoned Philosopher picks an each night role. Do they ping the Chambermaid for each night that they wake up?

Yes, they are waking for their own ability.

The Philosopher is poisoned or drunked on the night they use their ability. They become healthy the next night. Do they have the ability they chose by then?

If the Philosopher is drunk or poisoned at the time they try to gain an ability, they fail to gain the ability and are a spent Philosopher with no ability. For as long as they remain drunk or poisoned, the ST should deceive them that they gained the ability by giving them arbitrary information when they would expect it. If they chose a mechanical ability, it will not work at all. But once they are sober and healthy again, the ST must stop the deception by treating them as a spent Philosopher that does not wake.

What happens when the Philosopher chooses Lunatic?

The Lunatic is drunked but from their point of view there is no difference:

  • they still believe that they are the Demon,
  • the ST still takes their choices,
  • they can still fake Marionette/Lunatic/King/Exorcist info.

The Demon:

  • learns the Philo as their Lunatic,
  • learns the Philo's picks for as long as the Philo is alive, sober and healthy,
  • has no idea who the Lunatic chose.

The Philosopher:

  • gets to guide the Demon‚Äôs attacks,
  • may cause the Lunatic to realise who they are due to their picks not dying.

If the Philosopher Lunatic ever becomes poisoned or drunk then the Lunatic will sober and the Demon will see the Lunatic's picks, not the Philo Lunatic's.

If the Philosopher was drunk or poisoned at the time they chose Lunatic then:

  • they lose their once per game ability and do not gain the Lunatic ability;
  • the Demon follows the Lunatic's picks as usual;
  • for as long as the Philo is drunk the ST can deceive them into thinking that they did gain the Lunatic ability (showing them a Demon token, taking their choices, ...) but once they become sober the deception must end.

Can the Pit-Hag create the Atheist?

Yes, and the good team wins if the Storyteller is executed. But the ST can now use their new game-breaking rules to do anything including turn the Atheist into any other character if they do not want to deal with it.

Can the Pit-Hag make someone the Barber, then someone else the Barber after the first one gets Fang Gu jumped?

If the Barber becomes the Fang Gu, then there is no Barber in play and it is valid for the Pit-Hag to make a new one.

Could the Pit-Hag turn the previous day's executee into the Barber or the Hatter and have their ability trigger?

No. The Barber and the Hatter only trigger if they die, not if they are dead. So if someone turned into Hatter or Barber after death, it does not trigger. Where abilities say 'when you die' or 'if you died' their triggers are on death.

Can the Pit-Hag create the Damsel?

Yes, but as per the Jinx the ST chooses who becomes the Damsel.

All Minions, including the Pit-Hag, learn immediately the Damsel is in play if the Damsel player is alive. If an evil Damsel is created, the evil team loses if a Minion guesses them.

If the Damsel comes into play after previously being in play, incorrectly guessed and removed, then the Minions get a fresh Damsel guess.

Can the Pit-Hag create the characters that the Drunk and the Marionette believe themselves to be?

Yes, they are out of play.

If the Pit-Hag changes somebody into the Drunk does the ST tell her that she got changed into a role?

The Drunk ability reads "You think you are a Townsfolk but you are not", so the ST's options are:

  1. tell her nothing, if she already thinks she is a Townsfolk, because she sees a Townsfolk token,
  2. change her into a different Townsfolk, despite the fact that she is the Drunk.

The Pit-Hag turns a good player into the Marionette. What does that player learn?

The Marionette has to think that she is a good character, so if a Townsfolk or Outsider is changed into the Marionette, the ST has several options:

  1. tell the now-Marionette nothing, as she already believes that she is a good character
  2. tell the now-Marionette that she is the character she already thought she was
  3. tell the now-Marionette that she is a different good character than what she previously believed

The first option is the most common, essentially it turns a player into a Drunk, except the Demon also knows who she is. But the other two options are viable depending on the game state.

The ST has a similiar decision if someone is made into the Drunk, except that they can only believe they are a Townsfolk, not an Outsider.

What happens if a good player is Pit-Hagged into an Evil Twin?

There is now a good player whose character is the Evil Twin. This new ability of hers causes her to be paired with an evil player and they learn who each other are:

  • the good-aligned twin learns what character the evil player is,
  • the evil-aligned twin learns the good player is the Evil Twin.

While both twins are alive, good cannot win., and if the good-aligned Evil Twin is executed, then evil wins.

The most obvious choice for the evil player would be the Pit-Hag, but the Demon could be chosen or a dead player if the game is almost at the end and good do not have enough time to execute two people.

The Gambler gambles wrong. Later that night the Pit-Hag creates a Demon. Can the Gambler survive because deaths are arbitary?

No.

The Gambler goes before PH in the night order and would be already dead by the time the Pit-Hag acts. With the PH ability, the ST can only prevent subsequent deaths or cause new ones; they cannot resurrect the dead.

Can the Pit-Hag create the character that the Philosopher picks the ability of?

Yes, they are out of play.

The Philosopher only gained the ability, they did not become the chosen role, so the Pit-Hag can successfully create the character.

What happens if the Pit-Hag tries to create the evil Politician? Does it just fail, or do they learn they cannot do this and must choose again?

The ST could remind the PH of the jinx if it is a player they know is evil or they could choose to fail it otherwise.

If the Pit-Hag creates a Snitch, do the Minions immediately get extra bluffs?

Not immediately, after kills and droisoning roles. Any starting info roles that enter the game on nights other than the first activate after kills and droisoning.

Could the Spy or the Recluse misregister as another role so appear to be out of play so allowing a Pit-Hag to create another?

Yes.

Can the ST kill the Zombuul twice when there is a Pit-Hag Demon change?

Yes.

If the Pit-Hag creates a Demon but then loses their ability can an arbitrary deaths night still occur?

Yes. As soon as the Pit-Hag creates a Demon arbitrary deaths are global and cannot be removed.

This covers:

  • the Vigormortis changing character causing the Pit-Hag to lose their ability
  • the Alchemist Assassin, whose ability cannot be blocked, killing the Pit-Hag
  • the Pit-Hag changing themselves to a Demon

If the Pit-Hag changes the Demon, is the Demon still asked to make a choice as to who to kill?

ST choice. They do not have to, but they can.

After the Pit-Hag creates a Demon and deaths are arbitrary, can the ST allow the Demon's kill to go through?

Yes.

If the Pit-Hag changes another Minion to the Witch, then because the Witch comes before the Pit-Hag in the night order, does the new Witch wait until the following night to use their ability?

Yes.

By the official strict night order ruling, the Witch must wait. Some STs run it so that the Witch and the Cerenovus should get to act even if they were created that night, and so long as the ST is consistent and sticks to the spirit of the night order, it is fine. Ôªø

When do arbitary kills due to the Pit-Hag happen in the night order?

The arbitrary deaths happen from during the Pit-Hag's turn in the night up to dawn.

When the Pit-Hag makes deaths arbitary, can the ST kill off players that are protected by the Innkeeper or the Lycanthrope?

Yes, if the Innkeeper / Lycanthrope is killed first. Deaths may be arbitary, but protection still works. The Lycan's target can also be saved, as they pick after the PH acts.

Only one jinxed role can be in play so what happens if the Pit-Hag attempts to make a character that is hard jinxed by a currently in play character? (e.g. trying to create the Spy/Widow while the Heretic is in play)

The Pit-Hag attempting to make a character that is hard jinxed with an in play character would simply fail in the same way it would if the character was already in play. The Pit-Hag is not informed of the failure. But if they tried to create a Heretic, the ST should probably shake their head no, point at the jinx area of the character sheet, and wait for a valid choice, because the PH has tried to make an invalid choice by their own character's rules.

If the Pit-Hag turns the Demon into a non-Demon, what happens?

If there is no living Demon, then barring some other effect that would prolong the game (Evil Twin), good would immediately win because "no living Demons" is good's win condition.

Can the Pit-Hag turn a dead player? Is that not a waste of their ability?

They can and there are reasons for doing so:

  • to turn an alive player into that role requires it being out of play first, such as removing a dead Assassin allows a new Assassin the next night;
  • they could be possibly revived or picked by another player that night;
  • turning someone into the Politician still allows them to turn;
  • turning someone into the Drunk when they expect to be Professor revived, can be awesome to cause confusion.

Are the Pit-Hag's transformations reverted on their death?

No.

Can the Pixie created mid game be shown a Townsfolk turned evil (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter / Cult Leader / ...)?

Yes; the only requirement for the Pixie is that they are shown an in play Townsfolk, who can be good or evil.

After a player dies, could the drunk or poisoned Pixie believe that they gained their ability?

Yes, but if they ever become sober and healthy then they must be treated normally.

If they believed that they gained an ability that wakes at night, they might become suspicious when they are no longer woken. So it might be best to only do this when the poisoning or drunking is permanent or long-lasting, for example when the Pixie is in fact the Drunk.

If the Pixie is shown the Village Idiot, does only one of the VIs need to die in order to turn the Pixie?

During setup the ST will have marked one of the VIs with the Pixie reminder token - this is the VI that needs to die in order to turn the Pixie. The marked VI could the sober one or the drunk one, if there is one.

Could the Pixie get their ability just before being killed if their marked player dies during the same selection of a multi-kill Demon (Al-Hadikhia / Po / Shabaloth)?

She could. The order of the deaths would matter: if the marked player dies before the Pixie then she can gain her ability.

For example, if the Ravenkeeper and the Pixie-Ravenkeeper both died in that order on the same night, then both could get their info.

If the Pixie is created late enough that there are no other Townsfolk alive, do they learn a dead in play Townsfolk and just never get the ability?

The Pixie created mid game can be shown a dead in play Townsfolk and will likely never get their ability.

A late game Pixie is essentially just confirming an in play Townsfolk and should probably not be trying to gain their ability nor likely can they.

Can the Pixie learn themselves?

Yes.

If no other player is a Townsfolk, does a Pixie just learn themselves?

Yes.

If the Gambler dies to their own gamble, does the Pixie mad about the Gambler get to use that ability that night?

No, it is now past the Gambler's turn in the night order, as their death concludes their turn, so the Pixie-Gambler will act the next night instead.

Would the Pixie Artist be told "you do not have this ability" if they failed madness or the Artist did not die?

Yes.

If the Pixie is made Cerenovus-mad about another character, does it break her initial Pixie madness?

Generally, yes. If they are not Cere mad on a later day, they may still be able to bring it back around though. They can say "I was Cere mad yesterday, I am still the (madness target)".

The Slayer is killed by the Psychopath, and the Pixie-Slayer, if they had been mad enough, would immediately get the Slayer ability and be able to shoot the Demon, correct?

Yes.

If the Pixie is drunk or poisoned at the moment their target dies, but is then sober and healthy that night, do they gain the ability?

No, a droisoned Pixie cannot gain an ability. For as long as they are droisoned the ST can make them think they did though.

What would happen if a character known to the Pixie becomes a different role, like a Farmer?

That player still needs to die and the Pixie still needs to be mad as the character they were shown, and will receive the ability shown if sufficiently mad.

How does a Pixie who is N1 poisoned or drunk work?

The Pixie still gains the ability they see if they are mad as that role, after the player marked with the Pixie mad token dies.

They will likely be shown an out of play role, and an arbitrary player is marked, but probably best it is not the Demon. As long as the Pixie is mad about the shown role and the marked player dies, they still gain the role they saw.

What happens when the Pixie is affected by the Spy misregistering?

The Spy is the marked player and they must die. If the Pixie is sufficiently mad about being the role that they saw, they will gain the ability. Note:

  • The Spy could have misregistered as an in play role
  • The Spy registering as another character when executed makes no difference to the ability that the Pixie gains

What happens if the Townsfolk the Pixie is mad about goes out of play (Pit-Hag)?

Nothing. When that player dies, if the Pixie was mad they will get the original ability regardless of their new ability.

What happens if the Plague Doctor dies multiple times?

The ST gains multiple abilities. If all abilities are in play they can get an in play ability. That can happen if the PD is Barber swapped to a living player or a new one is made by the Pit-Hag. There is no way for the ST to lose an ability they gained.

Can the ST lose the ability granted by the Plague Doctor if the Minion comes into play or a player gains the ability (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Engineer / Alchemist)?

No.

If the Plague Doctor gives the Baron ability, does the ST tell the players who changed roles?

Yes.

What happens if all Minions on a script are in play when the Plague Doctor dies?

Minion abilities can be duplicated:

  • The ST gains an in play Minion ability.
  • The Alchemist, if in the game, can change abilities and duplicate an in play Minion ability.

What makes the Pixie gaining an ability different from the ST gaining a Minion ability from the Plague Doctor? If the PD gave the ST an ability and is then swapped away, the ST keeps the ability, right?

Pixie and PD are run differently.

The PD dies and their reminder token is put on the side of the Grimoire indicating that the ST has gained an ability forever. At that point the ability the ST gains is independent from the PD ability.

In contrast, the ability gained through the Pixie is a function of the Pixie ability and so intrinsically tied to it, same as the Philosopher who gains an ability loses it if they are switched to another character.

If the ST gains the Poisoner ability via the Plague Doctor dying to the Demon at night, do they get to use it the same night?

No, as the Poisoner's spot in the night order will have already passed, since the Demon acts after the Poisoner. If the ST wants to run things differently that is fine, but they should inform their players if that is the case. If the PD had died during the day however then they would have gotten to use it.

Can a newly created Po (Engineer/ Pit-Hag / Hatter / Barber / ...) get a triple kill if as their last character they picked no one?

No, their only choice is to kill no one or one player on their first night. Choices or lack thereof as their previous character have no effect on their current character.

For a triple kill, the Demon as the Po must actively choose no one to satisfy their ability.

If the Po charges, are they allowed to attack fewer than three people?

No, the Po that chose to attack no one last time must now choose exactly three different players.

Does the sober and healthy Po get three kills if they charged the previous night while drunk or poisoned?

Yes.

The Po looks back at what it did the prior night; it does not matter whether they were drunk/poisoned or sober/healthy that night or not, their choice was still their choice. If their choice was no one last night, tonight they must choose three players.

The Po chooses to charge. The next night the Exorcist picks the Po. The night after that, how many players does the Po select?

Three. The Exorcist effectively pauses the Po for one night and they triple kill the following night; the Po does not lose their charge.

The Exorcist prevents Demons from making a pick the night that they are exorcised but does not change what the Po's last choice was. And when the Po's last active choice is no one, then the next night that they are able to wake they must choose three players.

This differs from Courtier and Minstrel drunking where the Po can still choose to kill one person or none and it will be applied despite their drunkenness, and their kill (should they choose to kill) just will not work because they are drunk.

Can the Po pick someone three times? Or do they have to pick a dead person to disguise their kills as less kills?

They must choose three unique people. If they want to sink kills, they have to choose the dead.

If the Po charges, is then Courtier drunked, do they retain the charge or is it expended?

They must pick three players the following day but none of them will die, nor will anyone they choose in the next two nights (as long as the Courtier lives and is not drunked or poisoned). Compare with if they charge while drunk and then become sober, then they must pick three players who do die. In summary:

  • At night: Charged
  • In between: Gets drunk
  • Following night: Chooses three in the night (none die)
  • Night after that: Gets to choose one kill or charge again

If the Po figures out that they are drunk, can they refuse to use their ability ? e.g. A Courtier drunked Po is woken and told to choose three players, but instead they shake their head.

No, that is not allowed.

The Po charges then is switched to another player (Scarlet Woman / Hatter / Barber / Snake Charmer / ...). Do three kills still happen?

No. It is a new instance of the character, so a reset of the ability.

If there is more than one healthy and sober Politican ability in play (Philosopher / Cannibal) can they all change alignment and win?

No, only one can change alignment and win. They are now in competition as only one player can be most responsible for their team losing.

Does the Politician work well in a Legion game?

It is not that fun - the Politician is incentivised to vote on literally any execution but their own and be the single good vote Legion needs to pass every vote ‚Äì it is difficult to claim they were not the most responsible for the good team's loss.

How does the Politician in a Revolutionary pair work?

If the Politician is in a Revolutionary pair, it is the Politician who must be most responsible for the game end in order to potentially flip both players‚Äô alignments, not the pair as a duo.

Can the Politician be Mezepheles turned, betray the evil team, and win with the good team?

Yes. The Politician is not restricted to only switching from good to evil at the end of the game, they can switch the other way too.

If the Pit-Hag turns himself into the Politician, could he campaign for his Demon's execution causing his team to lose, then flip alignment to win with the good team?

No. As per the jinx: the Pit-Hag cannot create an evil Politician. This prevents this exact scenario.

The Pit-Hag role does not work great with alignment changers such as the Goon and the Cult Leader.

Can the Politician campaign for their own Fearmonger-execution and win with evil?

Yes.

The Politician flipping alignment does not change the result of the game; if they are Fearmonger-executed, the evil team's win is guaranteed. With the result decided, the ST must now consider if the Politician was most responsible for the good team losing.

Arguably if the Politician successfully campaigns for their execution, perhaps after finding out that they were targeted, triggers the Fearmonger ability and causes the good team to lose, then the Politician should flip alignment and win with evil.

Can the Politician campaign for themselves to be the second good player execution in a Leviathan game and win with evil?

Yes.

The Politician flipping alignment does not change the result of the game; if they are the second execution of a good player then the evil team's win is guaranteed. With the result decided, if the ST then decides that the Politician was the main influence in causing their to team to lose, then the Politician can flip alignment and win with the evil team.

Can the Politician campaign for their execution on a Mastermind day and win with evil?

Yes.

The Politician flipping alignment does not change the result of the game; if they are the executed then the evil team's win is guaranteed. With the result decided, if the ST then decides that the Politician was the main influence in causing their to team to lose, then the Politician can flip alignment and win with the evil team.

How can the Politician win in an Atheist game?

If the Politician successfully makes the entire good team believe that the Atheist is evil, and manages to get them to execute down to final 2, then they can be the only player that wins in an Atheist game.

How does it work if there is more than one Politician ability (Cannibal / Philosopher / Pixie / ...) in play?

With multiple Politician abilities in play, there can be multiple players playing for the evil team. However, only the most responsible player can change teams, so they are in direct competition with one another. If any of these die while they have the Politician ability, they maintain the ability even if dead and can change alignments to win at the end of the game.

When does the Politician flip alignment in a Heretic game?

The Politician‚Äôs changing of alignment is decided after the Heretic impacts the result of who actually won the game.

Can the Politician be the good twin to the Evil Twin?

Yes, but don't; they will likely campaign for their own execution, never mentioning the twins, then win the game with evil as a result - it is pretty hard to argue they were not most responsible in that situation!

What is the Poppy Grower jinx with the Marionette?

When the Poppy Grower dies, the Demon learns the Marionette but the Marionette learns nothing.

Does the Poppy Grower prevent the Demon from learning who the King and the Lunatic are?

No.

Does the Demon learn the Marionette in a Poppy Grower game on N1?

No, assuming a sober and healthy PG ability.

What happens if in a Poppy Grower game the Pit-Hag turns their Demon into a non-Demon?

If there is no Demon in the game and nothing else to keep it going, such as the Evil Twin, then the game just ends with good winning.

Do evil Townsfolk or Outsiders (Bounty Hunter / Mezepheles / Cult Leader / Goon / ...) or evil Travellers learn the evil team when the Poppy Grower dies?

No, only Minions and Demons learn each other.

If the Poppy Grower is swapped out of the game (Pit-Hag / Farmer / ...), do evil learn each other?

No, the Poppy Grower must die for evil to learn each other.

What could cause the Poppy Grower in the game from the start to fail to prevent the evil team from learning each other?

As the Poppy Grower acts early in the night, she would need to be poisoned or drunked on N1 from setup, via being:

  • sat next to the No Dashii
  • Puzzle Master drunk
  • the Drunk

Other sources of drunking and poisoning act after the Poppy Grower so will not impact her ability.

What happens when the Lleech poisons the Poppy Grower?

The PG is the poisoned host and unless evil can shift this (Pit-Hag makes a new demon / Barber swap / Hatter swap / ...) then evil will not be able to kill the PG without losing and so will never learn each other.

If the Snake Charmer succeeds in becoming the new Demon and the Poppy Grower later dies, will the evil team learn the old Demon or the new Demon?

New Demon; the old Demon is no longer a Demon so would not be in any info.

If there is a dead Demon and a living Demon (Scarlet Woman / Fang Gu jump / Imp self-kill /...) what is shown if the Poppy Grower dies?

All Minions learn every Demon, and all Demons learn of every Minion, regardless of living status.

If the Poppy Grower is ever poisoned or drunked, do the evil team learn each other?

Only if they start the game poisoned by being sat next to the No Dashii or start drunk due to the Puzzle Master. After N1, droisoning benefits the good team because it deactivates the second part of the Poppy Grower's ability, meaning that if the Poppy Grower dies while droisoned, the evil team never learns each other.

If the Poppy Grower dies while drunk or poisoned, evil do not learn each other, correct?

Correct.

Does the Pixie or the Cannibal gaining the Poppy Grower ability prevent evil learning each other when the PG dies?

Yes. They get their ability immediately upon the PG's death, meaning there is no "gap" between the two abilities wherein evil would be able to learn each other.

If the Pixie sees the Poppy Grower and has been sufficiently mad then when the PG dies do evil still learn each other or would the Pixie Poppy Grower hold it off for longer?

The Pixie-PG would hold it off. Double PG abilities through Philo, Cannibal, or Pixie require them both to die sober/healthy in order for evil to learn each other.

If the Philosopher Poppy Grower dies while the Poppy Grower is alive, sober and healthy do the evil team learn each other as the ability says "if you die, they learn who you are"?

No, because there is an active PG ability still in play.

If the Demon kills the Poppy Grower at night, when does the evil team learn each other?

As soon as possible.

If the Poppy Grower dies to the Demon at night (past the Poppy Grower's night order), does the evil team have to wait until the next night to learn their teammates?

The evil team learn each other at the first opportunity after the PG dies. If she is executed, that is the start of the night; if she dies at night, it is immediately after that death.

What happens when the Cannibal-Poppy Grower is the last living instance of the Poppy Grower ability but they lose their ability not when they die but when someone else is executed?

Evil will never learn each other.

According to the jinx, the Spy / the Widow do not see the Grimoire until the Poppy Grower dies. What if there is a Cannibal Poppy Grower in the game?

They see the Grimoire when the last Poppy Grower ability (Cannibal / Pixie / Philosopher / ...) dies.

Can the Preacher preach the ST if the Plague Doctor is on the script?

No. Also the ST is not a Minion so would not lose the ability anyway.

If a preached Minion becomes another Minion (Engineer / Hatter / Pit-Hag / ...) do they lose their preached status?

No, a preached Minion remains preached so long as they are a Minion. They do not get to use their new Minion ability while the Preacher is alive, sober and healthy.

If they are switched to a non-Minion they would no longer be preached, then could become an unpreached Minion with an ability again. That is, until the Preacher picks them again.

Can the ST gain the ability of a preached Minion when the Plague Doctor dies?

No, the ability may not be functioning at the moment but it is still in play.

Does a preached Minion who dies and is then resurrected by the Al-Hadikhia regain their ability?

No, they did not stop being a Minion when they died, and they are still preached provided the Preacher is still alive. (the Preacher's reminder token would still be next to them in the Grimoire)

In contrast, resurrecting the Preacher does not cause Minions to lose their ability again; as a fresh instance of the Preacher they must start their preaching over (when the Preacher originally died the ST would have removed their reminder tokens from the Grimoire).

Does the Preacher dying giving the Minions a new instance of their ability or not? eg, an Assassin is preached after killing, the Preacher dies, can the Assassin kill again, or is re-activation simply just, as it was before.

No, this is not a new instance of the ability; their ability is simply reactivating.

The Preacher and Vigormortis interactions:
  1. The Preacher chooses a Vigor killed Minion: the dead Minion loses their ability, the neighbouring Townsfolk is still poisoned.
  2. The Preacher chooses a Minion who is then Vigor killed: the Minion is dead, poisons their neighbour, no ability.
  3. either of the above then the Preacher dies: the Minion regains their ability.

All correct.

If the Preacher selects a Minion (say Devil's Advocate) and the Demon kills the Preacher the same night, should the DA's ability work that night?

No. The DA is woken before the Demon kills so the DA must wait to the following night to use their ability.

If a Preacher targeted Minion later becomes a different Minion (Barber / Hatter / Pit-Hag / ...), are they still preached and without an ability?

Yes. As long as they are an uninterrupted Minion, even if they change Minion type, they would still be preached. This is similar to Vigormortis in that sense.

If the Plague Doctor gives a Minion a second ability, what happens when the Preacher preaches them?

The Minion cannot use either ability while the Plague Doctor is alive, sober or healthy.

The Preacher states that chosen Minions have no ability, so they lose both their native ability and the ability they gained from the Plague Doctor. The Preacher's ability is also stated in the present tense, so it is an ongoing effect, meaning that if a Minion is preached and then given an ability by the Plague Doctor, they are still preached and still have no ability.

If a preached Minion gain another Minion ability from the Plague Doctor, is that ability also suppressed?

Yes. They would still gain the second ability, but both abilities are suppressed while the Preacher is alive, healthy or sober.

If a preached Minion becomes a different character type, say a Demon, and then becomes a Minion again, will they still be preached?

No. The moment they stop being a Minion, the preached effect ends on them and does not ever return unless the Preacher chooses them again when they turn back.

Can the Professor resurrect a Townsfolk turned evil (Mezepheles / Bounty Hunter / ...)?

Yes.

If there are three people alive going into night, Demon kills one of them (two people alive), and then the Professor resurrects one (three people alive), does Evil win?

Evil won the moment there were only two people alive, which was immediately after the Demon chose a kill. The Professor does not get to act that night because the game was over already.

If there are no dead players, do you wake the Professor and tell them that?

You would wake the Professor, prompt them to use their ability, and they would presumably shake their head and go back to sleep, or they might try to choose the player that they think died tonight (to no avail, because no one is dead) and you would put them back to sleep after a couple times trying, to prevent them from fishing. Telling them that no one is dead at their point in the night order is giving them too much information. Waking them is also important to roles such as the Chambermaid.

If the Professor picks an alive player, is their ability spent?

No, the ST shakes their head to say that they should pick again, however if they‚Äôre just trying to see if others are dead or living, you should just put them to sleep.

If the Professor attempts to use their ability on a dead player when drunk/poisoned, is their once per game ability used up?

Yes.

If someone is resurrected before the Professor wakes, and if the Professor tries to resurrect them (thinking they are still dead), is the Professor's ability lost?

No as it would still be an invalid target. The ST should shake their head and prompt the player to pick again.

If a player is bluffing as the Psychopath and is executed, can they pretend to play roshambo with their nominator?

No, they are not the Psychopath so do not have the ability that allows them to play roshambo.

If the Psychopath is protected by the Devil's Advocate do they still play roshambo / Does the Alchemist Psychopath protected by the Tea Lady or Pacifist still play roshambo?

Yes, and then it is only if they lose and do not die that the good team discovers they were protected.

When can the Psychopath choose to kill someone?

Each day before nominations begin. They could kill as soon as the day starts if they wished. The Psychopath should not be allowed to interrupt an action such as the ST privately giving a player any information.

If the Psychopath self nominates, who do they play roshambo with?

The ST.

If the poisoned Psychopath is executed, do they play roshambo and die whatever the result? Or do they die without playing?

They just die without playing; mechanical effects do not happen while poisoned.

If the Alchemist Cerenovus chooses the Psychopath, and the Psychopath player breaks madness by choosing to kill the Alchemist, what happens?

The ST can choose to execute the Psychopath before the kill goes through or not. The Psychopath does not cause an instantaneous kill, as she must first publicly claim the ability and then choose a player, and could be executed mid sentence. If the ST does execute for the madness break then the Psychopath and ST will play roshambo to see if the Psychopath dies.

If the Psychopath is executed for breaking Cerenovus madness who do they play roshambo against?

The ST. From the how-to-run: "If the Psychopath nominates themselves or would be executed for another non-nomination reason (Cerenovus madness break, for example) the ST plays roshambo with the Psychopath." ‚Å†-------------

How do the Psychopath and the Vigormortis interact?

The Psychopath keeps their ability if killed by the Vigormortis. So they can still name a player before nominations to die, and if their corpse is executed, they play roshambo with the person who nominated them. There is no reason to nominate their body though since they are already dead and cannot die again, but it would be amusing.

The Vizier forces the execution of the Psychopath. Do they play romshambo?

The Psychopath and their nominator will play roshambo.

If the Psychopath who never claimed to be the Psychopath is executed, do they still play roshambo?

Yes, with whomever nominated them.

If the Psychopath never claims that they are the Psychopath and are nominated, are they announced?

No, the ST does not directly state that they are the Psychopath. If they are executed then they play roshambo with their whomever nominated them, so it will be pretty obvious what they are.

The drunk Psychopath cannot kill anyone, correct?

Correct. Drunk or poisoned characters do not actually have abilities.

If the Pukka passes to another player (Hatter / Scarlet Woman / Barber / ...), is the previously poisoned player still poisoned and scheduled to die?

No. As a new instance of the Pukka, the ability resets, so their victim immediately becomes healthy.

If the Pukka dies and the game continues (Evil Twin / Mastermind / ...) does the previously poisoned player still die?

No, killing the Pukka completely removes their ability from play: the victim immediately becomes healthy and does not die.

In contrast, drunking the Pukka keeps the poison in play, killing the player when the Pukka sobers.

What happens when the Pukka chooses while drunk or poisoned?

If the Pukka is drunk or poisoned when they pick at night then:

  1. the player who already has the poisoned token is temporarily healthy (some STs choose not to remove the token entirely to help them remember; some turn it upside down)
  2. no new token is placed down.

On the next night when the Pukka is both sober and healthy:

  1. the Pukka's choice will now cause a new poisoned token to be placed down.
  2. the previously poisoned player is re-poisoned, they die, then become healthy

If the Pukka is drunked (Courtier / Goon / ...) when does the previously poisoned player die?

When the Pukka becomes sober. Until then the previously poisoned player is temporarily healthy, which the ST can indicate by turning the poison reminder token upside-down.

If the Pukka becomes another Demon (Pit-Hag / Hatter / Engineer / ...), what happens to the previously poisoned player?

They are immediately no longer poisoned and will not die tonight.

What happens when the Pukka kills a character with an ability that acts on death (Sweetheart / Barber / Plague Doctor / Hatter / Farmer / Ravenkeeper / Sage / ...)?

Their ability does not trigger.

The Pukka's kills always die poisoned. This is what allows the Pukka to kill characters such as the Sailor or the Fool who might otherwise survive thanks to their own ability.

But dying poisoned also means that effects which trigger upon death malfunction meaning for example that:

  • the Pukka is not offered the Barber swap when the Barber dies
  • a good player is not drunked when the Sweetheart dies
  • the ST does not get an out of play Minion ability when the Plague Doctor dies
  • the evil players do not get to switch their roles when the Hatter dies
  • the evil team do not learn each other when the Poppy Grower dies

But while those were all bad for team evil, consider:

  • the Farmer does not create another Farmer
  • the Sage can be told two non Demon players
  • the Ravenkeeper may be given false info

If the Pukka is chosen by the Exorcist does the previously poisoned player still die?

Yes. The effect of the exorcism is to delay the Pukka's next kill.

The Exorcist only stops the Demon to wake to use their ability, but any other part of their ability still works.

In this case, the Exorcist causes the Pukka to not wake to choose a player, but she does not need to wake for the previously poisoned person to die then become healthy; that is a separate part of the ability.

The next night, the Pukka wakes as normal to poison a player and no one dies as the previously poisoned player is already dead.

Can the Pukka poisoned Fool die even if she has yet to use her ability?

If the Fool is poisoned, then she does not have her ability, so she will die the first time she is killed. The same goes for the Sailor.

If the Lycanthrope picks a good player but is then Pukka poisoned that night, can there be a Pukka kill tonight?

Yes, the Lycanthrope pick and the previous night's Pukka pick since the Lycanthrope protection is now poisoned.

In order to not die to the Pukka, does a player need to be Monk protected the night they are picked by the Pukka or the following night when they would die?

Either:

  • If they are protected the first night then the Pukka poison is never applied, so there is no "previously poisoned player" the following night, so no Demon kill.
  • If instead they are protected the following night then they do not die and become healthy.

The Pukka's target does not need to be protected on both nights: if they were protected on the first night, then the Monk is free to protect someone else the following night. From the Monk's perspective they have two good targets available to them, the player targeted the night before or the one targeted tonight - the Monk is super strong in a Pukka game.

If the Monk-protected player is picked by the Pukka, are they poisoned that night?

No (the ST does not place the Pukka poison token next to them), and they do not die the following night.

If the Monk-protected player is picked by the Pukka, do they still die the next night?

No, nor are they Pukka poisoned the night they are picked.

If the Monk protects a player who was Pukka poisoned on the previous night, even though that player was the "previously poisoned player", they will not die tonight, right?

Correct. The player does not die and becomes healthy.

N1 player X is Pukka poisoned. N2 the Monk protects player X but is then later targetted by the Pukka. What happens to player X?

They die.

Player X is no longer poisoned while Monk protected, but when the Monk becomes poisoned, the protection is removed. As player X is still the previously poisoned player, they die.

If the Monk-protected player is picked by the Pukka, they are not poisoned and do not die the next night, but does the Pukka's previous pick still die tonight?

Yes.

What happens when the Pukka picks herself?

Nothing good for the Pukka:

  • As soon as she picks herself she is permanently poisoned for the rest of the game, so she cannot kill anyone, including herself.
  • The previously poisoned player, if there is one, is immediately healthy, and does not die.
  • If she somehow became healthy on a later night then, as the previously poisoned player, she would die.

The Pukka's pick is poisoned and the following night dies and then becomes healthy. If that player does not die because of protection (Monk / Tea Lady / Innkeeper) do they still become healthy?

Yes. The player's dying and becoming healthy are two separate events, one does not rely on the other; if anything prevents them from dying, they still become healthy.

If the Puzzlemaster becomes a different character, is their drunkeness removed from game?

Yes.

If the Puzzlemaster's target changes character, is that player still drunk?

Yes. For as long as the Puzzlemaster is in the game and healthy and sober, the picked player is drunk, even if that player changes character.

Could the Puzzlemaster drunk a role in a hate jinx pair, allowing the other role to enter play?

No. Hate jinxes are a part of setup whereas the Puzzlemaster has no setup ability; the puzzledrunk player is decided after tokens have been distributed. So pairs of hate jinxed characters still cannot be placed in the token bag in a Puzzlemaster game.

On the other hand, if one of the hate jinxed pair is the Drunk then both roles can be put in the token bag, as then only one of the roles is techically in play.

When does the Puzzlemaster guess?

During the day.

If a character is drunk because of the Puzzlemaster, are their setup abilities in effect?

Yes.

The reminder token is placed on N1, after tokens are sent out and [setup abilities] have already resolved, so that is when the drunking starts.

If a dead player is Pit-Hagged into the Puzzlemaster, is a player made Puzzlemaster-drunk?

No. Their ability reads "1 player is drunk, even if you die", rather than "even if you are dead", so the Puzzlemaster does not start making someone drunk if they enter play while already dead. The Puzzlemaster must be alive to drunk a player and when they die continue to drunk that player, which prevents Puzzlemasters from just getting themselves killed early to stop making their teammates drunk.

Does the Puzzlemaster that guessed wrong in a Vortox game gets the correct Demon?

No. Puzzlemaster is an Outsider and is therefore not affected by Vortox.

If the Puzzlemaster guesses their drunk player in a Legion game, what happens?

They are given any one Legion, ST's choice. It should also be a living Legion, as the ability says "the Demon" and when there are multiple Demons in the game, that means living Demons who are "the" Demon (while both living and dead Demons are "a Demon").

If the Puzzlemaster guesses their drunk player on a Mastermind day with no Demon alive, what happens?

If all the Demons are dead then the ST chooses one of the dead Demons.

If the Puzzlemaster guesses their drunk player and there is no Demon in the game, after the Demon was pit-hagged out of the game with an Evil Twin in play, what happens?

The ST will tell them no one.

If the Puzzlemaster is droisoned, is the puzzle-drunk player still puzzle-drunk?

If the Puzzlemaster is drunked / poisoned, their ability does not work, so the person they have made drunk is temporarily sober (the ST can indicate this by turning the Puzzlemaster drunk reminder token upside down)

If the Puzzlemaster is created mid game, does the ST immediately make someone puzzle-drunk?

Yes.

Could the Recluse misregister as a Minion or a Demon if picked by the Courtier to avoid being drunked?

Yes, but don't.

Can the Recluse register as evil at the end of the game and win with evil?

No.

Can the Recluse registering as the Demon learn the King?

Yes, but don't.

Can the Recluse, registering as a Minion, successfully guess the Damsel?

Yes, ending the game.

They could also learn the Damsel is in play if they register as a Minion at any time, but it is generally not the point of Outsiders that they can be hard-confirmed to other players, so do not do this.

When the Snake Charmer swaps with the Recluse, there are no alignment changes, so after telling the Recluse that they are now the Snake Charmer, are they told that they are good?

No, players are only informed of their alignment after it changes. If they ask the next day then the ST can explain that they are only informed of aligment when it changes, so they can probably work out that they are still good from this.

They will not know for sure if they changed character because of the Pit-Hag / Snake Charmer / Barber / ...

Is it legal to show the Recluse to the Demon as a Minion?

Yes, but don‚Äôt, as that would be an Outsider ability hurting evil.

Can the Recluse register as a good Minion/Demon?

Yes.

If the Recluse dies, could they misregister as a Demon and trigger the Scarlet Woman? What would the SW become?

They could, but probably should not.

The SW's ability explicitly says "you become the Demon." They would become whatever Demon the ST registers the Recluse as, but never a Recluse.

Can the Recluse be told that there is a Damsel?

Yes but don't.

If the Recluse is picked by the Snake Charmer, could the SC become the Demon?

Yes. "Each night, choose an alive player: a chosen Demon swaps characters and alignments with you and is then poisoned." So if the Recluse registers as the Demon the swap happens, with the Snake Charmer becoming the Recluse or whatever Demon is on the script that the ST thinks the Recluse is registering as, and the Recluse becoming a self-poisoned Snake Charmer.

Could the Imp with no living Minions starpass to the Recluse?

Technically, yes; however, this makes the Recluse into the good Imp, meaning that they need only to get themselves killed in order to win. So it is not recommended for the Imp to do this.

Can the Recluse register as the Spy and trigger the Virgin?

No.

The Recluse only registers as the Spy, but does not gain the Spy ability, therefore cannot register as a Townsfolk.

Think of registering as: if an ability "asks" a player about their character or alignment or living status, they can "answer" with something other than what they are. Misregistering can never change the game directly (like executing someone). It can however trick someone else's ability into doing it for them, like the Spy who nominates the Virgin - the Spy's ability cannot kill themselves, but it can trick the Virgin's ability into thinking they are a Townsfolk, after which the Virgin's real ability can execute them.

If the Recluse is in play, the Scarlet Woman is on the script and the Zombuul is executed, can the Recluse register as the Scarlet Woman and become a good Zombuul?

No, they do not actually have the Scarlet Woman's ability. If the Recluse dies the Scarlet Woman can become the Demon however.

If the Snake Charmer is turned into the Recluse (Pit-Hag / Barber / ...), is the ST allowed to show the former SC "you are now the evil Pukka" using the Recluse's register as a Demon ability?

No.

The ST is not allowed to lie to the player about their character or alignment unless the ability allows for that specifically (like Lunatic, for example). The Recluse does not believe they are anything else; they always know that they are the Recluse.

The ST could never falsely tell the Recluse they are evil, a Minion, or a Demon. The Recluse's ability of possibly registering as evil does not allow them to believe that they are the Demon. This is opposed to the wording on the Drunk or Lunatic which specifically say they believe they are something else.

Can a Traveller and a non-Traveller sat together be a Revolutionary pair, assuming both are present at the start of the game?

Yes.

What happens if an alignment changing ablity (Snake Charmer / Mezepheles / ...) targets a player in a Revolutionary pair?

This is a matter of ST judgement: it either has no effect and both players stay their prior alignment, or both players change to the new alignment.

Can the Bounty Hunter turn a Townsfolk player who is in a Revolutionary pair?

Revolutionary pairs are decided at setup, the same time as the Bounty Hunter evil Townsfolk. As such, if the two players in the pair are good, then neither of them can become the Bounty Hunter evil Townsfolk. However, the ST could pair the evil Townsfolk with a Minion or the Demon.

Can the Bounty Hunter incorrectly learn a good player in a Revolutionary pair who registers falsely?

Yes.

Could the Revolutionary cause the Damsel to register falsely as another character when guessed by a Minion?

Yes but don't.

Could the Revolutionary cause a good player to register falsely as a Minion when they accuse someone of being the Damsel?

Yes but don't.

How does a Revolutionary pair work if the first half draws the Lunatic?

The other person is given any good character. The Lunatic player will probably figure it out immediately.

What is the Hatter jinx with Riot?

If the Hatter dies in a Riot game, and a Riot chooses a different Demon, a normal evil team is created from the Riot players.

If the Hatter dies and the Demon chooses Riot, the Minions become Riot too.

Can there be a call to exile a Traveller while there is a Riot active?

No, the call should be made before nominations open.

In a Riot game calling for the exile of a Traveller does not kill them immediately; Riot only affects nominations, so a Traveller exile vote should be run as normal. There should be no interruptions once a Riot nomination train is rolling, so all calls for Traveller exiles should occur before nominations open.

If a Townsfolk nominates the Virgin in a Riot game, which ability takes priority?

If the Virgin is nominated by a Townsfolk in a Riot game, the Virgin dies and the Townsfolk is immediately executed, ending the day.

If it is day three, the game ends and the evil team wins. After all, it is the Virgin's job to ask Townsfolk to not nominate her, or do it before day three.

Can each Riot be told different bluffs, or do all of them have to receive the same three?

ST choice. When there are multiple Demons (like Legion), if the ST wants, each Demon can receive different bluffs.

The Golem nominates a Riot player who does not die. Does the Riot player get to nominate?

Based on how Soldier is explained, players who do not die do not have to nominate but can.

The Golem is alive in a Riot game and has already used their nomination. What happens on D3 if they are nominated?

The Riot ability forces them to nominate again. There is no issue with them being the Golem as they would be already dead at that point and have no ability.

It is while the Golem is alive that their ability would prevent them from killing a Riot player.

In a Riot game, is there an extra Minion in play, for example four total evil in a 12 player game? Lil' Monsta specifically says there is +1 minion, but Riot does not specify this.

There is no +1 Minion, because the Demon is already Riot, so there is the usual number of evil players who are all are Riot.

The Lil' Monsta adds +1 Minion because the Monsta token does not actually go into the bag; the extra Minion is dealt so that there are the correct number of evil players. In the case of Riot, the correct number of evil tokens go into the bag because the ST adds that many Riot tokens, so there is no need to add an extra Minion.

Just to clarify:

  • there are not supposed to be Minions in Riot games; the problem for good is that every starting evil player is a Demon, so they need to get rid of every evil player to win.
  • no player is the Lil' Monsta; the Minions choose a babysitter for the Lil' Monsta each night, making that player count as the Demon for all game mechanics that care.

Would the Sage wake up if they are killed by a nomination from the Demon?

No, unless it is a Riot game because of the jinx.

Does a Mayor bounce to the Sage register as a Demon kill?

Yes.

The Demon is still the source of the attack and the ST would place the Demon's dead token.

Does a new instance of the Sailor created mid game (Damsel / Pit-Hag / Barber / Philosopher / Cannibal / ...) get to drink with someone the night that they are created?

Philosopher Sailor and Cannibal Sailor sure, otherwise no, because it would already be past the Sailor's turn in the night order. Not drinking means that they cannot die that night or the following day.

Can the Gossip kill the Sailor?

Only if the Sailor is drunk or poisoned, otherwise the Sailor cannot die by any means except to the Assassin.

If the Philosoper Saint nominates the unspent Virgin, do good lose?

Yes.

Can the Recluse register good in the first part of Savant info, and then register evil in the second part, or do they have to register the same in both parts of the Savant info?

If you are running with misregistration in Savant info (which there is some contention about) then yes, the Recluse (and even the Spy) can register differently to two parts of a single ability.

Can the poisoned Savant receive two true statements?

Yes, assuming no Vortox is in play.

Not that you should, but can the Scapegoat save the good Evil Twin or the Saint from being executed?

Yes.

If the Demon is executed in final five, does the Scarlet Woman become the new Demon?

Yes, as it needs to be five alive at the time of the Demon's execution for the Scarlet Woman ability to trigger.

Can the Demon who was the Scarlet Woman guess the Damsel?

No, they are no longer a Minion.

What is the Al-Hadikhia jinx with the Scarlet Woman?

If there are two living Al-Hadikhias, the Scarlet Woman Al-Hadikhia becomes the Scarlet Woman again.

This means that if the Scarlet Woman turned Al-Hadikhia resurrects the Al-Hadikhia, they revert to being the Scarlet Woman rather than staying the Demon themselves as well.

There are five players left alive including the Imp and the Scarlet Woman. The Imp is executed, leaving four alive. Does the SW activate?

Yes.

If the Slayer slays the Imp, but the Scarlet Woman is in play, what happens?

Assuming none of these players are poisoned or drunk, in Trouble Brewing, if there are five or more players when the Slayer slays the Imp, the Imp dies and the Scarlet Woman will immediately become the Imp, The former SW should be informed at the next available opportunity the following night that they are now the Imp, before getting their kill.

In a Poppy Grower game, the Psychopath kills the Demon and then, later that same day, the Slayer chooses the Scarlet Woman. Does the SW die?

Yes. The SW became the Demon even before they were informed. The SW's ability takes over the Demonhood immediately upon the Demon's death. If they did not, then the game would technically be over in the space between the Demon's death and the night phase.

If the Scarlet Woman becomes the Demon during the middle of the day (due to the Slayer, the Witch, ...), when are they informed? Should they ask? Do they have to wait until the SW's turn at night?

Wait until the start of the next night phase. The SW's position in the night order is really just a reminder in case the ST forgots to inform them of the demonhood after the Demon died during the day. So if you get to that point and realize you have not yet, no big deal.

Trigger based abilities are meant to happen the moment they trigger, with any relevant things that may need to be done, or info given, at the first reasonable opportunity, often the start of the night. The night order for trigger abilities should be considered flexible.

If the Scarlet Woman catches the demonhood, but is then instantly Snake Charmed, would they learn who the King, Marionette and Lunatic are?

Yes, the SW is woken to learn of those characters before the Snake Charmer acts.

If the Shabaloth sinks a kill into a dead player, can that player be regurgitated the next night even though they were not killed by the Shab?

Yes, since the Shab's ability is "a player you chose last night might be regurgitated"; it does not specify needing to be the killer.

The Shabaloth dies and the game continues (Scarlet Woman / Mastermind / Evil Twin / ...). The dead Shabaloth‚Äôs kills can no longer be regurgitated, correct?

Correct, as the Shabaloth who picked them no longer has an ability, so cannot regurgitate anyone.

If the Shabaloth picks two player while drunk / poisoned they do not die that night, but if one of the is executed the next day, could they be regurgitated the following night?

Yes.

What if four players go to night with the Shabaloth alive? Does the Shabaloth killing two players happens at the same time as the revival of a previously killed player? Or when four players go into the night with the Shabaloth in play is it effectively the end of the game?

Regurgitation, if the ST chooses to do it, happens before the Shabaloth's killls, so there would be five alive then two would die, and the game can continue.

Can the Shabaloth choose to regurgitate people?

The Shabaloth does not control whether someone is regurgitated; that choice falls to the Storyteller.

Can the Shabaloth pick the same player twice?

Not on the same night, since that would still only amount to one player being chosen. The clause "choose two players‚Äù is not equal to "choose a player, then make that same choice again‚Äù. It specifically requires two unique players to be chosen in order to satisfy.

Could the Scarlet Woman who becomes the new Shabaloth resurrect the old Shab?

The ST should never use the Shab's ability to resurrect another demon.

Does the Shabaloth regurgitate before or after they kill?

Before.

Does the Shabaloth get shown who is regurgitated that night before she picks her next two kills?

No, the Shabaloth is not told anything about regurgitations. The ST makes the decision on regurgitation before the Shabaloth wakes, (i.e. before the kills) then wakes the Shab and have her point to two players. Any deaths and resurrections are announced at the start of the day, and the players update the Town Square accordingly.

How exactly does the Shabaloth work? When does regurgitation happen?

If the Shabaloth chose two people the night before, then just before they attack tonight, one of those people they chose, if they are currently dead, may come back to life. Note that if the Shabaloth is chosen by an Exorcist and does not wake to attack anyone tonight, they can still bring one of their previous night's targets back to life because regurgitation is not tied to their waking up.

Note that the Shabaloth's previous targets do not need to have been killed by the Shabaloth's attack in order to be revived, they only need to be dead on the next night. This means that the Shabaloth can choose someone who is already dead and revive them the next night, or the Shabaloth's target can survive the attack, then die the next day and subsequently be revived because they are now dead in time.

When is the last moment a character can activate their ability? Should the Slayer be allowed to use their ability after the day's execution has been carried out?

Any time before they die, and before the day officially ends. So after they are on the block but before they are actually executed is fine.
